
=== Kumara1output-1-to-1.json ==========================
1
śrī sōmaprabhācāryaviracitaḥ
kumārapālapratibōdhaḥ ।
ōṁ namō vītarāgāya ।
prathamaḥ prastāvaḥ ।
causu disāsu pasariyaṁ mōha-balaṁ nijiuṁ payaṭṭō vva ।
payaḍiya - dhamma- caukkō cau-dēhō jaya jiṇa-nāhō ॥ 1 ॥
taṁ namaha risahanāhaṁ nāṇa-nihāṇassa jassa aṁsēsu ।
ali-kasiṇō kēsa bharō rēhai rukkhē bhuyaṁgō vva ॥ 2 ॥
taṁ saraha saṁtināhaṁ pavanna caraṇaṁ pi jaṁ caraṇa- laggā ।
tiyasa-kaya-kaṇaya-paṁkaya-misēṇa sēvaṁti nava nihiṇō ॥ 3 ॥
kajjala - samāṇa - vannaṁ sivaṁga-bhūyaṁ nisiddha-maya-māraṁ ।
parihariya- rāyamaiyaṁ duhā nama̭sāmi nēmijiṇaṁ ॥ 4 ॥
majjha pasīya pāsō pāsē jassōragiṁda-phaṇa-maṇiṇō ।
dippaṁti satta-dīva vva satta tattāim̐ pāyaḍiuṁ ॥ 5 ॥
sō jaya mahāvīrō sarīra- duggāô bhāva - riu - vaggō ।
ciramanna-pāṇa- rōhaṁ kāuṁ nivvāsiō jēṇa ॥ 6 ॥
vitthāriya- paramatthaṁ aṇaggha- rayaṇāsayaṁ suvanna- payaṁ ।
dōgacca -dalaṇa- niuṇaṁ namaha nihāṇaṁ va jiṇa vayaṇaṁ ॥ 7 ॥
jēsiṁ tuṭṭhi laṭṭhi va lahiu maṁdō vi akhaliya-paēhiṁ ।
visamē vi kavva- maggē saṁcaraha jayaṁtu tē guruṇō ॥ 8 ॥
kaṇa jayaṁtu tē jalahiṇō vva uvajīviūṇa jāṇa payaṁ ।
annē vi ghaṇā bhuvaṇē kuṇaṁti dhannāṇa ukkarisaṁ ॥ 9 ॥
jalahi-jala-galiya- rayaṇaṁ va dullahaṁ māṇusattaṇaṁ lahiuṁ ।

2
kumārapāla pratibōdhē
jiṇadhammaṁmi payattō kāyavvō buddhimaṁtēṇa ॥ 10 ॥
saggō tāṇa gharaṁgaṇaṁ sahayarā savvā suhā saṁpayā
sōhaggāi - guṇāvalī virayaē savvaṁgamāliṁgaṇaṁ ।
saṁsārō na duruttarō siva-suhaṁ pattaṁ karabhōruhē
[ prathamaḥ
jē sammaṁ jiṇadhamma-kammakaraṇē vati udvārayā ॥ 11 ॥
sappurisa-carittāṇaṁ saraṇēṇa payaṁpaṇēṇa savaṇēṇa ।
aṇumōyaṇēṇa ya phuḍaṁ jiṇadhammō lahai ukkarisaṁ ॥ 12 ॥
puvvaṁ jiṇā gaṇaharā caudasa-dasa-pubviṇō carima-taṇuṇō ।
cārita dharā bahavō jāyā annē vi sappurisā ॥ 13 ॥
taha bharahēsara - sēṇiya- saṁpainiva-pabhiṇō samutpannā ।
pavayaṇa- pabhāvaṇā-guṇa-nihiṇō gihiṇō vi sappurisā ॥ 14 ॥
tēsiṁ nāma-ggahaṇaṁ pi jaṇai jaṁtūṇa punna- pabhāraṁ ।
saggā-pavagga-suha-saṁpayāu saṁpāḍai kamēṇa ॥ 15 ॥
saṁpai purṇa sappurisō ēkkō siri-hēmacaṁda - muṇi-ṇāhō ।
phuriyaṁ dūsama - samaē vi jassa lōuttaraṁ cariyaṁ ॥ 16 ॥
duiō vi daliya - riu - cakka - vikkamō kumaravāla - bhūpālō ।
jēṇa daḍhaṁ paḍivannō jiṇa dhammō dūsamāē vi ॥ 17 ॥
kēvala-nāṇa- palōia - tailōkkāṇaṁ jiṇāṇa vayaṇēhiṁ ।
puvvanivā paḍibuddhā jiṇadhammē jaṁ na taṁ bhujjaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
bhujjamiṇaṁ jaṁ rāyā kumāravālō parūḍha - micchattō ।
chaumatthēṇa vi pahuṇā jiṇadhamma-parāyaṇō vihiō ॥ 19 ॥
tuliya-tavaṇijja-kaṁtī sayavatta-savatta-nayaṇa - ramaṇijā ।
pallaviya lōya- lōyaṇa - harisa- ppasarā sarīra-sirī ॥ 20 ॥
ābālattaṇaō vi hu cārittaṁ jaṇiya jaṇa camakkāraṁ ।
bāvīsa- parīsaha - sahaṇa-duddharaṁ tivva-tava-pavaraṁ ॥ 21 ॥
muṇiya-visamattha-satthā nimmiya - vāyaraṇa- pamuha-gaṁdha-gaṇā ।
paravāi- parājaya- jāya- kittī maī jaya-pasiḍā ॥ 22 ॥
dhamma- paḍivatti-jaṇaṇaṁ atuccha-micchatta-mucchiāṇaṁ pi ।
mahu-khīra - pamuha - mahuratta nimmiyaṁ dhamma - vāgaraṇaṁ ॥ 23 ॥
sars- guṇōhaṁ hēmasariṇō pēcchiūṇa chēya-jaṇō ।

prastāva: ]
aṇahillapāṭakanagaranarēndravaṁśavarṇanam
sadahai adiṭṭhē vihu titthaṁkara - gaṇahara - ppamuhē ॥ 24 ॥
jiṇadhammē paḍivattiṁ kumaranariṁdassa lōiuṁ lōō ।
pattiyai vva ciraṁtaṇa-bhūmivaīṇaṁ pi aviappaṁ ॥ 25 ॥
siva-paha kahagē'vi sayaṁ vīrajiṇē sēṇiēṇa naravaiṇā ।
jīva-dayaṁ kāraviḍaṁ na sakkiō kālasōyariō ॥ 26 ॥
dūsama - samaē'vi hu hēmasūriṇō nisuṇiūṇa vayaṇāī ।
savva jaṇō jīva dayaṁ karāviō kumaravālēṇa ॥ 27 ॥
tattō duvē'vi ēē imaṁmi samaē asaṁbhava - carittā ।
kaya-kayajuyā vayārā jiṇadhamma- pabhāvaṇa- pahāṇā ॥ 28 ॥
dumha vi imāṇa cariyaṁ bhaṇijamāṇaṁ maē nisāmēha |
vittharai jēṇa sukathaṁ thirattaṇaṁ hōi jiṇadhammē ॥ 29 ॥
jai vi cariyaṁ imāṇaṁ maṇōharaṁ asthi bahuyamannaṁ pi ।
taha vi jiṇadhamma-paḍibōha-baṁdhuraṁ kiṁ pi jaṁpēmi ॥ 30 ॥
bahu-bhakkha - juyāi vi rasavaīê majjhāō kiṁci bhuṁjaṁtō ।
niya icchā aṇurūvaṁ purisō kiṁ hōi vayaṇijō ॥ 31 ॥
aṇahillapāṭakapuravarṇanam
atthi mahī- mahilāē muhaṁ mahaṁtaṁ mayaṁka paḍibimbaṁ ।
jaṁbuddīva-chalēṇaṁ nahalacchi dahumunnamiyaṁ ॥ 32 ॥
tuṁgō nāsā- vaṁsō vva sōhaē tiyasa-pavvaō jattha ।
sīyā- sīōyāō dīhā diṭṭhīō va sahati ॥ 33 ॥
tatthārōviya-guṇa-dhaṇu-nibhaṁ nalāḍaṁ va bhārahaṁ atthi ।
jattha virāyai viulō vēyaḍḍō rayaya-paṭṭō vva ॥ 34 ॥
jaṁ gaṁga - siṁdhu- sariyā - muttiya sariyāhi saṁgayaṁ sahai ।
tīra-vaṇa-paṁti kuṁtala - kalāva- rēhaṁta pēraṁtaṁ ॥ 35 ॥
tatthasthitilaya-tullaṁ aṇahilavāḍaya-puraṁ ghaṇa-suvannaṁ ।
pēraṁta- muttiyāvali - samō sahai jattha siya-sālō ॥ 36 ॥
garuō gujjara-dēsō nagarāgara - gāma - gōulāinnō ।
sura-lōya - riddhi-maya-vijaya paṁḍiō maṁḍiō jēṇa ॥ 37 ॥
jaṁmi niraṁtara - sura- bhavaṇa-paḍima-pavaṇaṁbu - pūra - sitta vva ।

kumārapālapratibōdhē
sahalā maṇōraha-dumā dhammiya - lōyassa jāyaṁti ॥ 38 ॥
jattha sahati suvannā kaṁcaṇa - kalasā ya sura- ghara - sirēsu ।
gayaṇa-bhama -
khinna- nisaṇṇa- khayara-taruṇīṇa pīṇa thaṇā ॥ 39 ॥
abbhaṁliha- sura-maṁdira - sira- vilasira-kaṇaya-kēyaṇa - bhuēhiṁ ।
naccai va jattha lacchī suṭṭāṇa-nivēsa harisa-vasā ॥ 40 ॥
jattha maṇi-bhavaṇa- bhittīsa pēcchiuṁ attaṇō vi paḍibiṁbaṁ ।
paḍijuvai - saṁkirīō kuppaṁti piēsa muḍāō ॥ 41 ॥
jammi mahā - purisāṇaṁ dhaṇa-dāṇaṁ niruvamaṁ niēūṇa ।
ajahattha-nāmaō lajiō vva dūraṁ gaō ghaṇaō ॥ 42 ॥
jassi samaccharamaṇā jalāsayā na uṇa dhammiya - samūhā ।
kamalōvakārayā sūra - rassiṇō na uṇa sappurisā ॥ 43 ॥
jattha ramaṇīṇa rūvaṁ ramaṇijjaṁ pēcchiūṇa amarīō ।
lajaṁtīō ciṁtāi kaha vi niddaṁ na pāvaṁti ॥ 44 ॥
narēndravaṁśavarṇanam
tatthāsi mūlarāō rāyā cōlukka-kula- naha - mayaṁkō ।
jaṇiyā jaṇāṇukūlā mūlēṇa va jēṇa nīi-layā ॥ 45 ॥
jasa- puṁḍarīya- maṇḍala - maṁḍiya- baṁbhaṁḍa- maṁḍavō tattō ।
khaṁḍiya -vipakkha-muṁḍō caṁḍō cāmuṁḍarāya - nivō ॥ 46 ॥
tatō vallaharāō rāyā rahavallahō vva ramaṇijō ।
jēṇa turaēhim̐ jagajhaṁpaṇu tti kittī jaē pattā ॥ 47 ॥
tattō dulaharāō rāyā samaraṁgaṇaṁmi jassa karē ।
-
karavālō chajjai jaya - sirōha maya - ṇāhi -tilaō vva ॥ 48 ॥
tattō bhīmanariṁdō bhīmō vva pathaṁḍa bāhu-bala- bhīmō ।
ari-cakkaṁ akkamiḍaṁ pāyaḍiō jēṇa paṁḍu-jasō ॥ 49 ॥
tō kannaēva nivaī jassāsi - jalaṁmi vilasiyā suiraṁ ।
jasa- rāyahaṁsa - sahiyā jaya lacchī rāyahaṁsī vva ॥ 50 ॥
tayaṇu jayasiṁhadēvō paryaṁḍa-bhuya-daṁḍa- maṁḍavē jassa ।
kitti payāva-misēṇaṁ cirakālaṁ kīliyaṁ mihuṇaṁ ॥ 51 ॥
tammi gaē sura-lōyaṁ kāuṁ va surēsarēṇa saha mittiṁ ।

prastāva: ]
kumārapālasya dharmasvarūpajijñāsā
kamala-vaṇaṁ va diṇiṁdē atthamiē mauliyaṁ bhuvaṇaṁ ॥ 52 ॥
tattō pahāṇa - purisā niya-maha- māhappa - vijiya- sura-guruṇō ।
rajjamaṇāhaṁ dahuṁ jaṁpati parupparaṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 53 ॥
āsi siri- bhīmaēvassa naṁdaṇō jaṇiya-jaṇa-maṇāṇaṁdō ।
kaya-sayala - khōṇi- khēmō nāmēṇaṁ khēmarāu ti ॥ 54 ॥
tassa taṇaō tiṇīkaya-kaṁdappō dēha - suṁdarattēṇa ।
dēvapasāya - nāmō dēva- pasāyaṇa- pahāṇa-maṇō ॥ 55 ॥
tassaṁgaruhō garuō para - ramaṇi - paraṁmuhō mahā-sūrō ।
tiyasa - sari- sarisa - kittī tihuyaṇapālō tti nāmēṇa ॥ 56 ॥
tassa sruō tēyassī pasanna-vayaṇō suriṁda- sama- rūvō ।
dēva-guru- prayaṇa- parō parōvayārujjaō dhīrō ॥ 57 ॥
dakkhō dakkhinna-nihī nayavaṁtō savva-satta-saṁjuttō ।
sūrō cāī paḍivanna- vacchalō kumaravālō tti ॥ 58 ॥
ēsō juggō rajassa rajjalakkhaṇa-saṇāha - savvaṁgō ।
tā jhatti ṭhavijjau nigguṇēhiṁ pajjattamannēhiṁ ॥ 59 ॥
ēvaṁ parupparaṁ maṁtiūṇa taha giṇhiūṇa saṁvāyaṁ ।
sāmuddiya- mōhuttiya sāuṇiya- nēmittiya - narāṇa ॥ 60 ॥
rajjami pariṭṭhaviō kumāravālō pahāṇa - purisēhiṁ ।
tattō bhuvaṇamasēsaṁ pariōsa - paraṁ vva saṁjāyaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
tuha- hāra-daṁturiya- gharaṁgaṇa nacciya- cāru-vilāsa-paṇaṁgaṇa |
ninbhara - saha - bhariya bhuvaṇaṁtara vajjiya-maṁgala-tūra- niraṁtara ॥ 62 ॥
sāhiya- disā - caukkō cau - vvihōvāya- dhariya- caḍa - vannō ।
cau-vagga- sēvaṇa- parō kumara - nariṁdō kuṇai rajjaṁ ॥ 63 ॥
kumārapālasya dharmasvarūpajijñāsā
aha annayā viyaḍḍē bahuṇō bahu-dhamma-sattha-nāṇaḍḍē ।
vippapahāṇē hakkāriūṇa rannā bhaṇiyamēvaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
kari turaya-raha- samiddhaṁ nariṁda-siri-kusuma-līḍha-paya- vīḍhaṁ ।
laṁghiya - vasaṇa-sahassō saṁpattō jaṁ ahaṁ rajjaṁ ॥ 65 ॥
taṁ puvva-bhavē dhammō suhēka hēū kaō maē kō vi ।

kumārapāla pratibōdhē
kajjassa daṁsaṇāō jāṇaṁti hi kāraṇaṁ niuṇā ॥ 66 ॥
tā dhammassa sarūvaṁ kahēhi paribhāviūṇa satthatthaṁ ।
jēṇa tamāyariūṇaṁ karēmi maṇuyattaṇaṁ sahalaṁ ॥ 67 ॥
maṇuyattaṇē vi laddhē kuṇaṁti dhammaṁ na jē vimūḍhamaṇā ।
tē rōhaṇaṁ pi pattā mahaggharayaṇaṁ na giṇhati ॥ 68 ॥
tō vuḍa-baṁbhaṇēhiṁ nivassa vēyāi - sattha- pannattō ।
pasu-vaha-pahāṇa - jāgāi - lakkhaṇō akkhiō dhammō ॥ 69 ॥
taṁ sōūṇa nivēṇaṁ phuriya-vivēṣaṇa ciṁtiyaṁ cittē ।
ahaha diya-puṁgavēhiṁ na sōhaṇī sāhiō dhammō ॥ 70 ॥
paṁciṁdiya-jīva- vahō nikkaruṇa-maṇēhim̐ kīraē jattha ।
jai sō vi hōja dhammō natthi ahammō taō kō vi ॥ 71 ॥
tā dhammassa sarūvaṁ jahaṭṭiyaṁ kiṁ imē na jāṇaṁti ? |
kiṁ vā jāṇaṁtā vihu maṁ vippā vippayāraṁti ॥ 72 ॥
iya ciṁtāē niddaṁ alahaṁtō nisi bharaṁmi naranāhō ।
namiūṇa amacēṇaṁ bāhaḍadēvēṇa vinnattō ॥ 73 ॥
dhammādhamma-sarūvaṁ nariṁda ! jai jāṇiuṁ tumaṁ mahasi ।
khaṇamēkamēgacittō nisuṇasu jaṁ kiṁ pi jaṁpēmi ॥ 74 ॥
śrīdattagurōḥ yaśōbhadranupapratibōdhaḥ
āsi bhrama- rahiō punnatalla-guru-gaccha-duma-kusuma-gucchō ।
samaya-mayaraṁda - sārō siridattagurū surahi sālō ॥ 75 ॥
sō vihiṇā viharaṁtō gāmāgara - nagara -bhūsiyaṁ vasuhaṁ ।
vāgaḍa - visaya- vayaṁsē rayaṇapurē pura-varē pattō ॥ 76 ॥
tattha nivō jasabhaddō bhadda-gayaṁdō vva dāṇa - laḍa - jasō ।
vēri-kari-dalaṇa-sūrō unnaya-vaṁsō visāla-karō ॥ 77 ॥
tammiṁ nariṁda-maṁdira - adūra-dēsaṁmi gihiuṁ vasahiṁ ।
caṁdō vva tāraya-juō muṇi-pariyariō ṭhiō ēsō ॥ 78 ॥
tassa suhā rasa - sāraṇi-sahōyaraṁ dhamma - dēsaṇaṁ sōḍaṁ ।
saṁvēya-vāsiya-maṇā kē vi pavajjaṁti pavvajjaṁ ॥ 79 ॥
annē gihattha - dhammōciāī bārasavayāiṁ giṇhaṁti ।

prastāvaḥ
mūladēvakathānakam
mōkkha-taru- bīya-bhūyaṁ sammattaṁ āyaraṁti parē ॥ 80 ॥
aha annayā nisāē sajjhāya-jhuṇiṁ muṇīṇa sōūṇa ।
jasabhadda- nivō saṁvēga - parigaō ciṁtaē cittē ॥ 81 ॥
dhannā ēē muṇiṇō kāuṁ jē savva-saṁga parihāraṁ ।
para-lōya - maggamēkaṁ mukka-bhavāsā payaṁpaṁti ॥ 82 ॥
tā ēyāṇa muṇīṇaṁ paya- pauma-namaṁsaṇēṇa appāṇaṁ ।
parigaliya- pāva - paṁkaṁ pahāya - samaē karissāmi ॥ 83 ॥
ēvaṁ dhamma- maṇōraha - kaliya-maṇō patthivō lahai niddaṁ ।
maṁgala-tūra - ravēṇaṁ paḍibuddhō pacchimē jāmē ॥ 84 ॥
kaya-sayala - gōsa- kiccō samatta sāmaṁta- maṁti- pariyariō ।
kari turaya-raha- samēō pattō siridatta guru-pāsē ॥ 85 ॥
bhūmi- nihiuttamaṁgō bhatti- samaggō guruṁ paṇamiūṇa ।
puraō nivō niviṭṭhō kayaṁjalī bhaṇiumāḍhatō ॥ 86 ॥
bhayavaṁ ! dhannā tumbhē saṁsārāsārayaṁ maṇē dhariḍaṁ ।
jē catta- savva-saṁgā para - lōyārāhaṇaṁ kuṇaha ॥ 87 ॥
amhārisā ahannā paralōya - paraṁmuhā mahāraṁbhā ।
aniyatta-visaya-taṇhā jē ihabhava - mētta - paḍibaḍā ॥ 88 ॥
aha jaṁpiuṁ pavattō siridattagurū nahaṁgaṇaṁ sayalaṁ ।
tava - siri-muttā-paṁtīhi daṁta-kaṁtīhi dhavalaṁtō ॥ 89 ॥
muha-sasi-pavēsa- suviṇōvamāi dulahaṁ narattaṇaṁ lahiuṁ ।
khaṇamēkaṁ pi māō buhēṇa dhammē na kāyavvō ॥ 90 ॥
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ ! kā sā suviṇōvama tti ? mē kahasu ।
guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ naravara ! kahēmi jaṁ pucchiaṁ tumaē ॥ 91 ॥
mūladēvakathānakam
asthi purī ujjēṇī avaṁtī - visayāvayaṁsa- sāricchā |
sarakūvavāvi- pamuhā jalāsayā na uṇa jattha jaṇā ॥ 92 ॥
tattha-tthi mūladēvō rāya -suō pavara- rūva-lāvannō ।
nīsēsa - kalā-kusalō vinnāṇa-nihī guṇa-samaggō ॥ 93 ॥

kumārapālapratibōdhē
sō pāḍaliputtāō jūya-pasattō'vamāṇiō piuṇā ।
nīhariō puhavīē bhramamāṇō āgaō tattha ॥ 94 ॥
guliyā-paōga- nimmiya - vāmaṇa-rūvēṇa viviha- kuhagēhiṁ ।
gaṁdhavvāi - kalāhi ya tēṇa jaṇō vimyaṁ nīō ॥ 95 ॥
tattha-tthi dēvadattā gaṇiyā ruvāi-guṇa-garuya-gavvā ।
sā purisēṇa na kēṇa vi raṁjijjai suyamiṇaṁ tēṇa ॥ 96 ॥
sō tīê khōhaṇatthaṁ gōsē savihaṁmi viviha-bhaṁgīhiṁ ।
bahumanna-vēha - maṇaharamāḍhattō gāiuṁ gīyaṁ ॥ 97 ॥
taṁ suṇiya dēvadattā ciṁtai vāṇī ahō asāmannā ।
tā kō imō ? tti jāṇaṇa- nimittamaha pēsaē cēḍī ॥ 98 ॥
dahuṁ tamāgayā ya cēḍī vinnavaha dēvadattāē ।
gāēi vāmaṇō kō vi ēsa dēhēṇa na guṇēhiṁ ॥ 99 ॥
sā tassāṇayaṇatthaṁ cēḍiṁ paṭṭhavaha māhaviṁ khujjaṁ ।
gaṁtūṇa mūladēvaṁ sā jaṁpara sāmiṇī amha ॥ 100 ॥
vinnavai dēvadattā aṇuggahaṁ kuṇaha ēha amha gharaṁ ।
tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ nisiddhō vēsāsaṁgō visihāṇa ॥ 101 ॥
khujjāē taha ēsō pannaviō viviha- bhaṇii-niuṇāē ।
jaha caliō tīē saha na dukkaraṁ kiṁ pi kusalāṇaṁ ॥ 102 ॥
vijjā- kalāsu kusalēṇa tēṇa apphāliūṇa sā khujjā ।
pauṇīkayā pahiḍā tīē nīō gharaṁ ēsō ॥ 103 ॥
diṭṭhō ya dēvadattāi vāmaṇō ēsa auvva-lāvaṇṇō ।
vimhiya-maṇāi tīē tassa kayā uciya- paḍivattī ॥ 104 ॥
khujjā aṇēṇa paraṇīkayatti muṇiūṇa vimhiyā bāḍhaṁ ।
sā raṁjiyā ya imiṇā mahurālāvaṁ kuṇatēṇa ॥ 105 ॥
jaō-
aṇuṇaya- kusalaṁ parihāsa-pēsalaṁ laḍaha - vāṇidullaliyaṁ ।
ālavaṇaṁ pi hu chēyāṇa kammaṇaṁ kimiha mūlīhiṁ ॥ 106 ॥
pattō vīṇāgārē tatthēkkā tēṇa vāiyā vīṇā ।
tō bhai dēvadattā bhadda ! kalā avikalā tujjha ॥ 107 ॥
jaṁpēi mūladēvō ujjēṇīē jaṇō ahō niuṇō ।
muṇai guṇā-guṇa-vr̥ttaṁ tō bhaṇiyaṁ dēvadattā ॥ 108 ॥

9
bhō kimēttha khūṇaṁ ? । tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ - vaṁsō asuddhō, sagabbhā ya taṁtī,
appaha vīṇaṁ daṁsēmi । samappiyā vīṇā mūladēvassa । kaḍḍiō tēṇa vaṁsāō kakkarō,
taṁtīē vālō samāraiūṇa vājhyā vīṇā, kayā paravasa-bhaṇā sa pariyaṇā dēvadattā ।
ciṁtiyaṁ tīē - ahō pacchanna-rūvō vissakammā, ēsō visajiō vīṇā vāyagō ।
āgayā bhōyaṇa - vēlā । bhaṇiyaṁ dēvadattāē - - vāharaha aṁgamaddayaṁ, jēṇa dō vi
amhē majjāmō । mūladēvēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ -aṇumannaha ahaṁ caiva karēmi tumha abhaṁgaṇaṁ ।
tīē bhaṇiyaṁ kimēyaṁ pi jāṇasi । sō bhagaina jāṇāmi sammaṁ, paraṁ ṭhiō
jāṇaga-sayāsē । āṇīyaṁ caṁpaga - tēlaṁ | āḍhatō sō abhaṁgiḍaṁ । vimhiya-maṇāē
ciṁtitamēyāē ahō asamāṇaṁ vinnāṇaṁ, ahō kaya-maṇukkarisō kara-kamala-pharisō,
tā hōyavvaṁ imiṇā kēṇāvi pacchanna-rūvēṇa siddha-purisēṇaṁ । taō paṇaya - patthaṇā-
puvvaṁ payaṁpiō sō - bhō mahāsatta ! guṇēhiṁ vinnāō bhaē tumaṁ uttamapurisō nti ।
jamhā-
abhihāṇamabhaṇatō vi hōi payaḍō guṇēhiṁ sappurisō ॥
channō vi caṁdaṇa-dumō kiṁ na kahijai parimalēṇaṁ ।
tā daṁsēhi attāṇayaṁ, ukkaṁṭhiyaṁ tuha daṁsaṇassa mē hiyayaṁ । ēvaṁ nibbaṁdhē
kaē īsi hasiūṇa avaṇīyā muhāō mūladēvēṇa guliyā । jāō sahāvatthō
ēsō । mayaṇaṁ va maṇahara-rūva-lāvanna tāruna punna- dēhaṁ taṁ daddūṇa vimhiya-muhīē
mahā-pasāō tti bhaṇiya tīē anbhaṁgiō sahatthēhiṁ । tō kayaṁ majjaṇaṁ dōhiṁ pi ।
parihāviō sō dēvadsāiṁ । tēṇa samaṁ jimiyā mahā - vibhūīē sā । kayā kalā-
viyāra-guṭṭhī imēhiṁ । bhaṇiō sō tīē - mahābhāga ! tumaṁ vinā na annēṇaṁ
raṁjiyaṁ mē maṇaṁ, tō sacamēyaṁ,
nayaṇēhiṁ kō na dīsaha kēṇa samāṇaṁ na huṁti ullāvā ।
jaṁ puṇa hiyayāṇaṁṁ jaṇēi taṁ māṇusaṁ viralaṁ ॥
tā nicamēva mē gihāgamaṇēṇa aṇuggahō kāyavyō । mūladēvēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ-
guṇarāgiṇa ! anna- dēsiēsa niḍaṇēsu ya amhārisē na rēhaē siṇēhō । tīē
bhaṇiyaṁ - vidēsaṁ gayā vi guṇiṇō gacchaṁti gōravaṁ ।
jaō-
jalahi-visaṁghaṭṭiēṇa vi nivabhijjai harasirammi caṁdēṇa ।
jattha gayā tattha gayā guṇiṇō sīsēṇa vujjhati ॥

maggiyaṁ । vahai mūladēvōvari paōsaṁ, maggaē chiddāṇi । tassa saṁkāē avasara

dēvadattāē vr̥ttaṁ - aṁba ! kō saguṇō nigguṇō va tti parikkhēhi । taō
akkāē bhaṇiō ayalō। dēvadattāē ucchuicchā । tēṇa ucchu-bhariyaṁ pēsiyaṁ sa-
gaḍaṁ । tīē vr̥ttaṁ - kimahaṁ kariṇī jaṁ sapatta-ḍālā ucchū pēsiyā । ihi mūladēvaṁ
maggēsu ucchu jēṇa jāṇijai vivēgē tēsiṁ visēsō । akkāē kahāviyaṁ mūladē-
vassa ucchū pēsēhitti । tēṇāvi gahigaō laṭṭhāō ucchu-gaṭṭhīō nicchalliūṇa
kayāō du-aṁgula - ppamāṇaō rasa- kuṁḍiyāō gaṁḍiyāō cāujjāyāvaguṁḍiyāō
kappūra-parāya-maṁḍiyāō mūlā bhinnāō sarāva saṁpuḍē khiviūṇa pēsiyāō ।
dahūṇa dēvadattā tāō vajaraī pēcchasē amba ! |
dhuttāhiva acalāṇaṁ suvanna-rīrīṇa va visēsaṁ ॥
akkāē ciṁtiyaṁ - acaṁta- mūḍhā ēsā, na mēllēi mūladēvaṁ । taō ayalēṇa
saha maṁtiō tanniggamōvāō । ayalēṇa bhaṇiyā dēvadattā - ahaṁ gāmaṁ gami
ssāmiti । niggaō sō । pavēsiō imīē mūladēvō । jāṇāviō
jaṇaṇīē ayalō āgaō sāmaggīē । diṭṭhō dēvadattāē । patta-karaṁḍō vva palaṁ-
ka- hiṭṭhā ṭhāviō mūladēvō । lakkhiō । ayalēṇa । nivisiūṇa pallēkē bhaṇiyā
sā ' karēha nhāṇa - sāmariṁga ' । tīē vr̥ttaṁ -- ēvaṁ, tā uṭṭhēha, niyaṁsaha putti, jēṇa
abhaṁgēmi । ayalēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ-
ajja suviṇammi pahāō pallēkatthō niyattha-vatthōhaṁ ।
tō saccamiṇaṁ kāhaṁ jēṇa na hōjjā aṇattha-phalaṁ ॥
tō bhāi dēvadattā tūlī dhūlī havēja taṇu ēsā ।
ayalō jaṁpai kiṁ tē kiviṇattaṁ ērisaṁ suyaṇu ! ॥
ayalē paiṁmi annāō ki na tūlīō tujjha hōhiṁ ti ।
sīējja sō na lavaṇēṇa jassa rayaṇāyarō mittō ॥
sā akkāē buttā paḍivajjasu putti ! jaṁ bhaṇai acalō ।
tō abhaṁgu-vvaṭṭaṇa- pahāṇāī kayāī pallēkē ॥
gahiyāuhā paviṭṭhā purisā akkāi saṁniō ayalī ।
khali-salila-bhariya-gattaṁ dhuttaṁ hēṭṭhāō kaḍḍhē ॥
gahiuṁ kēsēsu imō bhaṇiō nayapaṁḍiō 'si mē kahasu ।
kō hōi niggahō tē imassa kammassa aṇurūvō ॥
dhaṇa- vivasāō vēsāō huṁti tā jai imīē tuha kajaṁ ।
tā gāma-paṭṭayaṁ piva giṇhēsi na kiṁ bahu-dhaṇēṇa ॥

13
ladvā kummāsā । niggacchaṁtēṇa tēṇa diṭṭhō tivva-tava-susiya- gattō mahā-sattō
māsakkhamaṇa-pāraṇatthaṁ tattha pavisamāṇō samaṇō ॥
taṁ dahuṁ sō ciṁtai jāō puṇṇōdaō ahō majjha ।
bhava -
jalahi-jāṇavattaṁ pattamiṇaṁ jaṁ maē pattaṁ ॥ 1 ॥
tā dāḍaṁ kummāsē ēyassa karēmi jīviyaṁ sahalaṁ ।
tattō dinnā muṇiṇō kummāsā huṁti tēṇa paḍhiyaṁ ca ॥ 2 ॥
dhannāṇaṁ khu narāṇaṁ kummāsā sāhupāraṇaē ।
ētthaṁtarasmi tanbhatti-raṁjiyā dēvayā bhaṇai bhayaṇē ॥ 3 ॥
bhō mūladēva puttaya ! suṁdaramaṇuciṭṭhiyaṁ imaṁ tumaē ।
tattō maggasu gāhāi pacchimadvēṇa rucaē jaṁ bhē ॥ 4 ॥
harisa - paravvasa - hiyaēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ mūladēvēṇa ।
maha dēhi dēvadattaṁ daṁtisahassaṁ ca rajjaṁ ca ॥ 5 ॥
ēvaṁ hōhi tti bhaṇēi dēvayā tō muṇiṁ namaha dhuttō ।
gāmaṁmi maggiuṁ sō puṇō vi bhikkhaṁ sayaṁ bhuṁjē ॥ 6 ॥
pattō kamēṇa vinnāyaḍaṁmi rayaṇīē pahiyasālāē ।
suttō dhuttō pēcchai pacchima-jāmē suviṇamēyaṁ ॥ 7 ॥
maha paḍipunnō caṁdō muhē paviṭṭhō siaha tahiṁ kō vi ।
kappaḍiō ēvaṁ ciya suviṇaṁ dahūṇa jaggēi ॥ 8 ॥
annēsiṁ kappaḍiyāṇa kahai ēkkēṇa tattha vāgariyaṁ ।
lahihisi tumaṁ akhaṁḍaṁ sakhaṁḍa - ghayamaṁḍagaṁ ajja ॥ 9 ॥
taṁ sōuṁ kappaḍiō ēvaṁ hōu ti jaṁpaē tuṭṭō |
bayarēhiṁ pi siyālassa ūsavō jāyaē jamhā ॥ 10 ॥
tēsiṁ vivēga vajjiya-maṇāṇa dhuttāṇa bhakkhaṇaṁ suviṇaṁ ।
rayaṇaṁ pi daṁsiyaṁ khalu bhaṇaṁti mukkhā uvala-khaṇḍaṁ ॥ 11 ॥
kappaḍiēṇa jahuttō gharachāiṇiyāi maṁḍaō laḍō ।
pāēṇa jaō suviṇō phalai viyārāṇusārēṇa ॥ 12 ॥
mūladēvō gōsē gaō ārāmaṁ । tōsiō tattha kusumuccaya- sāhijjēṇa mālāgā -
rō । dinnāī tēṇa puṣpaphalāī । tāī dhētūna suībhūō gaō suviṇa-sattha- pāḍhagassa
gēhaṁ । puppha-phala- samappaṇa-puvvaṁ paṇamiūṇa taṁ pucchaē suviṇatthaṁ । uvajjhāō saha-
risō bhai-sumuhuttē kahissāmi suviṇa phalaṁ । ajja tāva atihī hōsu amhāṇaṁ ।

=== Kumara1output-14-to-14.json ==========================
14
kumārapāla pratibōdhē
[ prathamaḥ
haviūṇa bhuṁjāviūṇa ya sagōravaṁ pariṇāviō niya-kannaṁ mūladēvō uvajjhāēṇa ।
satta-dina- majjhē tumaṁ rāyā hōhisi tti siṭṭō tassa suviṇatthō । laḍa - [ hiṭṭha]maṇō
mūladēvō tattha vasamāṇō gaō paṁcama-diṇē nayara bāhiṁ, pasuttō ya caṁpaya-talē ।
tayā ya tattha pathivō attō pattō paṁcataṁ । ahivāsiyāṇi paṁca divvāṇi, bha-
miūṇa maggē [jjhē] nayarīē niggayāṇi bāhiṁ, pattāṇi mūladēva - pāsaṁ । aparica-
ttamāṇa-tarucchāyāē hēṭuō taṁ daṭṭhūṇa gajiaṁ gaēṇa । hēsiyaṁ haēṇa । bhiṁgārēṇa
kaō agghō । cāmarēhiṁ vīiō ēsō । ṭhiyaṁ sirōvari siyāyavattaṁ, ārōviō
sō khaṁdhi siṁdhurēṇaṁ । viviha tūra - ravāūriya- diyaṁtarō paviṭṭhō nayaraṁ । ahisittō
maṁti- sāmaṁtēhiṁ । bhaṇiyaṁ gayaṇa-yala-gayāē dēvayāē - bhō ēsa asēsa - kalā- pāra-
ō payaṁḍa - vikkamō vikkamarāō nāma rāyā, tā ēyassa sāsaṇē jō na vahissai taṁ
niggahissāmiti । taō savvē sāmaṁtāiṇō āṇā - parā jāyā । sō udāraṁ
rajja - suhaṁ aṇuhavaṁtō ciṭṭhai । jāyā tassa ujjēṇisāmiṇā jiyasattuṇā saha
parōppara - pāhuḍa - pēsaṇēṇa pīī । iō ya dēvadattā tārisaṁ viḍaṁbaṇaṁ daddūṇa virattā
ya ayalōvari । nimbhacchiō tīē ayalō, bhō davva- dappaṁdha ! kiṁ tē ahaṁ kula-
ghariṇī jamēvaṁ mē gihē vavaharasi, tā majjha gēhē aō paraṁ nāgaṁtavvaṁ ti bha-
ṇiūṇa gayā rannō pāsaṁ । namiūṇa vinnattō rāyā-dēva ! dēhi mē varaṁ । rannā
vr̥ttaṁ - maggasu jahicchaṁ, jēṇa taṁ payacchāmi । tīē vuttaṁ - mūladēvaṁ viṇā na
annō purisō āṇavēyavvō, ēsō ya ayalō mama gharaṁ āgacchaṁtō nivāriyavvō ।
rannā vuttaṁ - ēvaṁ, paraṁ kahēhi kō ēttha hēū । taō kahiō māhavīē । ruṭṭēṇa
rannā hakkārikaṇa bhaṇiō ayalō । bhō ! mama nayarīē ēyāī dunni rayaṇāī, tāī
tumaṁ khalīkarēsi, tā pāṇa-viṇāsaṁ viṇā natthi tē daṁḍō | dēvadattāē nivāriō ।
rannā vr̥ttaṁ - imīē vayaṇēṇa mukkō tumaṁ, kiṁtu taṁ āṇiūṇa ēttha vasijjasu ।
taō nabhiūṇa rāyāṇaṁ niggaō ayalō । naṭṭa-rayaṇaṁ va satrvattha taṁ gavēsiuṁ
pavattō, tahāvi na laḍō sō । taō tīē cēva ūṇimāē bhariūṇa bhaṁḍassa
vahaṇāīṁ gaō pārasa - kulaṁ ।
aha mūladēva rāō ciṁtai maha bhōyaṇaṁ alavaṇaṁ va ।
na kuṇai harisaṁ rajjaṁ pi vajjiyaṁ dēvadattāē ॥
taō tēṇa pahāṇa - pāhuḍa - parigaō pēsiō dūō, gaō sō ujjēṇīē,
vinnattō tēṇa rāyā - dēva ! dēvayā - dinna - rajjō dēvadattāṇurattō mūladēvō jaṁpai " jaha
imī tumhaṁ ca rucaē tā pēsijjau ēsa" tti । rannā vr̥ttaṁ - kittiyamiṇaṁ maggiyaṁ

15
mūladēvēṇa । jaō mama tassa ya rajjē vi natthi bhēō । taō hakkāriā dēvadattā ।
kahiūṇa vr̥ttaṁtaṁ bhaṇiyā sā । punnā tē maṇōrahā, tō gaccha tattha tumaṁ । tīē
vr̥ttaṁ - mahā-pasāō ti । rannā saṁpūiūṇa pēsiyā sā pattā vinnāyaḍaṁ ।
tō harisa - nivbharēṇaṁ vikkamarāēṇa guru-vibhūīē ।
niya - hiyayammi va viulē bhavaṇaṁmi pavēsiyā ēsā ॥
jaṇiya- jiṇa-paḍima-pūō naēṇa sō rajja- pālaṇujjuntō ।
paribhutta-dēvadatta tivagga- laggō gamai kālaṁ ॥
aha pārasa - kūlāō viḍhavia - davvō samāgaō tattha ।
ayalō pahāṇa- pāhuḍa- hatthō pattō nivaṁ dahuṁ ॥
uvalakkhiō nivēṇaṁ sō tēṇa u nōvalakkhiō rāyā ।
rannā vr̥ttaṁ kattō tumaṁ ti ayalēṇa vinnattaṁ ॥
pārasa - kūlāō samāgaō mhi paṭṭhavaha kaṁ pijō bhaṁḍa |
majjha nirūvai rannā vr̥ttaṁ sayamāgamissāmi ॥
tō paṁca-ula-samēō ayalāvāsaṁmi patthivō pattō ।
daṁsiyamimēṇa bhaṁḍa maṁjiṭṭā-paṭṭa - suttāī ॥
bhaṁḍa kimittiyaṁ ciya kahēsu saccaṁ ti paē rāyā ।
ayalō bhāsai dēvassa kiṁ purō vuccaē aliyaṁ ॥
tō rannā vajjariyaṁ imassa sēṭṭhissa saccavāissa ।
kārēha addha-dāṇaṁ sammaṁ bhaṁḍaṁ ca jōēha ||
tō vaṁsavēha - pāyappahāra - bhārēhiṁ paṁca- uliēhiṁ ।
muṇiyaṁ mahagghabhaṁḍaṁ maṁjiṭṭhāīṇa majjha gayaṁ ॥
bhinnāim̐ bhaṁḍaṭhāṇāim̐ rāya - purisēhim̐ tēsu varabhaṁḍaṁ ।
taṁ dahaṁ ruṭṭēṇaṁ rannā baṁdhāviō ayalō ||
nēyāviūṇa gēhaṁ chōḍiya-baṁdhō paryaṁpiō rannā ।
jāṇasi maṁ bhaṇai imō kō na muṇai diṇayaraṁ va tumaṁ ॥
rannā vuttaṁ alaṁ uvayāra - vayaṇēhiṁ, phuḍaṁ sāhasu jai jāṇasi । ayalēṇa
bhaṇiyaṁ - dēva na jāṇāmi sammaṁ । rannā vāharāviyā dēvadattā । āgayā varacchara
vva savvaṁga - bhūsaṇa-dharā । taṁ daṭṭhūṇa lajjiō ayalō । bhaṇiō dēvadattāē - bhō
ēsa sō mūladēvō, jō tumaē tayā vr̥ttō, ahaṁ pi tumaē vasaṇa - pattō mōttavvō ti
mukō ya sākkōsēṇa dēvēṇa sarīra-saṁdēha - kāraṇa - vasaṇaṁ pattō tumaṁ । taō vila-

kkha-cittēṇa tēṇa paṇamiūṇa vinnattaṁ - khamasu mē savvāvarāhaṁ, tēṇāvarāhēṇa ruṭṭhō
jiasattū na dēi ujjēṇīē mē pavēsaṁ, tumha vayaṇēṇa dāhī । rannā bhaṇiyaṁ khamiyaṁ

khamiuṁ avarāhaṁ mūladēva - vayaṇēhiṁ tassa jiyasattū |
dēha purī pavēsaṁ tammūlō jēṇa sē kōvō ॥
aha mūladēva - rajjaṁ sōuṁ sō saddhaḍō tahiṁ pattō ।

suviṇō tārisaō ciya diṭṭhō kēṇāvi annēṇa ॥

yaśōbhadra nr̥pavairāgyōtpattiḥ ।

tattha jalaṇēṇa ḍajjhata- viggahaṁ ganbha-nigbharaṁ bhuyagiṁ ।

kumārapālapratibōdhē
jassa calaṇāraviṁdaṁ caritta lacchī-vilāsa - vāsaharaṁ ।
muṇi- bhamarēhi amukkaṁ jiṇamaya-mayaraṁda-ludvēhiṁ ॥
sō viharaṁtō mahī - maṁḍalammi khaṁḍiya-payaṁḍa-bhāvariū ।
sayala - bhuvaṇē-ka-baṁdhū dhaṁdhukkayaṁ puravarē pattō ॥
sō tattha paṇamaṇa-tthaṁ samāgayāṇaṁ jaṇāṇa paurāṇaṁ ।
saṁsārā-sārattaṇa-payāsaṇiṁ dēṇaṁ kuṇai ॥
taṁ sōḍaṁ saṁviggō sarīra - suṁdara - vijiya- surakumarō ।
ēkkō vaṇiya kumārō kayaṁjalī bhaṇiumādattō ॥
bhayavaṁ ! bhavaṇṇavāō jamma-jarā-maraṇa-lahari-hīraṁtaṁ ।
maṁ nitthārasu sucāritta jāṇavatta-payāṇēṇa ॥
guruṇā vr̥ttaṁ bālaya ! kiṁ nāmō kassa vā suō taṁsi ।
tō tassa māulēṇaṁ payaṁpiaṁ nēmināmēṇa ॥
bhayavaṁ ! iha-tthi hatthi vva mōḍhakula- viṁjha-saṁbhavō bhahō ।
kaya-dēva-guru-jaṇaccō caccō nāmā pahāṇa-vaṇī ॥
nimmala-kula- saṁbhūyā bhūri-guṇābharaṇa-bhūsiya- sarīrā ।
tassa-tthi gēhiṇī cāhiṇi tti sā hōi maha bahiṇī ॥
jīē vimalaṁ sīlaṁ dadda lajjāē caṁdamā niccaṁ ।
carama - jalahimmi majjai kalaṁka- pakkhālaṇatthaṁ va ॥
tāṇaṁ taṇaō ēsō niruvama-rūvō pagiṭṭha mai-vihavō ।
bhuvaṇa-ḍaraṇa-maṇōhara - ciṁcaiō caṁgadēvō tti ॥
gabbhā-vayāra - samaē imassa jaṇaṇīē suviṇaē diṭṭhō ।
niya gēhē sahayārō samuggaō vuḍḍimaṇupattō ॥
jā puppha-phalā-raṁbhō tattō muttūṇa maṁdiraṁ majjha ।
annattha mahārāmē maṇābhirāmē imō pattō ॥
chāyāē pallavēhiṁ kusumēhiṁ phalēhiṁ tattha pavarēhiṁ ।
bahuya jaṇāṇaṁ ēsō uvayāraṁ kāumāḍhattō ॥
gabhagaē vi imissi iha dēsē naṭṭhamasiva- nāmaṁ pi ।
taha aṇabhinnō jāō lōō dubbhikkha- dukkhassa ॥
paracakka-caraḍa-cōrāi-vidhavā dūramuvagayā sacvē ।
na phuraṁti ghūya-pamuhā mēha-cchannē vi diṇanāhē ॥

hēmacandrajanmādivarṇanam ।
iya tassa jamma- diyahē jāyāī disā suhāī vimalāī ।
dēva-guru-vaṁdaṇēṇa dhammatthīṇaṁ maṇāī va ॥
harisa-jaṇaṇō jaṇāṇaṁ suyaṇō vva samīraṇō samullasiō ।
raya-pasamaṇaṁ nivaḍiyaṁ gurūṇa vayaṇaṁ va gaṁdhajalaṁ ॥
bhavaṇammi kusuma - vuṭṭhī susāmi tuhi vva sēvaē jāyā ।
kavva-guṇō vva sahiyaē phuriō gayaṇaṁmi tūra- ravō ॥
ēsō pariōsa-karō bālattaṇaō vi amaya - ghaḍiō vva ।
rayaṇaṁ va karāō karaṁ saṁcariō sayala - lōyassa ॥
saṁpai imassa cittaṁ na ramaha annattha vajjiḍaṁ dhammaṁ ।
māṇasa - saraṁmi sutuṁ haṁsassa va pallala-jalēsu ॥
guruṇā vr̥ttaṁ jattaṁ jaṁ kuṇai imō caritta paḍivattiṁ ।
jēṇa sō paramatthō jaṇaṇī- diṭṭhassa suviṇassa ॥
gahiūṇa vayaṁ avagāhiūṇa nīsēsa- sattha- paramatthaṁ ।
titthakarō vva ēsō jaṇassa uvayāraō hōhī ॥
tattō imassa jaṇayaṁ cacaṁ nāmēṇa bhaṇaha tō tubbhē ।
jaha caṁgadēvamēyaṁ vaya - gahaṇatthaṁ visajjēi ॥
sō bahu- siṇēha - juttō bahuṁ pi bhaṇiō visajjai na puttaṁ ।
tattō pattō vi darda kaujjamō saṁjama-ggahaṇē ॥
māulaya- aṇumayaṁ givhiūṇa ṭhāṇaṁtarammi saṁcaliō ।
guṇa- guruṇā saha guruṇā saṁpattō khaṁbhatitthammi ॥
tattha pavannō dikkhaṁ kuṇamāṇō sayala - saṁgha - pariōsaṁ ।
sō sōma-muhō sōmō vva sōmacaṁdō tti kayanāmō ॥
thēvēṇa vi kālēna kāūṇa tavaṁ jiṇāgamuddinaṁ ।
gaṁbhīrassa vi suya - sāgarassa pāraṁgaō ēsō ॥
dūsama-samaya-asaṁbhava-guṇōha - kaliō vibhāviḍaṁ hiyaē ।
siridēvacaṁda - guruṇā ēsō gaṇahara-paē ṭhaviō ॥
hēma - samacchavi-dēhō caṁdō vva jaṇāṇa jaṇiya-āṇaṁdō ।
tattō imō pasiddhō nāmēṇaṁ hēmacaṁdō tti ॥
nicaṁ sahāva- ucciya- samagga- lōōvayāra kaya-cittō ।
sō dēvayāi buttō viharaṁtō viviha- dēsēsu ||

kumārapālapratibōdhē
gujjara- visayaṁ muttuṁ mā kuṇasu vihāramanna- dēsēsu ।
kāhisi parōvayāraṁ jēṇittha ṭhiō tumaṁ garuyaṁ ॥
tō tīē vayaṇēṇaṁ dēnaṁtara - viharaṇāu viṇiyattō ।
ciṭṭhā ihēva ēsō paḍibōhaṁtō bhaviya vaggaṁ ॥
buha- yaṇa- cūḍāmaṇiṇō bhuvaṇa-pasiddhassa siddharāyassa ।
saṁsaya pasu savvēsu pucchaṇijō imō jāō ॥
ēassa dēsaṇaṁ nisuṇiūṇa micchatta mōhiya- maī ।
vijayasiṁhō nivō jāō jiniṁda-dhammāṇuratta-maṇō ॥
tattō tēṇittha purē rāya - vihārō karāviō rammō ।
cau - jiṇapaḍima- samiḍō siddhavihārō ya siddhipurē ॥
jayasiṁhadēva - vayaṇā nimmiyaṁ siddhahēma-vāgaraṇaṁ ।
nīsēsa -saha- lakkhaṇa- nihāṇamimiṇā muṇidēṇa ॥
amaō-vamēya-vāṇī-visālamēyaṁ a picchamāṇassa ।
āsi khaṇaṁ pi na tittī cittē jayasiṁhadēvassa ॥
tō jai tumaṁ pi vaṁchasi dhamma-sarūvaṁ jahaṭṭhiyaṁ nāuṁ ।
tō muṇipuṁgava - mēyaṁ pucchasu hōūṇa bhakti-parō ॥
iya sammaṁ dhamma-sarūva-sāhagō sāhiō amacēṇaṁ ।
tō hēmacaṁda sūriṁ kumara - nariṁdō namai nicaṁ ॥
sammaṁ dhamma-sarūvaṁ tassa samīvaṁmi pucchaē rāyā ।
muṇiya-sayalāgamatthō muṇi-nāhō jaṁpaē ēvaṁ ॥
hēmacandrasūrēḥ kumārapālaṁ prati sadbōdhaḥ ।
bhavasiṁdhu tarī tulaṁ mahalla-kallāṇa- valli jalakulaṁ ।
kaya-sayala - suha-samudayaṁ jīvadayaṁ ciya muṇasu dhammaṁ ॥
āuṁ dīhamarōgamaṁgamasamaṁ rūvaṁ pagiddhaṁ balaṁ,
sōhaggaṁ ti jaguttamaṁ nirūvamō bhōgō jasō nimmalō ।
āēsēkka - parāyaṇō pariyaṇō lacchī avicchēddaṇī,
hōjjā tassa bhavaṁtarē kuṇai jō jīvāṇukaṁpaṁ narō ॥
narayapura - sarala-saraṇī avāya saṁghāya vagdha-vaṇa-dharaṇī ।
nīsēsa- dukkha jaṇaṇī hīṁsā jīvāṇa suha-haṇaṇī ॥

25
imaṁ sōccā ṭhiō tuhikō chagalō । vimhiya-maṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kumārēṇa ।
bhayavaṁ ! ēsa chagalō kiṁ tumha paḍhiyamittēṇa caiva tuhikkō ṭhiō । sāhuṇā
vr̥ttaṁ - bhadda ! rudasammō nāma imassa purisassa piyā āsi । tēṇa khaṇāviyaṁ
imaṁ talāyaṁ, pālīē ārōviyā rukkhā, paivarisaṁ pavattiō janō, jattha chaga-
lagā vahiti । kālēṇa ruddasammō maō, jāō chagalagō । haṇiō imiṇā

daṁsaṇēṇa saṁjāya - jāisaraṇō ēsa chagalō imaṁ bhaṇai - puttaya ! kiṁ mārēsi maṁ,
tuha piyāhaṁ ruhasammō । jai na pattiyasi, tā karēmi ahinnāṇaṁ, daṁsēmi nihāṇaṁ,
jaṁ maē taha parukkhaṁ nikkhayaṁ atthi । purisēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - bhayavaṁ ! jai saccamēyaṁ tā
daṁsēu ēsō taṁ । imaṁ sōūṇa caliō chagalō, gaō bhiṁtaraṁ nihāṇa - paēsaṁ ।
pāēhiṁ pahaṇiuṁ payō । khaṇiē laddhaṁ nihāṇaṁ । jāya-paccaō muṇi-samīvē dhammaṁ
sōūṇa paḍivannō sammattaṁ । purisō (?) kumārēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ - bhayavaṁ ! jai sattha-vi-
hiyassa vi pasu vahassa ērisō pariṇāmō, tā maē kāyacyā jīva-dayā । chagalō

vuccati cōra -saddēṇa kēvalaṁ na uṇa nāyarayā ॥

taṁ pāraddhaṁ dahūṁ kumarō karuṇāi hiṁsagē bhāi |
mā haṇaha imē, tē biṁti kō tumaṁ vāragō amha ॥
niva vayaṇēṇa pasu vahaṁ kuṇimō niva-vayaṇaō ya viramāmō ।
iya bhaṇiūṇa payaddā kāuṁ taṁ dr̥ḍhayaraṁ purisā ॥

tatō vimhiya-cittō bhāṇunivō tattha saṁpattō ॥
diṭṭhō kumarō amarō vva tēṇa ramaṇīya-rūva-saṁpannō ।
sō vi namiō nariṁdaṁ jaṁpai kimimē haṇijjaṁtē ॥
nahi pasu vahēṇa asivaṁ niyattaē avi ya baḍhaē bāḍhaṁ ।

vajjaraha bhāṇurāō niyattihī bhadda ! kahamiṇaṁ asivaṁ ।

daṁsaṇiṇō savē vihu mēlasu; tō mēliyā imē rannā ।

amarasiṁhakathā |
purō bhamaṁtīi vi aṁgaṇāē
sakajjalaṁ diṭṭhiyaṁ nava tti ।
"
paḍhiḍaṁ imā samassā kumarēṇa samappiyā tēsiṁ ॥
cakkhuṁ ca huhaṁ dhaṇa-maṁḍalammi
aṇurakkhaṇaṁ tēṇa maē na nāyaṁ ।
purō bhramaṁtīi vi aṁgaṇāē
sakajjalaṁ diṭṭhiyaṁ navati ॥
""
ēvaṁ niya- niya-cittāṇusāraō juvai-vannaṇa-parēhiṁ ।
para- titthi ēhiṁ bahuhā kayaṁ samassāi puvvaddhaṁ ॥
bhaviyavvā vasēṇaṁ sōmamuṇī chagala- puvva-bhava-kahagō ।
tathāgaō aṇēṇa vi puvvaddhaṁ pūriyaṁ ēvaṁ ॥
" maggē tasā - thāvarajaṁturakkhā-
vakhittacittēṇa maē na nāyaṁ ।
purō bhamaṁtīha vi aṁgaṇāē
sakajjalaṁ diṭṭi juyaṁ na vatti ॥"
kumarō bhai imēsuṁ kassa maṇē phurai jīva dayā ।
rāyā jaṁpai jiṇa- muṇi-maṇaṁ vi muttuṁ na annēsiṁ ॥
annēsiṁ pi imassa va maṇaṁmi jaivi phurija jīva dayā ।
vayaṇaṁ pi tārisaṁ hōja na uṇa siṁgāra rasa-pavaraṁ ॥
tō muṇi-paya-pakkhālaṇa- jalēṇa ambhukkhiyaṁ nayaramakhilaṁ ।
taṁ asivaṁ uvasaṁtaṁ rāyā pariōsamāvannō ॥
jaṁpai kumaraṁ tumamuttamō tti sāmannāō jaivi nāyaṁ ।
tahavi tuha muṇiumicchara ṭhāṇa-kula-ppamuhamēsa jaṇō ॥
pura-kula- piu-pamuhaṁ kumara - saṁtiyaṁ kahaha savvamavi vimalō ।
niya-dhūyaṁ kaṇagavaī rannā pariṇāviō kumarō ॥
kumarassa kuṇai kari-turaya-kaṇaya-vatthāi - viyaraṇaṁ rāyā ।
iya tattha suhaṁ ciṭṭhai visayāsēvaṇa-parō kumarō ॥
aha purisā amarapurāu āgayā tattha tēhi vinnattō ।
kumarō tumaṁmi nayarāō niggaē sō samarasīhō ||
pāraddhi-parō rajjaṁ rakkhaṛa na parēhi viddivinaṁ taṁ ।

alaṁ pāva- hēuṇā kuṭuṁba-vattaṇēṇa, jaṁ jīva-vahēṇa kīrai । bhajjāē vr̥ttaṁ - darda bhamā-
ḍiō muṁḍēṇa kēṇa vi । na diṭṭhō tumaṁ dhammiṭṭhō, paḍissaha tē matthara dhammō,

nīō dahaṁ sunaṁdō ।

hūṇa dayāvasēṇa mukkā | āgaō gihaṁ, ēvaṁ duiya-taiya- diyahēsu vi kayaṁ । navaraṁ
ēkkassa macchassa paṁkhuḍiā khuḍiyā । bhaṇiyaṁ aṇēṇa ।

jassa kaē kōḍīō jīvāṇa vahēmi saṁpayaṁ mūḍhō ।
narayaṁ gayassa saraṇaṁ majjha kuṭuṁbaṁ na taṁ hōhī ॥
ēkkaṁ pi payaṁ vaccai jaṁ para - lōyaṁmi saha na jīvēṇa ।
tassa sarīrassa kaē kahaṁ pi kāhaṁ na jīva- vahaṁ ॥

magaha - visayā-vayaṁsaṁ rāyagihaṁ nāma atthi vara-nayaraṁ ।

disi bahu-vihasaṇēṇaṁ chajjai jasa-kusuma-nivahēṇa ॥

31
sēṇa caṁḍālēṇa dāmannagō nāsiumādattō, niyattō caṁḍālō । daṁsiyaṁ aṁguli - khaṁḍa
sāgarapōyassa । sō ya paccujjīviuvva paraṁ pariōsamāvannō । dāmannagō araṇṇē
paribhamaṁtō diṭṭhō sāgarapōyasaṁtiēṇa gōuliēṇa । suṁdarāgārō tti pucchiō 'kō
tumaṁ' ti । dāmannagēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - ucchannavaṁsō vaṇiyaputtō'haṁ । taō samuppanna - karuṇēṇa
nīō niya- gharaṁ । bhaṇiyā niya-ghariṇī, aputtāē tuha imō puttaō, parituṭṭhā ēsā ।
viṇaya- ppamuha-guṇēhiṁ tāṇaṁ pāṇa-ppiō imō jāō ।
savvattha guṇēhiṁ piyaṁ jaṁ kīrai taṁ kimacchēraṁ ॥
aha kāma - kēli - bhavaṇaṁ taruṇī yaṇa-nayaṇa- bhasala - kamalavaṇaṁ ।
sō dēha - suṁdarattaṇa- guṇavvaṇaṁ jōvvaṇaṁ pattō ॥
annayā gō-ula-palōyaṇatthaṁ tatthāgaō sāgarapōō । dahūṇa dāmannagaṁ
sāsaṁkēṇa pucchiō aṇēṇa gōuliō 'kō ēsutti । tēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - aṇāhō ti
ihāgaō ēsō, maē aputrēṇa puttō paḍivanō । taō takahaṇāō khaṁḍiyaṁguli-
daṁsaṇāō ya ciṁtiyamiṇaṁ sāgarapōēṇaṁ । jō maē mārāviō bālō sō cēva
ēsō, nūṇaṁ na vāvāiō caṁḍālēṇa । ahaha saṁjāō tāva bāhira - dhaṇassa sāmī
imō, kimannā hōi muṇi-vayaṇaṁ, tahāvi purisayārō na muttavvō tti । taō
bhaṇiō gōuliō, saṁpayaṁ gamissāmō gēhaṁ । tēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - cirakālā tumbhē
āgayā, ajjavi na gō- ulaṁ nirūviyaṁ । sāgarapōēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ— atthi mahaṁtaṁ
kajjaṁ । gōuliēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - jai ēvaṁ tā appēha lēhaṁ, jēṇa mē puttō vuccai ।
sāgarapōēṇa sa-hattha-lihiyaṁ lēhaṁ apiūṇa pēsiō dāmannagō । gaō sō
rāyagihaṁ, parissaṁtō vīsamiō mayaṇa dēva ulē । āgayā tassa niddā ।
aha tattha visā nāmēṇa mayaṇa- pūyā nimittamaṇupattā ।
tiya-lukka-tilaya-bhūyā sāgarapōyassa varadhūyā ॥
tīē ya mayaṇa- pūyaṁ kuṇamāṇī ēsa vimhaya - rasēhiṁ ।
nava-nīluppala-dala- dōharēhi nayaṇēhiṁ sō diṭṭhō ॥
jacca - suvanna savannō visāla-vacchatthalō palaṁba - bhuō ।
kamalāruṇa-kara-calaṇō kō ēsō kāma-sama-rūvō ॥
ēyaṁ vibhāvayantī lēhaṁ piu mudda-muddiyaṁ dihaṁ ।

kumārapālapratibōdhē
[ prathama:
taō tīē ciṁtiyaṁ nūṇaṁ tāyēṇa maha juggō ēsa laddhō varō, divasaṁ ca
suṁdaraṁ dihaṁ, tēṇa ēsō sigdhaṁ pēsiō । jaṁ ca visaṁmi aṇussārō taṁ bhamō tti ।
taō aṇussāraṁ phusiūṇa nayaṇaṁjaṇēṇa āyāra - rēhā kayā, puṇōvi lēhō muddi-
ūṇa tahēva mukkō, parituṭṭamāṇasā gayā gēhaṁ । thōva - vēlāē ya uṭṭhīūṇa dāmannagō
pattō sāgarapōya-gēhaṁ । samappiō samuddadattassa । lēhē vāiūṇa avadhāriō
Sṇēṇa hatthō । 'tāyāēsō mē pamāṇaṁ ti mannatēṇa kayā vivāha sāmaggī, sama-
ggō vi mēliō sayaṇa-vaggō । saṁvacchariya viṇicchiya takkāla- laggē visāē
kara-ggahaṇaṁ kārāviō dāmannagō । pāraddhaṁ vaḍāvaṇaṁ ।
ābharaṇa-kiraṇa-dippaṁta-dēha aharīkaya-surabahū-rūvarēha ।
ghaṇa- kuṁkuma-kaddama ghara-duvāri khuppaṁta-calaṇa naccaṁti nāri ॥
ētyaṁtarē pattō nagaraṁ sāgarapōō । maggi miliēṇa saṁlattō lōēṇa ।
suṁdarī tumaē jāmāugō pēsiō । sāgarapōēṇa ciṁtiyaṁ - nūṇaṁ tēṇa durappaṇā pa-
riṇīyā mē dhūyā । gihāgaēṇa diṭṭhō vivāha- kaṁkaṇālaṁkiya-karō dāmannagō । hā !
ahaṁ annā ciṁtēmi, kajjaṁ annahā pariṇamaha vihivasēṇa । saṁpayaṁ saṁpannō ghara-mā-
ṇusāṇaṁ sāmī ēsō । jaō gihatthāṇaṁ gihēsu mahilāō pamāṇaṁ, mahilāṇaṁ
puṇa pāṇa-piō jāmāugō ।
bhaṇiyaṁ ca-
tīyaha tinni piyārāī kali- kajjalu-siṁdūru ।
annai tinni piyārāhaṁ duhu jamvāi u tūru ॥
'
imaṁ ca aṇuciyaṁ na caēmi dahuṁ, varaṁ dhūyāē vi vēhavvaṁ ti ciṁtaṁtēṇa gaṁtr̥̄ṇa
bhaṇiō caṁḍālō । arē khaṁgilā ! na taē vāvāiō sō । tēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - kiṁ gayaṁ ?
daṁsēsu taṁ । saṁpayaṁ pivāvāissaṁ । sāgarapōēṇa vuttaṁ - jai ēvaṁ tā nayara - dēvayā-pūya-
ṇatthaṁ taṁ paṭṭhavissaṁ । taō gēhamāgaṁtr̥̄ṇa sāgarapōēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ vahu-varaṁ vaccaha
dēvakulācārō ti nagaradēviyaṁ puēḍaṁ । caliyaṁ taṁ vañcataṁ dihaṁ hahanividvēṇa samuddada-
ttēṇa । saṁpayaṁ atthamiē vāsarē sarē pariphuraṁtē timira - visarē ēvaṁ ciya cōrappasarē
nayara - parisarē aṇavasarō gaṁtuṁ bahū-varassa tti bhaṇatēṇa ṭhaviyaṁ haṭṭhē vahu-varaṁ । pūō-
vagaraṇaṁ vēttr̥ṇa gaō samuddadattō dēvayāyaṇaṁ, pavisaṁtō puvva-pavidvēṇa vāvāiō
khaṁgilēṇa । suyamiṇaṁ sāgarapōēṇa। sōya-sāgara - nimaggō ' hā dēva ! duvvārō tē

māṇī diṭṭhā kariṇā । dhāviō sō tassaṁmuhaṁ । addha-gahiyā sā tēṇa । pukkariyaṁ
pariyaṇēṇa - atthi kōi cauddasī - jāō jō amha sāmiṇi imāu kayaṁtāu vva
bhayaṁkarāō kariṇō rakkhēi । bhaviyavvayā - vasēṇa suyamiṇaṁ abhayasīhēṇa । karu-
ire dhāviūṇa 'arē durappa ! māyaṁgō si, na lajjasē itthī vahaṁ kuṇaṁtō tumaṁ ?”
ti vuttūṇa āhaō kulisa- kaḍhiṇa-muṭṭhiṇā pacchima bhāgē karī । muttūṇa rāya -kannaṁ

dēvaṇi । samāṇattō ya samaṁ tīē nivvisaō । visēsēṇa vr̥ttā dēiṇī - māṇēsu
appa - punnāī। tīē vr̥ttaṁ-jaṁ tumaṁ āṇavēsi । kilēsēṇa niggayāṇi nayarāō ।
miliyāṇi uttarā- vaha gāmiē satthē । diṭṭhō dēhaṇīē satthavaī । kahiō sē
vr̥ttaṁtō । bhaṇiō ya sa - bahu-māṇaṁ । jāva tāya-saṁtiyaṁ visayaṁ uttarāmō tāva
taē nēyavō ēsa mē bhattārō । paḍivannaṁ satthavāhēṇa । samappiō sē mahisagō ।
kamēṇa pattāṇi anna-rahaṁ । āvāsiō satthō aḍavīē । dēiṇī vi bhattāraṁ gi-
hiūṇa ṭhiyā tayāsannē । bhūyasāyā-pīḍhē kaō tīē taru-pallavēhiṁ sattharō । bhu-
bannō tattha ēsō । samāgayā sē niddā । dēiṇī vi sīsaṁ sē kurumālatī ciṭṭhā ।
iō ya jā puvvaṁ kumāra- māyā maṁgalā dēvī kurucaṁda-maraṇē mayā samāṇī tasē
vaṁtarī samuppannā । tīē diṭṭhō rāyahaṁsō, paccabhinnāō ya । taō divva-sattīē

mauḍō gauḍa-vaī tujjha rucai kimēsō ? |

1
saṁpayaṁ damayaṁtī cēva tuha bhajjā maṁtī mittaṁ pāikō ya । ēsā sirīsa-ku-
suma - sūmāla - sarīrā sūra-kara-niyara - saṁtatta- rēṇu - kaṇa- duggamē maggē kahaṁ kamala-kō-
malēhiṁ calaṇēhiṁ caṁkamihi tti ? । tā nāha ! giraha rahē । aṇugivha amhē । dē-
vīē samaṁ samārōha ittha । ēvaṁ pahāṇēhiṁ patthiō patthiō rahamārūhiūṇa
damayaṁtīē saha nalō । pahāṇujjayaṁ va ēga-vathaṁ damayaṁti hūṇa bāha-bi-
du-du-guṇiya-hārāhiṁ rōiyaṁ nagara - nārīhiṁ । vaccaṁtēṇa nalēṇa nayari- majjhē diṭṭhō
hattha-paṁca-saya-ppamāṇō khaṁbhō । rajja-bhaṁsubbhavaṁ dukkhaṁ amuṇaṁtēṇēva kōugēṇa
kayalī - khaṁbhō vva karēṇa ukkhaō līlāē । ukkhāya-paḍirōva-rūvaṁ rāya vvayaṁ va
daṁsayaṁtēṇa puṇō vi ārōviō tatthēva । imaṁ daṭṭhūṇa jaṁpiyaṁ nāyarēhiṁ - ahō !
bala - sāliṇō vi nalassa rajja - bhaṁsō tti vicittō vihi-niōgō । pucvaṁ naya-
rujjāṇē kūbarēṇa saha kīlaṁtassa nalassa samāgaō divva-nāṇa- nayaṇō muṇī ।
kahiyaṁ tēṇa - bhāvī bharaha- dāhiṇaddha-sāmī nalō । sō ya cālaissai nayara-ma-
jjhaṭṭhiyaṁ hattha-paṁca-saya-pyamāṇaṁ thaṁbhaṁ । ēvaṁ ubhayaṁ pi miliyaṁ dihaṁ amhēhiṁ
niya - nayaṇēhiṁ । jaṁ puṇa nalē jīvaṁtē vi kōsalāē annō rāyā saṁjāō taṁ visaṁ-

tappabhāvaō natthi mē bhayaṁ । dēva-guru-dhamma-sarūvaṁ savittharaṁ kahiūṇa karāviō
jiṇa dhamma- paḍivantiṁ sattha- vāhō । tāvasā vi saṁpatta - khīra - pāṇakaṁ jiyaṁ va niya-
dhammaṁ niṁdaṁtā pavannā jiṇa-dhammaṁ । tattha sattha- vāhēṇa karāviyaṁ puraṁ । taṁ ca paṁca-
sayāī tāvasāṇaṁ ittha paḍibuḍāī ti 'tāvasapuraṁ' ti pasiddhaṁ । tattha nimmāviyaṁ
saṁtināha - paḍimā -maṇa-haraṁ jiṇa -haraṁ । savvē vi jiṇa dhamma-parā kālaṁ vōlaṁti ।
annayā nisīhē sēla - siharē uggamaṁta-ravi- pahā - pūra vva ujjōō diṭṭhō damayaṁ-
tīē । diṭṭhā ya uppayaṁta nivayaṁtā dēvā । tēsiṁ jaya-jayārāvēṇa jaggiyā jaṇā ।
tēhiṁ samaṁ samārūḍhā damayaṁtī pavvayaṁ । tattha siṁhakēsari sāhuṇō kayā kēvalu-
patti - mahimā amarēhiṁ । vaṁdiūṇa taṁ muṇiṁ purō nisaṇṇā savvē । iō ya tassa
kēvaliṇō gurū jasabhaddō nāma tatthāgaō । sō vi kēvaliṇaṁ namiūṇa nisannō ।
-

kayā kēvaliṇā asāra-saṁsāra - sarūva-parūvaṇa-parā dhamma- dēsaṇā । ētyaṁtarē tatthā-
gaō gayaṇamujjōyaṁtō dēvō । kēvaliṇaṁ namiūṇa bhaṇiyā tēṇa damayaṁtī - bhaddē !
ihēva tavōvaṇē kula-vaiṇō sīsō tivva-tava-caraṇa-tapparō kapparō nāma aha-
māsi । paṁcagga- sāhagō vi nāhinaṁdiō tāvasēhiṁ । taō tēsu pasarata - rōsō
patthiō annattha । nīraṁgha - timira - niruddhāē nisāē vañcatō nivaḍiō giri-
kaṁdarē | giri-daṁtagga- laggā bhaggā mē daṁtā । daṁta-bhaṁga- pīḍā-para-vasō tatthēva paḍi-
ō । ṭhiō satta-rattaṁ । tāvasēhiṁ dussuviṇassēva tassa vattāvi na kayā, kiṁ puṇa
paḍīyārō ? | visēsaō bhuyaṁgē va gēhāō niggaē tavōvaṇāō tammi tāvasāṇaṁ
suhaṁ saṁjāyaṁ । sōvi tāvasēsu visēsullasaṁta- rōsō mariūṇa tatthēva tāvasārannē
samupapannō pannagō | kayāi kaya-phaṇa- kaḍappō pahāviō ahaṁ tuha ḍasaṇatthaṁ ।
tumaē vi maṁ daṭṭhaṇa paḍhiō paramiṭṭi maṁtō । tēṇa mē kanna- gōyaraṁ gaēṇa ruḍā gaī ।
puṇō vi paviṭṭhō bilaṁ । annayā taē tāvasāṇaṁ kahijjaṁtaṁ dhammaṁ suṇēmi ।
jō kōha- māṇa- māyā - lōhāṇugaō karēi pāṇi- vahaṁ ।
sō para bhavaṁmi pāvai jīvō tikkhāī dukkhāī ॥
taō ciṁtiyaṁ maē - hā ! kahaṁ bhavissaṁ 2, jō jīva-vahēṇa caiva jīvāmi ।
imēya maē tāvasā kahiṁci diṭṭha-puvva tti ūhāpōhaṁ kurṇatassa mēṁ jāyaṁ jāi-
saraṇaṁ । saṁvēga - puvvaṁ puvva- dukkaḍāī garahaṁtēṇa kathaṁ maē aṇasaṇaṁ । mariūṇa sō'haṁ
sōhammē samuppannō kusumappahō nāma dēvō । tuha dhamma-vayaṇa-savaṇāō samuvaladdhaṁ
surattaṇaṁ ti uvagāriṇi tumaṁ dahumāgaō'haṁ । tā dhamma- puttō ahaṁ tē । bhaṇiyā
ya tēṇa tāvasā - khamaha maha puvva - kōvācaraṇaṁ । pālēha puvva paḍivannaṁ sāva-
ya-vvayaṁ । taṁ ca sappa-kalēvaraṁ giri-kaṁdarāō kaḍḍiūṇa ōlaṁbiyaṁ pāyavē । bhaṇiyaṁ
ca - jō kōi kōvaṁ karējja sō kapparō vva sappō para bhavē havējjanti । taō
saṁvigga- cittēṇa kulavaiṇā bhaṇiō kēvalī - bhayavaṁ ! dēhi mē dikkhaṁ । kēva-
liṇā vr̥ttaṁ - ēsa jasabhadda-gurū dikkhissai tumaṁ । puṇō vi jaṁpiyaṁ kulavaṇā-
kahaṁ taē paḍivannā dikkhā ? । kēvaliṇā kahiyaṁ - kōsalāē nayarīē kūbarassa
naṁdaṇō ahaṁ । bhaṁgā-nayarī - sāmiṇā kēsariṇā dinnā mē baṁdhumaī nāma niya-dhūyā ।
jaṇayāēsēṇa gaṁtūṇa pariṇīyā sā maē । tīē saha niyattaṁtēṇa diṭṭhō maggē
samōsariō ēsa āyariō । vaṁdiō parama bhattīē suyā savaṇāmaya-sāraṇī
tassa dēkhaṇā । pucchiō ya - bhayavaṁ ! kinttiyaṁ mē jīciyaṁ ? | dinōvaōgēṇa

kumārapālapratibōdhē
bhaṇiyaṁ - bhayavaṁ ! thēva jīviō'haṁ kiṁ karēmi saṁpayaṁ ? | saṁpattamaṇukaṁpēṇa
guruṇā vr̥ttaṁ - vaccha ! mā gaccha khēyaṁ । paḍivajja pavvajjaṁ । jaō ēga- divasaṁ pi
ēsā saggāpavaggakāraṇaṁ । taō'haṁ pavannō dikkhaṁ । guru-niōgēṇa āgaō
ēttha । sukkajhāṇānalēṇa daḍa- kammiṁdhaṇō pattō kēvalaṁ । ēvaṁ kahiūṇa kaya-jōga-
nirōhō svaviya-bhavōvaggāhi-kammō siṁhakēsarī gaō mōkkhaṁ । kaō kēvali -
sarīrassa surēhiṁ sakkārō । paḍivannā kula-vaiṇā jasabhadda sūri-pāsē pavvajjā ।
damayaṁtīē bhaṇiō sūrī - mamāvi dēhi dikkhaṁ । sūriṇā bhaṇiyaṁ - bhaddē !
bhuttavvā taē nalēṇa saha bhōgā । aō nārihasi tumaṁ dikkhaṁ । pahāē pavva-
yāō uttariūṇa sūrī gaō tāvasapuraṁ । ēvaṁ dhamma - pasattā maliṇa- gattā satta-
saṁvaccharāī ṭhiyā giriguhāē damayaṁtī । annayā āyanniyaṁ tīē jahā - dama-
yaṁti ! diṭṭhō maē amuga-ppaēsē tuha para tti pahiya vayaṇaṁ । taō samuppannapari-
ōsā niggayā guhāō sā । pahāviyā vayaṇāṇusārēṇa । gayā dūraṁ । paḍiyā
arannē । nalaṁ apicchaṁtī rōviḍaṁ pavattā । hā ! kiṁ karēmi ? kattha vā jāmi ?
tti vilavaṁtī taṁ cēva giri-guhaṁ gaṁtumāraḍā । diṭṭhā pasāriya muhīē bhakkhissā-
mitti bhaṇaṁtīē rakkhasīē । tīē vi na sakkiyā sīla - ppabhāvaō bhakkhi ।
suviṇa - diṭṭha vva tirōhiyā rakkhasī । aggaō gacchaṁtīē tīē diṭṭhā nijjalā
naī । pivāsa-piḍiyāē pahi- pahārēṇa sīla-ppabhāvaō uppāiyaṁ tattha pāṇiyaṁ ।
pāūṇa taṁ patthiyā puraō । parissaṁtā vīsaṁtā naggōha - taru-talē । diṭṭhā sattha-
purisēhiṁ । bhaṇiyā ya-bhaddē ! kā tumaṁ dēvi vva dīsasi ? । tīē vr̥ttaṁ-
māṇusī ahaṁ sattha - paribhaṭṭhā'rannē saṁcarāmi । daṁsēhi mē tāvasapura-maggaṁ । tēhiṁ
vr̥ttaṁ - amhē pāṇiyāṇayaṇatthaṁ itthāgayā । attha-giri-matthaya-tthē akkē na sakēmō
tē maggaṁ daṁsiuṁ । jai puṇa amhēhiṁ saha āgacchasi tā satthēṇa samaṁ tumaṁ kiṁ
pi paṭṭaṇaṁ parāṇēmō । gayā sā tēhiṁ saha satthē । tattha dahūṇa dhaṇadēva-sattha- vāhēṇa
pucchiyā- kāsi tumaṁ ? । tīē vuttaṁ - vaṇiya- puttī ahaṁ pii-haraṁ patthiyā
arannē pattā paricattā bhattaṇā । baṁdhavēhiṁ va tuha purisēhiṁ sahāgayā । sattha-
vāhēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - ahaṁ acalapuraṁ gacchissaṁ tā tumaṁ pi āgaccha vacchē ! । pupphaṁ
va payattēṇa naissaṁ tumaṁ । taō ārōviyā pahāṇa - vāhaṇaṁ sā । patthiō sattha-
vāhō । āvāsiō viyasiya- duma- kusuma samullasiya-parāgapuṁjē giri- nikuṁjē ।
nisāē satthiēṇa paḍhijjatō paṁca-namōkkārō suō damayaṁtīē । tīē vuttō
satthavāhō-jō namukkāraṁ paḍhai sō sāvaō sāhammiō mē, taṁ daṭṭumicchāmi ।
।

takkarassa baṁdhā । viralīhūā talārā । imaṁ vr̥ttaṁtaṁ sōūṇa samāgaō tattha rāyā

vinnattaṁ - dēva ! dyā -para-vasa- maṇāē maē ēvaṁ kayaṁ tā khamiyavō mē imō
avarāhō । jaō duṭṭha-rōgō vva imassa pīḍā saṁkaṁtā mē maṇē । taō mukkō
takkarō rannā । sō vi tumaṁ mē māya ti jaṁpatō paidiṇaṁ paṇamēi damayaṁti । annayā

65
nāma bahuō । kamēṇa pattō acalapurē riupannassa rannō pāsaṁ । pucchiō caṁda-
jasā - dēvīē - kusalaṁ mama bahiṇīē puṣpadaṁtīē ? । baḍuēṇa vr̥ttaṁ -nicaṁ pi
kusalaṁ dēvīē । kiṁtu nala-damayaṁtī - rajja - bhaṁsa-savaṇāō saṁjāō dēvīē mahaṁtō
citta-saṁtāvō । caṁdajasāē buttaṁ - kiṁ bhaṇisi ? tti । bahuēṇa kahiō mūlāō
nala- jūya-vr̥ttaṁtō । taō caṁdajasaṁ ruyaṁtiṁ da parunnō rāya - lōō । savvaṁ sōya-
nivbharaṁ picchiūṇa chuhā- pīḍiō baḍuō gaō dāṇa-sālaṁ । niviṭṭō tattha
bhōyaṇatthaṁ । dāṇāhigāriṇi damayaṁtiṁ uvalakkhiūṇa samuppanna pariōsō paṇaō
sō । dēvi ! gimhē vīruhāē vva kā ēsā tē apasatthā avasthā ? diṭṭhiyā
divāsi jīvaṁtī | saṁpayaṁ kusalaṁ savvēsiṁ । ēvaṁ jaṁpiūṇa vīsariya chuhā- dukkhō
gaō caṁdajasā - samīvaṁ । bhaṇiyamaṇēṇa - vaḍāvijjasi, atthi tē dāṇasālāē
damayaṁtī । taṁ sōūṇa āgayā tattha caṁdajasā । tīē āliṁgiyā gāḍhaṁ damayaṁtī ।
bhaṇiyaṁ ca - dhiddhī maṁ jīē iyara - jaṇa - vilakkhaṇēhiṁ sāmuddiya-lakkhaṇēhiṁ
akkhiyāvi nōvalakkhiyā tumaṁ । vacchē ! vacchalāvi ahaṁ attāṇaṁ gōviūṇa
kiṁ vaṁciyā tumaē ? । kā vā tē lajjā mamaṁtiē ? । kahēhi kiṁ tumaē mukkō-
nalō ? nalēṇa vā mukkāsi ? | nūṇaṁ nalēṇa mukkā tumaṁ । tumaṁ pi jai vasaṇa-vaḍiyaṁ
paraṁ pariccayasi tā dhuvaṁ ravī avara - disāē uggamējjā । hā nala ! na lajjasē
guṇa-saṁcayaṁ cayaṁtō ēyaṁ ? kiṁ tē kulōciyamiṇaṁ ? । giṇhāmi tē dukkhaṁ ।
kijjāmi uyāraṇaṁ । khamēsu mē avarāhaṁ jaṁ nōvalakkhiyāsi । kattha vā phuriya-
kaṁti - nilaō tē bhāla-tilaō । taō niya-niḍīvaṇēṇa caṁdajasāē parāmu
bhāla - vahaṁ damayaṁtīē ।
akkō vva mēha-mukkō suvanna-piṁḍō vva anala - uttinnō ।
damayaṁtīē bhālē tilaō tō phuriumāraḍō ॥
aha dēvayāi paḍima vva ṇhāviyā niya-karēhiṁ dēvīē ।
pavaraṁsuyāi parihāviūṇa nīyā niva-samīvē ॥
caṁdajasā damayaṁtī ya dōvi rannō sahāi uvaviṭṭhā ।
taṁmi samayaṁmi sūrō bhuvaṇa-paīvō gaō atthaṁ ॥
timirēṇa kajjalēṇa va bhāyaṇaṁ gayaṇa-maṁḍalaṁ bhariyaṁ ।
tahavi na rāya - sahāē viyaṁbhiō timira - lēsō vi ॥
tō rannā vāgariyaṁ atthamiō naṇu ravī na iha dīvō ।
atthi na vā jalaṇō tā kisēsa ēvaṁ vihujāō ? |

[ prathamaḥ
taō dēvīē daṁsiō sahajō pahā - puṁja nilaō damayaṁtīē bhāla-tilaō ।
kōugēṇa rannā niya-karēṇa pihiō । taō giri-guha vva timira - nivbharā jāyā
rāya -sahā । ōsāriūṇa pāṇiṁ pucchiyā rannā rajja-bhaṁsāi-vattaṁ । ōṇaya-muhīē
ruyaṁtīē tīē kahiyā savvāvi sā । rannāvi niya-uttarijēṇa nayaṇāī parā -

taraṇi-kara- ṇi[kara]tēya- ppasarēṇa amarēṇa parisāē āgaṁtr̥̄ṇa kayaṁjaliṇā bhaṇiyā

paramēṭṭhiī- maṁtaṁ sumaraṁtō puvva-pāvāī garahaṁtō gaō paṁcattaṁ । saṁjāō pahā - pasara-bhā-
surō surō । avahiṇā muṇiya- puvva-bhavō jīviya- rakkhaṇēṇa pavvajjā-paḍivajā-

kōḍīō varisiūṇa tirōhiō dēvō । ēvaṁ dēvēṇa daṁsiyaṁ sukaya-phalaṁ paccakkhaṁ
pikkhatō pavannō rijvannō jiṇadhammē । samaē vinnattō bahuēṇa ēsō - dēva !

vantrēṇa rannā visajjiyā cauraṁga-bala- kaliyā caliyā damayaṁtī । taṁ āgacchaṁtiṁ
sōūna siṇēha taṁtu- saṁdāṇiō niggaō pupphadaṁtīē samaṁ saṁmuhō bhīma-bhūvaī ।
jaṇaṇi-jaṇaē hūṇa tuṭṭha-cittā muttr̥ṇa vāhaṇaṁ nivaḍiyā pāēsu tēsiṁ damayaṁtī ।
tāṇa ghaṇukaṁṭhāṇaṁ cirāō miliyāṇa nayaṇa-nīrēṇa ।
nivaḍatēṇa samaṁtā mahīyalē kaddamaṁ jāyaṁ ॥
jauṇa vva jaṇhu-kannaṁ jaṇaṇi āliṁgiūṇa damayaṁtī ।
laggūṇa jaṇaṇi-kaṁṭhē vimukka-kaṁṭhē ciraṁ ruyai ॥
tō vayaṇa-paṁkayāī jalēṇa pakkhāliūṇa vimalēṇa ।
akhilaṁ pi sukkha- dukkhaṁ parōpparaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ tēhiṁ ॥
aha bhaṇai puṣpadaṁtī aṁkaṁ ārōviūṇa damayaṁtiṁ ।
divāsi jaṁ jiyaṁtī taṁ sukayaṁ jaggaē amha ॥
amha gharē acchaṁtī suhēṇa picchihisi niya-paī vacchē ! |
cirakālāu vi pāva bhaddāī jaṇō hi jīvaṁtō ॥

taṁ sōyaṁ saṁpattō pārijjai jō na kahiuṁ pi ॥
damayaṁtī- piu-pāsē dahivanna-nivēṇa annayā dūō ।

sūrapāgaṁ rasavaī । taṁ sōūṇa damayaṁtīē jaṁpiō piyā - tāya ! paṇihiṁ pēsiūṇa
jāṇāhi, kērisō sūvayārō । nalaṁ viṇā na yāṇai sūrapāyaṁ rasavaī । jai puṇa
gōviyappā nalō cēva havijja ēsō ।

dahivantrēṇa — ahilasaṇīyā mē damayaṁtī, paraṁ dūra-dēsē sā, paccūsē paṁcamī, na tīrai
tattha gaṁtuṁ, tā kiṁ karēmi tti mīṇō vva thōya-jalē pattō araī dahivannō । khujjēṇa
ciṁtiyaṁ damayaṁtī mahāsaī na purisaṁtaramicchai, icchēja vā tahāvi maha vijja-

mamāvi pasaṁgēṇa daṁsaṇaṁ hōi । khujjēṇa vr̥ttō dahivannō - kiṁ tammasi tumaṁ ? kahēhi
kāraṇaṁ । nahi akahiya - rōgassa rōgiṇō cigicchā kīrai । rannā vuttaṁ - saṁpannō
kaya- surapura - pavēsa- maṁgalō nalō, puṇō vi damayaṁtī saṁpayaṁ sayaṁvaraṁ karissaha,
atthi mē damayaṁtīē ahilāsō, dūrē vidanbhā, chaccēva paharā aṁtarē, bahuya-divasēhiṁ

mi nivvuī । khujēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - jacca turaya-juttaṁ appēhi mē rahaṁ, jēṇa paccūsē tattha
tumaṁ nēmi । na sāmanna - purisō ēsō kiṁtu khēyarō surō vatti ciṁtiūṇa samappiō
jahutta rahō rannā । taṁ kāūṇa paguṇaṁ bhaṇiō nalēṇa dahivannō-ārōha rahē ।
rāyā thaiyāittō chattadharō dunni cāmarakarā ya ।
ārūḍhā taṁmi rahē paṁca imē, khujjaō chaṭṭaō ||
taṁ bilaṁ ca karaṁḍaṁ ca kaḍiyaḍē baṁdhiūṇa vatthēṇa ।
kaya-dēva-guru-sumaraṇō turaṁgamē khēḍaē khujō ॥

aha dahivannassa paḍō paḍiō raha vēga-pavaṇa-uhuō ।
tēṇa pariōsa vasaō nalassa ōyāraṇaṁ va kaō ॥
dahivantrēṇa kahiyamēyaṁ khujjassa, hasiūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ khujjēṇa — kattha
patthiva ! atthi tē paḍō ? paḍa- paḍaṇāō paṁcavīsaṁ jōyaṇāī āgaō rahō ।
kiṁca majjhimā imē turayā, jai puṇa uttamā havēja, tā ittiēṇa kālēṇa cōi-
jamāṇā vara- paṁcāsa - jōyaṇāī rahō āgacchējjā । dahivantrēṇa akkha-rukkhaṁ
pikkhiūṇa akkhiyaṁ - ittha akkhē jantiyāī phalāī cihuṁti agaṇaṁtō vi
tēsiṁ saṁkhaṁ jāṇēmi ahaṁ, niyattaṁtō tē kōugaṁ daṁsissaṁ । khujjaēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ-
maē sārahiṁmi mā bōhēsu kālakkhēvāō । ēga-muṭṭhi- ppahārēṇa pāḍēmi savvāī
phalāī tuha puraō । rannā vuttaṁ - pēccha acchēraṁ, pāḍēhi tumaṁ, ciṭṭhati aṭṭhārasa-
sahassāī phalāṇaṁ । taō muṭṭhi-ghāēṇa pāḍiyāiṁ tāiṁ khujjēṇa । gaṇiyāī dahi-
vantrēṇa, jāva tittiyāiṁ cēva । dinnā dahivannassa patthiēṇa turaya- hiyaya-vijjā
khujjēṇa । gahiyā dahivannāō phala-saṁkhā vijjā । pahāē kuṁḍiṇapurāsannē pattō
rahō viyasiya- vayaṇa-kamalō saṁpannō dahivannō । ētyaṁtarē rayaṇī - virāmē daṁmayatīē
diṭṭō suviṇaō । kahiō vihi-putravaṁ piuṇō । jahā - diṭṭhā maē nivvui-dēvī
āṇēyaṁtī ittha gayaṇē kōsalujāṇaṁ । dēvī - vayaṇēṇa puppha-phala- kaliyaṁ ārūḍhā
ahaṁ cūya- pāyavaṁ । mama hatthē samappiyaṁ pahāṇa- paramaṁ dēvīē । paḍiō puvvārūḍhō
jhati vihaṁgamō । bhīmēṇa vr̥ttaṁ-putti ! sōhaṇō suviṇō । nivvui-dēvī tē
punna - rāsī - jaggaō । kōsalujāṇaṁ kōsalā - rajja-lābha - karaṁ । māyaṁdārōhaṇaṁ nala-

73
tuha daṁsaṇatthamāgaō nalō, pattō aujjhāē parisarē । samāgayaṁ suṇiūṇa nalaṁ
analāliṁgiō vva jāō mahaṁta saṁtāva-kavaliya- kalēvarō kūbarō ।
vr̥ttō nalēṇa ēsō dūya-muhēṇaṁ - maē samaṁ jujjha ।
hōu maha tujjha lacchī mah lacchī vā havaha tujjha ॥
aha kūbarēṇa puṇaravi pāraḍaṁ jujjha bhīruṇā jūyaṁ ।
sō sukayamaṁsalēṇaṁ nalēṇa hārāviō savvaṁ ॥
kūrō vi kūbarō sō mama lahu-baṁdhu tti kōva - rahiēṇa ।
guṇa-nimmalēṇa vihiō nalēṇa puttaṁ vca juvarāō ॥
lahiūṇa niyaṁ rajjaṁ damayaṁtī-saṁjuō nalō rāyā ।
ukkaṁṭhiō narmasaha aujjha-nayarī - jiṇaharāī ॥
kaya- viviha- pāhuḍēhiṁ nalō nariṁdēhiṁ namiya-paya-kamalō ।
kuṇai bharahaḍa - rajjaṁ varisa - sahassāī bahuyāī ॥
anna dinē saggāō siha-surō tēya bhāsurō pattō ।
visaya- suha- sēvaṇāraṁbha-vinbhalaṁ bhaṇēi nalamēvaṁ ॥
rāgāi-takkarēhiṁ luṁṭijjaṁtaṁ vivēya- savvassaṁ ।
jō appaṇō vi rakkhasi na tumaṁ sō hōsi purisō kiṁ ? ॥
pavvajjā - samayaṁ tē kahissamiti jaṁpiyaṁ maē puvvaṁ ।
tā saṁpai māṇusa - jamma duma-phalaṁ saṁjamaṁ ginha ॥
iya jaṁpiūṇa dēvō tirōhiō, aha samāgaō tattha ।
jiṇabhaddō nāma gurū vimalāvahināṇa - rayaṇa-nihī ॥
tō gaṁtuṁ damayaṁtī - sahiēṇa nalēṇa vaṁdiō ēsō ।
taha uvavisiuṁ puraō paṁjaliṇā pucchiō ēvaṁ ॥
kiṁ puvva bhavē bhayavaṁ ! amhēhiṁ kayaṁ jamērisaṁ rajjaṁ ।
laḍūṇa hāriyaṁ aha puṇō vi laddhaṁ samaggaṁ pi ॥
guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ -suṇa sōma ! atthi ētthēva jaṁbudīvaṁmi ।
bhārahavāsē aṭṭhāvayassa giriṇō samīvaṁmi ॥
nicaṁ adi para cakka - saṁgaraṁ asthi saṁgaraṁ nagaraṁ ।
tatthāsi vihiya - disi - ramaṇi - kammaṇō mammaṇō rāyā ॥
tassa vīramaī dēvī । kayāi tīē saha pāraddhi-patriṇa patdhivēṇa nagara-
bāhiṁ satthēṇa saha gacchaṁtō dhammō vva muttimaṁtō pasaṁtō saṁtōsa-ppamuha-guṇavi-

[ prathamaḥ
siṭṭhō diṭṭhō muṇī | migayā - mahūsava - vigdha paḍaṇō asauṇō mē ēsō ti citi-
tēṇa tēṇa kuṁjarō vva jūhāō satthāō dhariō sō । niyattiūṇa nīō niya-
gēhūṁ । bārasa ghaḍiāō jāva viḍaṁbiō । pacchā pucchiō samucchaliya-kārunnēṇa
rannā dēvīē ya—kattō tumaṁ āgaō, kattha vā patthiōsi ? । muṇiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ-
rōhīḍayapurāō aṭṭhāvaya-pavvayāvayaṁsa- paḍibiṁbāṇaṁ jiṇabiṁbāṇaṁ vaṁdaṇatthaṁ satthēṇa
saha patthiō'haṁ । ēvaṁ muṇi vayaṇa - maṁta-savaṇēṇa visaṁ va visaharāṇaṁ viyaliō
tēsiṁ kōvō । bhaddaga-bhāvaṁ nāūṇa bhuṇiṇā kahiō jīva dayā- pahāṇō dhammō ।
ājammāō dhammakkharēhiṁ aviddha-kannāṇa tāṇa jāō kiṁci dhamma- pariṇāmō ।
paḍilāhiō tēhi sāhū bhatta - pāṇāiṇā । dhariō kēttiaṁ pi kālaṁ । ōsahaṁ
va rōgīṇa tēsiṁ dhamma-vinnāṇaṁ dāūṇa tēhiṁ visajjiō gaō muṇī aṭṭhāvayaṁ ।
ēvaṁ sāhu-saṁsaggaō paribuddhēhiṁ tēhiṁ daviṇaṁ va kivaṇēhiṁ jattaō pāliyaṁ
sāvagattaṇaṁ । annayā vīramaī dhammathirī- karaṇatthaṁ sāsaṇa- dēvayāē nīyā aṭṭhā-
vaya - pavvayaṁ । tattha niya-niya vanna - ppamāṇa - juttāō viviharayaṇa- pajjuttāō
surāsura - viṇimmiya-mahimāō arihaṁta - paḍimāō pēcchiūṇa paramaṁ pariō-
samāvannā । vaṁdiūṇa āgayā taō niyanayaraṁ । sā ya vīramaī mahaṁtaṁ tittha-
mēyaṁ maē vaṁdiyaṁ tisaddhāē jiṇaṁ jiṇaṁ paḍuca vīsaṁ vīsaṁ āyaṁbilāī karēi ।
uvari nivēsiya- māṇika maṇaharē kaṇaga-nimmiē tilaē ।
cauvīsaṁ jiṇapaḍimāō juggē kāravai vīramaī ॥
anna- diṇē ahāvaya - girimmi gaṁtuṁ imā saparivārā ।
pūjaṁ kuṇai jiṇāṇaṁ pahavaṇa- vilēvaṇa-bali-ppamuhaṁ ॥
jiṇa-paḍimāṇa nilāḍēsu tāī tilayāī ṭhavai bhattīē ।
tappunna- pāyavarasa va jāī virāyaṁti kusumāī ॥
cāraṇa-samaṇāiṇaṁ titthē tatthāgayāṇa dāūṇa ।
dāṇaṁ jahārihaṁ sā iya kuṇai tavassa ujjavaṇaṁ ॥
kaya- kicaṁ maṇuya bhavaṁ sahalaṁ vihavaṁ kayatthamavi jīyaṁ ।
mannaṁtī vīramaī puṇō vi pattā niyaṁ nayaraṁ ॥
iya bhinna- sarīrāṇa vi tēsiṁ dōnhaṁ abhinna-cittāṇaṁ ।
jiṇadhamma-kaya-maṇāṇaṁ bahuō kālō akaṁtō ॥
jīvāṇa maraṇa dhamma- taṇēṇa samaē samāhi-maraṇēṇa ।
mariūṇa mammaṇa- nivō pattō sōhamma-suralōyaṁ ॥

tō calasu nayara - majjhē majjha imaṁ mahisamāruhiuṁ ॥

tō dhannaēṇa sahiō sāhū saṇiyaṁ gaō nayaraṁ ॥

=== Kumara1output-76-to-76.json ==========================
76
kumārapālapratibōdhē
satta varisāim̐ taṁ pāliūṇa dhannō maō saha piyāē ।
juyalattaṇēṇa jāō hēmavaē vāsaṇā-vasaō ॥
tattō mariḍaṁ jāō sō sōhammaṁmi khīraḍiṁḍirō ।
dēvō sā uṇa dēvī tanbhajjā khīraḍiṁḍirā ॥
caviūṇa dhannaō sō sōhammāō tumaṁ nalō jāō ।
naranāha ! dhūsari ciya imā piyā tujjha damayaṁtī ॥
jaṁ puvva-bhavē dinaṁ muṇi-dāṇaṁ sāvagattaṇaṁ ca kathaṁ ।
tassa phalēṇa surūvaṁ rajjaṁ ca taē imaṁ pattaṁ ॥
ēsā vi hu damayaṁtī taddhamma-phalēṇa tuha piyā jāyā ।
kēṇa vi agaṁjiyappā visēsa-tava-tilaya- dāṇēhiṁ ॥
jaṁ puṇa vārasa ghaḍiā viḍaṁbaṇā tassa sāhuṇō vihiyā ।
tumhaṁ raja-bhaṁsō bārasa- varisāim̐ taṁ jāō ॥
iya guru- vayaṇaṁ suṇiuṁ saṁvēgamuvāgaō nalō rāyā ।
puttaṁ pukkhalanāmaṁ guṇābhirāmaṁ ṭhavai rajjē ||
damayaṁtī ēm̐ samēō gahiuṁ dikkhaṁ nalō guru- samīvē ।
paḍhai suyaṁ kuṇai tavaṁ parīsahē dussahē sahai ॥
aha kammassa vicittattaṇaō rāyassa dujjayattaṇaō ।
bhōgatthaṁ damayaṁtīi kuṇai cittaṁ nalō sāhū ॥
tattō guruhiṁ cattō piuṇā paḍibōhiō ya āgaṁtuṁ ।
paripāliḍaṁ asakkō vayaṁ imō aṇasaṇaṁ kuṇai ॥
damayaṁtīē vi kayaṁ nalāṇurattāi taṁ taō mariuṁ ।
jāō nalō kubērō damayaṁtī tassa puṇa bhajjā ॥
kiṁci vaya- virāhaṇaō nīya-surattaṁ imēhiṁ saṁpattaṁ ।

jaṁtamaō hatthī kāriō । nīō kōsaṁbī - samāsannē rannē । ṭhāviyaṁ tassa adūrā-

=== Kumara1output-82-to-82.json ==========================
82
kumārapāla pratibōdhē
[ prathamaḥ
yaṇāī gaō udyaṇō । ēvaṁ sēsāō vi tinni muttadhaḍiyāō bhaggāō ।
kōsaṁbiṁ paviṭṭhō udyaṇō । annayā ujjēṇīyē upāyaggī uḍiō kahiṁ pi nōva-
samai । rannā abhaō pucchiō । sō bhaṇai - ' viṣasya viṣamauṣadham, agnēra-
nirēva ।' tō aggīō annō aggīkaō । tēṇa sō āhaō aggī, taō
thakkō jalaṁtō । taiō rannā dinnō barō । ēsō vi ṭhāviō abharaṇa rannō pāsē ।
annayā ujjēṇīē asivaṁ udyadviyaṁ । abhaō pucchiō uvasamōvāyaṁ, bhaṇai-
abhitariyāē atthāṇīē dēvīō vibhūsiyāō itu jā tumhēhiṁ rāyālaṁkāra-
bhūsiēhiṁ diṭṭhīē jigaha taṁ mē kahijjahaṁ । tahēva kathaṁ । rāyā palōēi, savvāō
hāmuhīō ṭhāyaṁti । sivāē rāyā jiō । kahiaṁ abhayassa । abhaō
bhai - ratiṁ avasaṇā ēsā kūrabaliṁ karēu । jaṁ bhūyaṁ uṭṭhaha tassa muddē kūraṁ
chuhau । tava kathaṁ । liē caukkē ahālaē ya jāhē dēvayā sivārūvēṇa vāsara,
tāhē kūraṁ tassa muddē chuhara, bhaṇai ya-- ahaṁ sivā gōpālaga - pālaga-māyatti ।
ēvaṁ savvāṇi vinijjiyāṇi bhūyāṇi । jāyā purīi saṁtī । dēi cautthaṁ varaṁ
nivō tassa | ciṁta abhayakumārō, ciṭṭhissaṁ kēciraṁ ittha, rāyagihaṁ vaccāmi
tti । tō bhaṇai - dēva ! dēhi majjha varaṁ । rannā vuttaṁ - maggasu । aha abhaō
jaṁpaē ēvaṁ-
nalagiri-hatthihiṁmiṁ ṭhitaī sivadēvihi ucchaṁgi ।
aggibhīru-raha- dāruhahi aggi dēhi maha aṁgi ॥
buḍīē attāṇaṁ visajjāvēi tti ciṁtiūṇa rannā sakkāra - puvvaṁ visajjiō
abhaō, bhaṇai - tumhēhiṁ chalēṇa aṇiō ahaṁ, maha puṇa painnaṁ suṇa-
karivi paī sahassakaru nagarīmajjhiṇa sāmi !
jai na raḍaṁtu taī harauṁ aggihiṁ pavisāmi ॥
taṁ bhajjaṁ cittūṇa gaō abhaō rāyagihaṁ, ṭhiō kaṁci kālaṁ । pacchā
caṁda- suṁdara - vayaṇāō kamala-dala- dīha - nayaṇāō vitthiṣṇa-thaṇa- kalasāō vivi
ha - viyārēsu aṇalasāō dō gaṇiyāō ghēttūṇa vaṇiya-vēsēṇa pattō ujjēṇiṁ ।
rāya-maggē givhaē āvāsaṁ । annayā diṭṭhāō pajjōēṇa gaṇiyāō । tāhi
visa-vilāsāhi diṭṭhīhiṁ nijjhāiō gaō nighāvāsaṁ । pēsaha dūī । tāhiṁ kuvi-
yāhi va dhāḍiūṇa dūī bhaṇiyaṁ, na hōi ēsa rāyā jō para mahilamahilasaiti ।
bīya-diṇē saṇiyaṁ ruṭṭhāō । taiya-diṇē bhaṇiyā dūī -sattamē divasē dēvaulē
dēvajattaṁ karissara amha bhāyā tattha rahō tti āgaccha । annayā bhāyā rakkhai ।

dhūmō vva citta kammaṁ jaṁ guṇa-gaṇamujjalaṁ pi maliṇēi ।
jaṁ dōsāṇa nivāsō vaṁmiya-vivaraṁ va bhuyagāṇaṁ ॥

pacchā pacchāyāvēṇa lahai sōyaṁ asōō vva ॥

jaṁ cavaṇa -
jamma nikkhamaṇa nāṇa-ṭhāṇaṁ ti sīyalajiṇassa |
bhadēhi vihiyasēvaṁ tamatthi bhaddilapuraṁ nayaraṁ ॥
tattha jasabhahō rāyā ।
ari-kāmiṇīṇa kuṁkuma-kacchūrī-kajjalāī aṁgēsu ।
jassa karavāla - dhārā jalēṇa sahasa tti ghōāī ||
[ prathamaḥ
tassa sammaō samaō vva bahuyattha-saṁgaō gaō vva pavattiya dāṇa-pasa-

jaō-
viviha-maṇi kaṇaya-bhūsaṇa- juyā vi juvaī viṇā avaccēṇa ।
na virāya vallirapallavā vi valli vva phalahīṇā ॥
lacchīē bhaṇiō sēṭṭhī - kiṁ tumaṁ visannō va dīsasi ? । tēṇa vr̥ttaṁ -jaṁ
tumaṁ niravacca tti taṁ maha mahaṁtō saṁtāvō । tīē bhaṇiyaṁ jai ēvaṁ tā annaṁ
pariṇēsu । tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ-piē ! na mē anna-bhajjāē avacēṇāvi maṇa- nivvuī ।

asthi, sā samatta - jaṇa-patthiyatthē payacchēi । tā tīē uvāiyaṁ karēsu । 'jutta-
mēyaṁ' ti bhaṇiūṇa gaō sēṭṭhī lacchīē samaṁ sīyalajiṇa bhavaṇaṁ । kappūrakuṁ-

=== Kumara1output-88-to-88.json ==========================
88
kumārapālapratibōdhē
pālaṁti na vēsāō niya-jīhāē vi paḍivannaṁ ॥
[ prathamaḥ
mayaṇāē aṇurattō bhaddō nāma vāṇiuttō । niḍaṇō tti taṁ na kāmaē
maghaṇā । sō parābhava-payaṁ appāṇaṁ mannatō atthatthī gaō asōyā - dēvīē
bhavaṇaṁ । aciūṇa taṁ niviṭṭō tīē puraō । paricatta- caugvihāhārō ṭhiō
aṭṭha ahōrattāī । aṭṭhama- rayaṇīē bhaṇiō dēvayāē - bhō ! kimēvaṁ ciṭṭhasi ? |
bhaddēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ - dēvī ! dhaṇatthī tumaṁ sēvēmi । dēvīē vr̥ttaṁ - natthi tē punnaṁ ।
tēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - jai mē ciṁtāmaṇī-payāṇēṇa pasāyaṁ karēsi tō uṭṭhēmi, annahā
ētthēva kimipuṁjō hōmi । muṇiya tannicchyāē dēvayāē dinō tassa ciṁtāmaṇī
kahiyaṁ ca - paṁca-paramiṭṭi - maṁta-saraṇa - puvvaṁ maggiō paidiṇaṁ paṁca-diṇāra - sadhāī
viyarissara ēsō tti tirōhiyā dēvī । sō vi ciṁtāmaṇī - māhappēṇa saṁpunna-ma-
gōrahō vilasaha । saghaṇō ti muṇiuṁ mayaṇāē pavēsiō niyadharaṁ । dēha
ēsō jaṁ maggiyaṁ । ciṁtiyaṁ mayaṇāē-nūrṇa imassa pariggahē asthi ciṁtā -
maṇī, annahā kahaṁ ērisī dāṇa- sattī, tā taṁ giṇhāmi । taō pahāṇōva-
viṭṭhassa tassa kuppāsaṁ khallayāō gahiō tīē ciṁtāmaṇī । puṇō kiṁpi maggi-
ēṇa nihāliyaṁ aṇēṇa khayaṁ । taṁ apēcchantēṇa pāraddhā gavēsaṇā । bhaṇiyaṁ
mayaṇāē - pajjattaṁ tuha dāṇēṇa । mā mē pariyaṇaṁ anbhakkhāṇēṇa dumihisi, tā
niggaccha gēhāō । bhaddēṇa ciṁtiyaṁ - nūṇaṁ imīē hariō cintāmaṇī, kaha
annahā siddha-kajjaṁ va niddakkhiṇaṁ jaṁpai, paraṁ kiṁ kirai adiṭṭha cōrō rāya ti
vilakkhacittō niggaō bhahō । cintiyaṁ asōēṇa-
na dayā na lōya-lajjā nākitti bhayaṁ na pāva - saṁkāya ।
attha- gahaṇattha-viraiya- viviha- kilēsāṇa vēsāṇa ||
ēvaṁ ṭhiō varisamēkaṁ asōō । jaṁpiyā aṇēṇa kuṭṭiṇī - muṇiyaṁ maē
vēsā - sarūvaṁ । nīō asōgō suṁdara - samīvē tīē । bhaṇiō suṁdarō-jāṇā-
viō maē tuha suō vēsā-sarūvaṁ, kahaṁ pi na vaṁcijjai vēsāhiṁ । suṁdarēṇa diṣṇaṁ
paḍivannaṁ dōṇāra lakkhaṁ kuṭṭiṇīē । aikaṁtō kōi kālō । kayāi ciṁtiyaṁ
asōēṇa-
sōhai sisuttaṇēcciya na jubvaṇē juyamiṇaṁ maṇussassa ।
jaṇaṇi thaṇa-duddha-pāṇaṁ piu-lacchīē ya paribhōgō ॥
tā gaṁtr̥̄ṇa dēsaṁtaraṁ viḍhavēmi vihavaṁ, tōsēmi sayaṇa-gaṇaṁ, karēmi dēvaguru-
pūyaṁ, pūrēmi samagga-maggaṇa-maṇōrahē । taō jaṇaṇī - jaṇāyāṇunnāō dōṇāra -

dasa - lakkha mullaṁ bhaṁḍaṁ gahiūṇa gaō gayauraṁ nayaraṁ asōgō । pavattō tattha vavaha-
rijaṁ । diṭṭhō kāmalayāē gaṇiyāē । tā kahaṁ pi giṇhāmi imassa dhaṇaṁ ti ciṁti-
ūṇa palōiō vilāsa-pēsalāē diṭṭhīē, dhaṇa- gahaṇa - kayāvēsā vēsā ēsa ti
ciṁtiuṁ imiṇā bhaya - visa-visaṁṭhulēṇaṁ sigghaṁ vagdhi vva sā mukkā । tīē ya
diṭṭhi- dūī paṭṭaviḍaṁ vaṁciuṁ asakkāē pacchā taṁ āṇēuṁ paṭṭaviyā cēḍiyā dūī ।
tīē vi bhaṇiha - niuṇāē āṇiḍaṁ sakkiō na sō gēhaṁ ।
pacchā gayā sayaṁ ciya kāmalayā tassa āvāsē ॥
bhaṇiō imīē - jappabhii suhaya ! diṭṭhōsi amara kumarō vva ।
tappabhiī maha jāō kusumasarō tatta-lōha -sarō ॥
tā kāūṇa pasāyaṁ maha hiyayaṁ jaha alaṁkiyaṁ tumaē ।
taha majjha maṁdiraṁ pi hu niya-āgamaṇēṇa maṁḍēsu ॥
ēvaṁ bhaṇiō vi imō kāmalayāē gihē na saṁpattō ।
tā paidiṇamāḍhattā taṁ paṛa sā patthaṇaṁ kāuṁ ॥
paidiyaha- patthaṇāē jāō tā niṭhurō vi mauya-maṇō ।
jaṁ pattharō vi bhijjai niraṁtaraṁ nīra- pūrēṇa ॥
dhaṇamēva na dāyacvaṁ kō maha dōsō imīē giha- gamaṇē ।
iya ciṁtiuṁ asōō kāmalayāē gharaṁ pattō ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ imīē-
ajju vihāṇaḍaṁ ajju diṇu ajju suvāu pavattu ।
ajju galatthiu sayalu duhu jaṁ tuhuṁ maha ghari pattu ॥
iya cāḍu vayaṇa-saṁjaṇiya-saṁbhamō nicamēi taggēhē ।
sō taduvarōhaō cciya tāē saha kuṇai saṁbhōgaṁ ॥
vēsā - jaṇōcciyēhiṁ kavaḍōvāēhiṁ kiṁtu vivihēhiṁ ।
sō maggaō vi tīē maṇicchiyaṁ dēi nahu vittaṁ ॥

taō pāḍavēsiya-kuṭṭiṇīō mēliūṇa bhaṇiyā kāmalayā kuṭṭiṇīē -

vi vēsā - sarūvaṁ । tāhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ - jīvaṁta kavaḍāī kayāī kāmalaē ! tara,

[ prathamaḥ
tthāharaṇāī parihiūṇa asōga dinēṇa mahāvibhavēṇa tumaṁ aciyavvō । annahā
tuha aggaō aggī-sāhiyavvō । tā piyayama ! saṁpāḍēsu savvamēyaṁ । taṁ
sōūṇa asōgō ṭhiō tuhikkō । taō bhaṇiyaṁ kāmalayāē - nāha ! nāhaṁ
vallahā tē kiṁ tu tumaṁ dhaṇaṁ bahu mannēsi, tā kiṁ mē jīviēṇaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa
jakkhassa puraō rayāviyā caṁdaṇāgaru -kaṭṭa- niciyā ciyā । akaya-sōyassa
asōyassa paccakkhaṁ paviṭṭhā tattha sā । jālājāla - pallaviya - disimuhō pajjā-

sōgaṁ । kaya- kavaḍa - visēsāō vēsāō imāō kahavi na maraṁti । jaṇiya-ja-
laṇa-pavēsā vēsā ēsā na hōi phuḍaṁ । tā jaṁ imā maraṁtī uvēkkhiyā taṁ maē
kayaṁ na suhaṁ । cukkō ahaṁ abhaggō hā ! ērisa - ramaṇī - rayaṇassa । iya vilavaṁtō
jā kuṭṭiṇīṇa pāsaṁmi acchai asōgō kaya- purisa- vējja-rūvā tā annā kuṭṭiṇī
bhaṇai – kuṭṭha - bhagaṁdara - khaya- sāsa-kāsa- pamuhē harāmi rōgē'haṁ । maṁtōsahēhiṁ rubhēmi
thāvaraṁ jaṁgamaṁ ca visaṁ । rakēmi jaraka - rakasa - ḍāyaṇi bhūya-ggahāiṇō dōsē |

gēṇa - bhadda ! jai ēvaṁ tā jīvāvēsu mē hiyaya-vallahaṁ । vējjēṇa vr̥ttaṁ daṁsēsu

ālihiyaṁ maṁḍalaṁ । pāraḍō hōmō । sattama diṇē suraṁgāmaggēṇa āgayā kāma-

thēva - dihiṁ asōgō saṁjāō khīṇa-sayala-dhaṇō ॥
tō niḍaṇō ti muṇiḍaṁ tīē nissāriō niyagharāō ।
sō sāhā cukkō makkaḍō vva jāō vilaka-maṇō ॥
ciṁtēi imaṁ hā ! ēttiyaṁ pi mūḍhēṇa jāṇiyaṁ na maē ।

taṁ sō pavajjiḍaṁ gahiya - saṁjamō nēmināha - pāsaṁmi ।

hā ! pāvanihī hā ! duṭṭhaciṭṭhiō hā ! abhaggavaṁtō'haṁ ।

maṁ kō vi kōvaijjatti jāmi annattha purimimaṁ muttuṁ ।
iya ciṁtiūṇa vijaṇē varṇami dīvāyaṇō pattō ॥
dahūṇa taṁ kumārēhiṁ jaṁpiyaṁ majja - pāṇa- mattēhiṁ ।
niddaya-maṇō durappā sō dīvāyaṇarisī ēsō ॥
vāravaīē khaya-kāraō tti jō riṭṭhanēmiṇā kahiō ।
tā nivbharaṁ haṇāmō nikkāraṇavēriyaṁ ēyaṁ ॥
tō kuviēhiṁ taha tāhiṁ tāḍiō muṭṭhi-lēhu-laṭṭhīhiṁ ।
jaha nīharaṁta - ruhirō paḍiō dharaṇīyalē ēsō ॥

mahārāya - kaṇha ! hā rāma ! hā putta ! hā vaccha ! hā nāha ! parittāyahi pari-
tāyahi ti sayalagharēsu uṭṭhiyā karuṇa-samullāvā । taō baladēva kaṇhēhiṁ turiya-
turiyaṁ gōura- hāraṁ jāva nīyā dōvi rahā, iṁdakīlēṇaṁ ca tē ruḍā । taō tami-
dakīlaṁ pāēṇa baladēvō jāva cunnēi tāva jalaṇēṇaṁ taṁ duvāraṁ jālāhiṁ jaliu -
māḍhattaṁ । ētyaṁtarē dīvāyaṇēṇa saṁlattaṁ - bhō ! maē putrvamēva bhaṇiyaṁ jahā tunbhē
duvē muttūṇa annassa mukkhō natthi tti mē pannā । taō vāsudēvēṇa pāyatalāhayaṁ
kavāḍamēkaṁ dharaṇī-yalē nivāḍiyaṁ, viiyaṁ ca jālāvalī - palittaṁ rāmēṇa । taō
tē vasudēva- rōhiṇī - dēvahiṁ bhaṇiyā-puttayā ! tubhēhiṁ jīvamāṇēhiṁ jāyavaku-
lassa puṇō visamunnaī bhavissai tā turiya-turiyaṁ vacchayā ! nigacchaha tti ।
taō dīvāyaṇassa māyā-piūṇaṁ ca vayaṇēṇa sakaruṇaṁ ruyaṁtā niggayā kaṇha-bala-
dēvā । bāhiṁ bhaggujjāṇē ṭhiyā ujjhamāṇaṁ vāravaī picchaṁti । dīvāyaṇēṇa vi
sayalāī duvārāī dēva- sattīē ḍhakkiūṇa visēsēṇa pajjāliyā nayarī । ētyaṁtarē
rāmassa pāṇa-vallahō puttō maṇujjō kujjavāraō nāma bālakumārō carama- dēha dharō
sō niyaya-bhavattamaṁgē samāruhiūṇa bhaṇai - bhō ! bhō ! suṇaṁtu samāsanna-
dēvaya-jaṇā ! ariṭṭhanēmi - sāmiṇō ahaṁ sissō । samaṇō daṁtō savva-bhūya - dayā-
varō mōkkhaṁ gamissami tti sāmiṇā samāiṭṭhō caramadēhō । taṁ jai saccaṁ bhaya-
vaō vayaṇaṁ tā kimēyaṁ ? ti bhaṇiē uvaḍiyā jaṁbhagā dēvā । tēhi ukkhittō
jalaṁta - jalaṇāō । nīō palhavadēsaṁ nēmi pāsē ।
aha pāyavōvagamaṇaṁ samabhāvēṇaṁ aṇuṭṭhiyaṁ laiyā |
kaṇhassa mahīvaiṇō sōlasa dēvī - sahassēhiṁ ॥
taha pāyavōvagamaṇaṁ saṁjāyaṁ jāyavāṇa mahilāṇa ।
savvāsi ciya dhammujjayāṇa jalaṇāu bhīyāṇaṁ ॥
iya jāyavāṇa saṭṭī jaṇāṇa bāvattarī ya sēsāṇa ।
kulakōḍīō dīvāyaṇēṇa nayarīēm̐ daḍḍhāō ॥
ēvaṁ chammāsēṇaṁ daḍḍhā dīvāyaṇēṇa vāravaī ।
tēṇa ya palāviyā sā pacchā pacchima-samuddami ॥
baladēva- vāsudēvā ḍajjhati picchiūṇa vāravaī ।
bāha bhariyacchi-juyalā jaṁpati parōpparaṁ ēvaṁ ॥
nīsēsa - sayaṇa-rahiyā rajja-viuttā viṇaṭṭa parivārā ।
bhaya-taralacchā hariṇa vva saṁpayaṁ kattha gacchāmō ॥

taō kaṇhō pahāra - pīḍā - paravvasō namōkkāraṁ kāumāraddhō-namō parama-
pūyārihāṇaṁ arahaṁtāṇaṁ । namō sāsaya- suha samidvāṇaṁ siddhāṇaṁ । namō paṁca-vi-
hāyāra- parāṇaṁ āyariyāṇaṁ । namō sajjhāya-jjhāṇa-rayāṇaṁ uvajjhāyāṇaṁ । namō
mōkkha sāhaṇa-sahāyāṇaṁ sāhūṇaṁ । namō mama dhammaguruṇō nēmināhassa । taō

māraḍō-
dhannā kumarā pajjunna-saṁba- aniruddha- sāraṇa-ppamuhā ।
annē vi jāyava-jaṇā taha ruppiṇī- pamuha - dēvīō ॥
paricatta - savva-saṁgā sāmi-samīvaṁmi jē pavanna-vayā ।
akaya-tavaccaraṇō'haṁ tu pāvakammō marāmiti ॥
pajaṁtē dīvāyaṇa - saṁbharaṇuppanna - rōdda jjhāṇa-parō ।
sō varisa - sahassāū mariūṇa gaō taiya- puḍhaviṁ ॥
baladēvō vi javēṇaṁ gahiya-jalō naliṇi-patta- puḍaēṇa ।
vivarīya sauṇa-saṁkiya-cittō kaṇhaṁtiyaṁ pattō ॥
suttō imō tti muttūṇa sō jalaṁ ciṁtaē suvaō tāva ।
ēsō jaṇaddaṇō jaggiyassa dāhaṁ imassa jalaṁ ॥
nēha - nibbhara - maṇō mayaṁ pi taṁ na yāṇai । taō kaṁci kālaṁ paḍivāliḍaṁ
baladēvō niyacchai kasiṇamacchiyāhiṁ saṁcchannaṁ kaṇhaṁ । taō bhīō halī muhāō
vatthaṁ avaṇēha jāva hā ! mautti mucchāē paḍiō dharaṇīyalē । paccāgaya- cēya-
ṇēṇa mukkō sīnāō tahā jahā sāvayākulaṁ kāṇaṇaṁ kaṁpiumādattaṁ । bhaṇiuṁ
cāḍhatō halī- jēṇa mē ēsa bhāyā pāṇa-vallahō puhaīē ēka- vīrō nigdhiṇēṇa
durappaṇā viṇivāiō sō jai sacaṁ suhaḍō tō mē dēu daṁsaṇaṁ । kahaṁ vā suttē
pattē vāulē vā paharijjai । tā nūṇaṁ sō purisāhamō । ēvamuccasaddēṇa bhaṇatō
samaṁtaō varṇa hiṁḍiūṇa puṇō gōviṁda pāsamāgaō balō । rōviumāraddhō ya-

hā bhāya ! hā jaṇaddaṇa ! hā harivaṁsāvayaṁsa ! hā vīra ! |
kiṁ tē ruyāmi rūvaṁ sōhaggaṁ bhuyabalaṁ vihavaṁ ॥
iya vivihaṁ vilavaṁtō gamiūṇa diṇa-nisaṁ ca baladēvō ।
gōsē nēha - vimūḍhō caliō khaṁdhē hariṁ kāuṁ ॥
giri-gahaṇēsu bhamaṁtaṁ siddhattha-surō tamōhiṇā dahum̐ ।
tassa paḍibōhaṇatthaṁ ditē daṁsaē ēvaṁ ॥
giri - magga-abhaggaṁ samapahammi bhaggaṁ ca saṁghai rahaṁ sō ।
nara - rūvō ārōvai umiṇisaṁḍa silāvaṭṭē ॥
dava-daḍḍū -thāṇu- sarisaṁ tiṁduiṇi-taruṁ jalēṇa siṁcēi ।
hariya-taṇaṁkura - niyaraṁ gāvi- karōḍī muhē chuhai ॥
taṁ duhuṁ bhai balō - alaṁ kilēsēṇa tumha jaṁ imiṇā ।
raha-naliṇī- tiṁduiṇī-gāvīṇa na kōi hōi guṇō ॥
siddhattha-surō jaṁpai - jaiyā tuha khaṁdha-saṁṭhiyaṁ maḍayaṁ ।
jīvihii tathā hōhī guṇō rahāīṇa ēēsiṁ ॥
tā laddha - cēyaṇēṇaṁ balēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ - kimēsa mē bhāyā ।
saccaṁ maō tti jaṁ ēsa kō vi maṁ ēvamullavai ॥
tō paccakkhō hōuṁ siddhatthō bhaṇai - jarakumārāō ।
kaṇhassa vahō kahiō jiṇēṇa sō tahā jāō ॥
bhai balō - kaṇha - vahō vihiō kaiyā jarākumārēṇa ।
siddhatthō kahara - jarākumāra - vr̥ttaṁtamēyassa |
sō siddhatthaṁ āliṁgiuṁ bhaṇai - kahasu majjha kāyavvaṁ ।
bhaṇai surō - jiṇa vayaṇaṁ saṁbhara paḍivaja pavvajjaṁ ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ baladēvēṇaṁ karēmi ēyaṁ kahaṁ hari - sarīraṁ ।
nai duma-saṁgama- puliṇē sakārasu iya surō bhaṇai ॥
uttama purisā pyāriha tti taṁ pujiuṁ tahēva karyaṁ ।
aha nēmijiṇāṇattō cāraṇa-samaṇō tahiṁ pattō ॥
tassa samīvē vēraggasaṁgaō giṇhai balō dikkhaṁ ।
tuṁgē luṁgiya- siharē gaṁtuṁ tibvaṁ tavaṁ tavai ॥
aha jarakumarō pattō dāhiṇamahurāi paṁḍavāṇa imō ।
appē kutthuhamaṇi kahē vāravai - dāhāi ||

tē saṁviggā rajjaṁ dāuṁ tassēva nēmi -paya-mūlē ।

aha taṁ baladēvarisiṁ pañcaṁta-nivā jaṇāō sōūṇa ।
ciṁtaṁti amha rajjaṁ vaṁchaṁtō kō vi kuṇai tavaṁ ॥
vijjaṁ ca sāhaha imō tattō cauraṁga sēnna- pariyariyā ।

dāḍhā - karāla - vayaṇā rāmassa cauddisiṁ sīhā ॥

niya - niya-nayarēsu gayā tattō lōyaṁmi baladēvō ॥
narasiṁhō tti pasiḍō tavaṁ visēsēṇa kuṇai pasama- parō ।

jaggaṁtō suttō vā na lahai sukkhaṁ diṇē nisāē vā ।
saṁkā - churiyāē chijjamāṇa-hiyaō dhuvaṁ cōrō ॥

paradhanaharaṇē varuṇakathā |
tā tumha nr̥ṇamēyaṁ aṇuttaraṁ citta-kamma- caurataṁ ।
iya majjha phurai cittaṁ, tō bhaṇiyaṁ kusala - niuṇēhiṁ ॥
amhāṇamiha na kiṁci vi cittakaraṁ citta - kamma- caurattaṁ ।
dahuṁ pi paḍicchaṁdaṁ na jēhiṁ sammaṁ imā lihiyā ॥
ēkkassa payāvaiṇō vannasu vinnāṇa- kōsalaṁ ēttha ।
jēṇa paḍicchaṁdayamaṁtarēṇa bālā viṇimmaviyā ॥

bhaṇiyaṁ -kahēha bhaddā ! kā ēsā kassa vā dhūyā ॥

107
tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ — kumāra ! suṇa । atthi kaṇagaura-nayarē kaṇagaḍaō rāyā,
kaṇagāvalī sē bhajjā, tāṇa kaṇagavaī nāma dhūyā ।
pasaratēṇa samaṁtā kaṇagujjala- kāya - kaṁti - paḍalēṇa ।
kaṇayābharaṇāī pi vajā disai disā puraṁdhīṇaṁ ॥
sāya ruvāisaēṇa muṇīṇa vi maṇahāriṇī kalā-kusalattaṇēṇa asarisī
anna- kannayāṇaṁ patta- jōvvaṇā samāgayā piu-pāya- paṇamatthamatthāṇamaṁḍavē । āya-
nīyaṁ tīē vaṁdiṇā kīraṁtaṁ kumāra ! tuha guṇa kittaṇaṁ । tappabhiīṁ ca paricatta-
sēsa-vāvārā aṭṭhāṇa - dinna - sunna- huṁkārā kaṁṭha-lōlaṁta - paṁcamuggārā garuya - pasaraṁtanī-
sāsā kumāra-guṇa-saṁkahā- mēnta - patta - āsāsā saṁjāyā sā । suṇiyamiṇaṁ sē sa-
hīhiṁtō rannā । kiṁ imīē ṭhāṇē aṇurāō, kumārassa vi kērisa imaṁ paha cittaṁ
ti jāṇaṇatthaṁ kumārassa paḍicchaṁdarya āṇēuṁ, imaṁ kaṇagavaī - paḍicchaṁdayaṁ ca
daṁsiuṁ pēsiyā ittha amhē । kumāra ! nagarujāṇē rāhāvēhēṇa dhaṇuvvēyamabbha-
saṁtō puraparisarē viviha turaṁga vagga vaggaṇa-viṇōyamaṇuhavaṁtō sīha-duvārē vāra-
ṇārōha - kīlaṁ kuṇatōya diṭṭhō tumaṁ । taō sarīra-suṁdēra daliya - kaṁpa- dappassa
kumārassa ahō avikalaṁ kalā-kōsalaṁ ti pattā vimhayaṁ amhē । imaṁ ca sōūṇa
mayaṇa-sara- gōyaraṁ gaō kumārō । tahā vi niyamāgāraṁ gr̥haṁtēṇa tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ-
bhaṇa bhō maisāra ! kiṁ pi samassā - payaṁ । pahasiya-muhēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ maisārēṇa -
' kari saphalaḍaṁ appāṇu '
sigdyamēva bhaṇiyaṁ kumārēṇa-
' paḍivajji vi daya dēva guru dēvi supattihi dāṇu ।
viraha vi dīṇa - jaṇuddharaṇu kari saphalauṁ appāṇu ॥'

muṇiūṇa gaṁgaṇāgō taṁ nahaṁ sōga-nibbharō bhai ।
hā ! nikkivēṇa kēṇa vi hariyaṁ maha jīviyaṁ va imaṁ ॥

121
dahaṁ imaṁ pabhāvaṁ asaṁbhavaṁ dēvapāla- dēvassa ।
savvē vinivā āṇaṁ vahati sīsēṇa kusumaṁ va ॥
kaṇaya-maya-pāsāyaṁ jugāidēvassa kāriūṇa imō ।
pahavaṇa- vilēvaṇa-bali-mīya- naha-pamuhaṁ kuṇai pūyaṁ ॥
lacchī jaṇaddaṇassa va maṇōramā tassa vallahā dēvī ।
tīē saha sō niccaṁ vaccai jiṇa-añccaṇa-nimittaṁ ॥
annayā rannā samaṁ vaccaṁtīē maṇōramāē dēvīē jiṇa-bhavaṇāsannē diṭṭhō khaṁdha-
dviya-kaha-kāvaḍi-saṇāhō kavāḍiō । taṁ daṇa kattha maē ēsa diṭṭhaputrvōtti
ciṁtaṁtīē dēvīē samāgayā mucchā, hā ! kimēyaṁ ti visantrēṇa rannā kayā si-
sirōvayārā, satthī yā dēvī bhaṇiyamaṇāē-
aḍavihi pattī naihi jala tō vina būhā hattha ।

piyē ! dhamma- gahilā tumaṁ kiṁ pi na jāṇasi, ahaṁ puṇa para pēsatta-dutthiō na sa-
kkēmi kiṁ pi kāuṁ । taō tumaṁ dhamma-vimuhaṁ muṇaṁtīē sayaṁ cēva naī-nīrēṇa ṇhavi-

ēsō jō tullē vi parapēsattaṇē pujjēi ēvaṁ dēvaṁ na uṇa mē pai tti । taō imassa
paramappaṇō pujjaṇēṇa jīviya - phalaṁ maē pattaṁ ti ciṁtaṁtī gayā sā gihaṁ । nisāē
visūiyā - vasēṇa tēṇēva suhajjhavasāṇēṇa mariūṇa samuppannā rāyadhūyā ēsā ahaṁ ।

paumuttarō aṇaṁ bhaṇiō - appēsa mē niya-piyāō ।
paumuttarēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - ahō ! ajuttaṁ kimāyarasi ? |
para - mahilā - ahilāsō maṇaṁmi kāuṁ pi aṇuciō cēva ।
purisassa kusala mahaṇō kiṁ puṇa vayaṇēṇa vajjariḍaṁ ॥
ummagga- vilaggāṇaṁ kuṇai nivō niggahaṁ samaggāṇaṁ ।
para- mahilaṁ maggaṁtō tumaṁ tu lajjasi na kiṁ mūḍha ! ॥
।
aha bhaṇai dēvaguttō - kiṁ imiṇā ? majjha dēhi ēyāō ।
jai sōhaṇēṇa karja annaha rajjaṁ pi gihissaṁ ॥
paumuttarēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - varamaṁdhō jō parōvaēsēṇa ।
ummaggāō niyattai na uṇa tumaṁ rāya ! rāyaṁdhō ॥
jai ajasāō na bīhasi paralōya bhayaṁ ca vahasi nō hiyaē ।
kiṁ tahavi jīviyāō nivvinnō vahasa jamēvaṁ ॥
jō ērisō tumaṁ khalu na tēṇa saha jaṁpiḍaṁ pi mē juttaṁ ।
ēvaṁ dūyamuhēhiṁ saṁlāvō tāṇa saṁjāō ||
paumuttarassa uvariṁ kuviya-maṇō patthiō imō sahasā ।
paramuttarō avannāi saṁmuhō tassa saṁcaliō ॥
miliyā sa visaya-sīmāi dō vi dappaṁdha-gaṁdhahatthi vva ।
paumuttarēṇa samarē viṇijjiō dēvagutta-nivō ॥
gahiō mahāvimaddēṇa kavi diyahāī ēsa dhariūṇa ।
saṁpūhaūṇa mukkō dīhō garuyāṇa nahi kōvō ॥
saṁjāya - sāhu-vāō pattō paumuttarō niyaṁ nagaraṁ ।
daṁḍēhiṁ ciya imiṇā vasīkayā nivaṇō annē ॥
anna- diṇē naravaiṇō sahā - nisannassa kō vi appāṇaṁ ।

māyā- ōga-pavaṇaṁ paḍihāra- muhēṇa vinnavai ॥

asi - phalaga karō pavaraṁgaṇāē sahiō nahapahēṇa ॥
pattō patthiva-pāsē sō rannā pucchiō tumaṁ kō'si ? |
kā vā ēsā, kajjēṇa kēṇa vā ittha pattō'si ? ॥
sō bhai khēyarōshaṁ imā piyā majjha aha chalaṁ lahiuṁ ।
vijjāharēṇa hariyā ēkkēṇa aṇaṁga - vidurēṇa ॥
paccāṇīyā ya maē maha vēramuvaṭṭhiyaṁ ca tēṇa samaṁ ।

sannihiyāē piyāē baḍō vva na jujjhiuṁ ahaṁ sakkō ।
tā rakkha tāva ēvaṁ jiṇēmi taṁ khēyaraṁ jāva ॥

tō khagga-phalaga - pakkhō khagō vva khayarō gaō gayaṇē ॥
tatthēva ṭhiō rāyā suṇēi gayaṇē ghaṇōhagajiṁ va ।

jō kaṁṭhē 'laṁkārō jāō gaṁḍasthalēsu uvahāṇaṁ ।

niya - hatthēṇa maē jō sō pāō aisa maha paiṇō ॥

chaliōsi chalannēsaṇa parēṇa ariṇā vihi-vasēṇa ॥

samaē imami uciyaṁ ēyaṁ cēva tti ciṁtiuṁ rannā ।

paṇanna- sāmannaṁ imassa vīṇā - vinnāṇaṁ । parituṭṭhā gaṁdhavvadattā । khittā tīē dīvasi-
hassa kaṁṭhē gaṁdha-luṅa- bhamaṁta bhamara-mālā vara - mālā । kayaṁ pabaṁghēṇa pāṇiggahaṇaṁ ।
kaya-sakkārō ṭhiō kēntiyaṁ pi kālaṁ kumārō | gaṁdhavvadattaṁ vēttr̥ṇa caliō ni-
yadēsaṁ । pattō paṭṭhāṇaṁ, āvāsiō parisarē । ētthaṁtaraṁmi tattha kakkarāya -dhūyā
līlāvaī nāma kannā ahiṇā daṭṭhā maya tti nīsārijjai । suō vāitta- sadō
kumārēṇa । bhaṇiyā gaṁdhavvadattā -piē ! sajīvaṁ māṇusaṁ nīsārijai । tīē bha-
ṇiyaṁ - kahaṁ jāṇasi । kumārēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - piē! sara - visēsaō । tīē bhaṇiyaṁ-
kahamēyaṁ । kumārēṇa vr̥ttaṁ -ahiṇā dahaṁ ti । tīē bhaṇiyaṁ - avi jīvāvēhi ēyaṁ
kumārēṇa vr̥ttaṁ -atthi tāva maṁtō। tīē bhaṇiyaṁ - ajjautta ! jai ēvaṁ tā jī-
vāvēhi । pēsiō'ṇēṇa niya-purisō । dharāviyaṁ maḍagaṁ liṁpāviyaṁ ciyā-samīvē ।
gaō pacchā dīvasihō । diṭṭhō kakkarāēṇa । ahō āgii tti vimhiō ēsō ।
jīvāviyā līlāvai tti samāsatthō cittēṇa । kaō dīvasihēṇa sihābaṁdhō ।
mōyāviyā sā litta - maṁḍalē | maṁtaṁ sariūṇa bhaṇiyā ya - uṭṭhēhi jaṇaṇīē muha-
sōyaṁ dēhitti । uṭṭiyā ēsā gahiyā suvannālugā । dinnaṁ muhasōyaṇaṁ । harisi-
yāṇi savvāṇi । aō vāyāviyaṁ turaṁ । vārāviyaṁ kumārēṇa । naṇu kimaṇēṇa ?
savisā khu ēsā । maē maṁta- sāmatthaṁ daṁsiyaṁ । na uṇa ajja vikammaṁ karēmi ।
tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ - mahāpabhāvō tumaṁ tā jīvāvēhi । pāḍiyā puṇō uttarijāha-
raṇa-visa- saṁkāmaṇēṇa, daṁsiyaṁ kiṁci vēlaṁ jaṇāṇa khēḍuṁ । pacchā jīvāviyā para-
matthēṇa । kayaṁ vadvāvaṇayaṁ । diṭṭhō sāhilāsaṁ tīē kumārō । sā vi savimhayaṁ
kumārēṇa ।
I
avarupparaṁ niyaṁtāṇa tāṇa sō mayaṇa- pannagō phuriō ।
ḍakkāi jēṇa jāyāī dō vi sunnāī sahassa tti ।
tō vijayavamma-puttōtti kakkarāēṇa jāṇiuṁ kumārō nīō sagihaṁ । sā
caiva tassa līlāvaī dinnā | mahāvibhūīē pavattō vivāhō । ṭhiō tattha kai vi
diṇē sō । puṇō payō sa-visayaṁ । kamēṇa pattō ujjēṇiṁ । āvāsiō tattha ।
divvajōgēṇa diṇāvasāṇē masāṇē tēṇa diṭṭhā jalatī ciyā । sa jīvāhiṭṭhiyā ti
lakkhiyā jālā visēsāō । asāhiūṇa dēvīṇaṁ khagga- hatthō gaō tattha sō ।
nisāē ṭhiō jāva pāyava - samīvē tāva jālārūvaṁ karēmāṇō āgaō vijñā-
sāhagō । naṭṭhā ciyā - bālā । ālihiyamaṇēṇa maṁḍalaṁ । maṁta-saraṇa - purassaraṁ vā-
iō ḍamarugō | taō khuiyā ciyā । saṁbhaṁtā uṛiyā kannagā । hā tāya । tti

ruyaṁtī bhaya kaṁpaṁta- hiyayā kēsēsu kaḍiūṇa nivēsiyā maṁḍala- majjhē । bhaṇiyā
sāhagēṇa — iṭṭha- dēvayaṁ sumarasu । ēya pajavasāṇō tē jīva- lōgō । gahiyā aṇēṇa
kattigā । akkaṁdiuṁ pavattā kannagā ।
tō kaḍḍiūṇa khaggaṁ mayacchi ! mā bīhasu tti jaṁpatō ।
karuṇika-nihī kumarō puraō hōuṁ 'imaṁ bhaṇai ॥
vijjā- sāhaga ! rē narāhama ! bhaōbbhaṁtacchi - paṁkēruhaṁ
sunnāranna -gayaṁ aṇāhamabalaṁ bālaṁ vahaṁtō imaṁ ।
sunnāranna-gayaṁ
aṁgē jāṇi vasaṁti paṁca bhavaō bhūyāṇi nō lajjasē
kiṁ tāṇaṁ pi aṇattha-sattha-bhavaṇaṁ hā ! duṭṭu tē ciṭṭhiyaṁ ॥
gaya- sucariya-pāṇē pāva- kamma- ppahāṇē
jaivi hu paharaṁtō tujjha ēyaṁmi aṁgē ।
karaḍi-dalaṇa-sajjhō lajjaē mē kivāṇō
tahavi juvai - rakkhaṁ kāumabhujaō'haṁ ||
ēvaṁ paryāpamāṇaṁ kumaraṁ daṭṭhūṇa sāhagō khuddō ।
garuṇa hakkiyāṇaṁ saṁbhavai bhayaṁ hi pāvāṇa ॥
vīsariya-sayala - vijjō na khamō kumarassa vippiyaṁ kāuṁ ।
sappō vva nivvisō sō kō vā pabhavai sa punnāṇa ॥
sāhagēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ - bhō mahāsatta ! na juttaṁ bhavaō mama vigdhakaraṇaṁ, ahaṁ
khu bhārabhūī nāma vijjā- sāhagō, pāraddhaṁ maē itthī rayaṇā - karisaṇassa maṁtassa
sāhaṇaṁ । bārasa - māsiyā kayā puvva-sēvā, ajja pāraḍā pahāṇa sēvā । ēttha puṇa
rāya - kannāē bali-dāṇaṁ ti tadatthaṁ avapphēri-ppaōgēṇa saṁniruddha cēyaṇā kariya-
maṁtēṇa āṇiyā ihēsā । thaṁbhiō bhayavaṁ huyāsaṇō, saṁpāḍēmi samīhiyaṁ, ēvaṁ
ka pahāṇa - siddhī havai, tā mē mā vigdhaṁ karēhi । dīva - sihēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ, bhō !
garahiō itthi vahō acaṁta- pāva hēū; tahā-
kiṁ maṁtasiddhīi visuddha dhamma-paccatthi-bhūyāi imāi bhadda ! |
samagga-lōgāgama-niṁdaṇijjō itthī vahō kīrai jattha ēvaṁ ॥
kallāṇā giī ya tumaṁ tā kiṁ juttamiṇaṁ bhavau vavasiuṁ ti ēvaṁ bhaṇiō

[ dvitīyaḥ
avaṁtiṇī nāma dhūyā । dīvasihēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ - saṁpāḍissāmi ahaṁ bhavaō āṇattiṁ ।
gaō sāhagō । dīvasihēṇa vi nīyā kannagā niyāvāsaṁ । sāhiō vuttaṁtō dē-
vīṇaṁ, vimhiyāō ēyāō, gōsē samappiyā avaṁtivadvaṇassa | sāhiyaṁ jahā-
vattaṁ । parituṭṭhō rāyā । dinnā sē avaṁtiṇī । uciya- samaē pavattō vivāhō ।
ṭhāūṇa kaha vidiyahē niya-dēsaṁ patthiō kamēṇa imō ।
paumāvaī - purīē pattō āvāsiō bāhiṁ ॥
muṇiō ya maṁcirāēṇaṁ gōravēṇa pavēsiō majjhē ।
aha naranāha - sahāē saṁlāvō ērisō jāō ॥
pattaṁmi dēvayā kiṁ phuḍamavayariūṇa jaṁpara nava tti ।
na hu jaṁpai tti pakkhō mama tāva, imaṁ bhaṇai rāyā ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ dīvasihēṇaṁ - mā ēvaṁ bhaṇaha, ghaḍai tāva imaṁ ।
avaraha māṇusē kahamamāṇusī iya nivō bhaṇai ॥
kumarō jaṁpai - jai tuha kuḍḍuṁ ahamēva tā karēmi imaṁ ।
bhaṇiyaṁ nivēṇa dukkaramiṇaṁ anēlāugē pattē ॥
jaṁpara dīvasihō maha na dukharaṁ, jai parēsi, tō rannā ।
āṇīyā tattha lahuṁ kāmalayā nāma niya-dhūyā ॥
kaṇagujjalāē dēha - pahāē dhavalēhiṁ taha kaḍakkhēhiṁ ।
raṁjaṁtī rāyasahaṁ kuṁkuma - caṁdaṇa - rasēhiṁ va ॥
kumarēṇa maṁḍalē sā nivēsiyā sumariō maṇē maṁtō ।
āviḍaṁ pattaṁ pavaṇa-paya-pataṁ va ghummēi ॥
navari na jaṁpai taṁ jāva tāva kumarō vi bāḍhamuvauttō ।
tattō khaṇaṁtarēṇaṁ āḍhantaṁ jaṁpiḍaṁ pattaṁ ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ dīvasihēṇaṁ - bhō ! ciṭṭhaṅa tāva avaramakkhēsu ।
kiṁ ēttha kāla-haraṇaṁ tō vr̥ttaṁ patta dēvīē ॥
mūyagamēyaṁ pattaṁ iha parakaraṇēhiṁ jaṁpiyavvaṁ mē ।
-
karaṇa paḍuttaṇa- hēuṁ himavaṁta - giriṁmi pattōhaṁ ॥
divvōsahimāṇēuṁ aō imaṁ ittha kālaharaṇaṁ ti ।
kahiyaṁ ca tīē savvaṁ jaṁ puḍhaṁ maṁcirāēṇa ॥
tō parituṭṭhō rāyā, dīvasihō dēvayaṁ visajjēi ।
tappabhii phuḍakkhara mullavēha vāṇī kāmalayā ॥

kumārapālapratibōdhē
dāūṇa ya āēsaṁ 'kumaravihārō' karāviō ēttha ।
aṭṭhāvaō vva rammō cauvīsa- jiṇālaō tuṁgō ॥
kaṇayāmalasāra pahāhiṁ piṁjarē jammi mērusāricchē ।
rēhati - kēudaṁḍā kaṇaya-mayā kappa-rukkha vva ॥
stambhaiḥ kandalitēva kāñcanamayairutkr̥ṣṭapaṭṭāṁśukō-
lōcaiḥ pallavitēva taiḥ kusumitēvōccūlamuktāphalaiḥ ।
sauvarṇaiḥ phalitēva yatra kalaśairābhāti siktā satī
śrī pārśvasya śarīrakāntilaharīlakṣēṇa lakṣmīlatā ॥
pāsassa mūlapaḍimā nimmaviyā jattha caṁdakaṁtamaī ।
jaṇa-nayaṇa- kuvalaullāsa - kāriṇī caṁda-mutti vva ॥
annāō vi bahuyāō cāmīyara - ruppa - pittalamaīō ।
lōyassa kassa na kuṇaṁti vimhayaṁ jattha paḍimāō ||
saṁpas dēva sarūvaṁ muṇiūṇa samullasaṁta-suha-bhāvō ।
titthayara - maṁdirāī savvattha vi kāravissāmi ॥
tattō ihēva nayarē kāraviō kumaravāla- dēvēṇa ।
garuō 'tihuṇa-vihārō' gayaṇa-taluttaṁbhaṇa-kkhaṁbhō ॥
kaṁcaṇamaya- āmalasāra-kalasa kē uppahāhiṁ piṁjariō ।
jō bhannai savvaṁ ciya jaṇēṇa mēru ti pāsāō ॥
jassi mahappamāṇā savyuttama nīlarayaṇa-nimmāyā ।
mūla-paḍimā nivēṇaṁ nivēsiyā nēmināhassa ॥
kusumōha - aciyā jā jaṇāṇa kāuṁ pavittayaṁ pattā ।
gaṁgā-taraṁga-raṁgata- caṁgimā sahai jauṇa vva ॥
vahaṁtāṇa jiṇāṇaṁ risaha-ppamuhāṇa jattha cauvīsā ।
pittalamaya-paḍimāō kārāviyā dēvauliyāsu ॥
ēvamaikaṁtāṇaṁ taha bhāvīṇaṁ jiṇāṇa paḍimāō ।
cavīsā cavīsā nivēsiyā dēvauliyāsu ॥
iya payaḍiya dhaya - jasaḍaṁbarāhiṁ bāhattarīi jō tuṁgō ।
sappurisōvva kalāhiṁ alaṁkiō dēvakuliyāhiṁ ||
annēvi cabbīsā caḍavīsāē jiṇāṇa pāsāyā ।
kāraviyā tivihāra - ppamuhā avarē vi iha bahavō ॥
jē uṇa annē annēsu nagara - gāmāiēsa kāraviyā ।

kumārapāla pratibōdhē
cēiya-dumassa kāuṁ payāhiṇaṁ paṇamiṇa taha titthaṁ ।
sīhāsaṇē nisannō puvvābhimuhō jiṇō vīrō ॥
