aha samayammi passūyā sujasā dhūyaṁ dharā-tilaya- bhūyaṁ ।
ānaṁdiya-sayala-jaṇaṁ sajaṇa-jīha vva mahura-giraṁ ॥
pariōsa - paravasa-maṇō vaddhāvaṇayaṁ karāvaē sēṭṭhī ।
nahi sukaya-sahāyāṇaṁ jīvāṇa asaṁbhavaṁ kiṁpi ॥
jaṁ suviṇayammi diṭṭhā sujasāē sirī aō vibhūīē ।
māsammi gaē jaṇaō siritti nāmaṁ kuṇai tīē ॥
bālā lahēi buddhiṁ kamēṇa maṇa-vaṁchiyattha- jōgēṇa ।
kitti vva guṇa-kalāvēṇa suyaṇa-saṁgēṇa sumai vva ॥
livi-gaṇiya-ppamuhāhiṁ kalāhiṁ sālaṁkiyā sahīhiṁ va ।
ēīê uvajjhāyā saṁjāyā sakkhiṇō cēya ॥
jiṇadhammē paḍivattī imīê mūlāō cēva jaṁ jāyā ।
tattha nimittaṁ punnōdaēṇa sāvaya- kuluppattī ॥
sajjhāyaṁ paḍhai suṇēi tassa atthaṁ gurūṇa paya-mūlē ।
pujjēi jiṇē ḍhōēi tāṇa puraō vicitta-baliṁ ॥
sāhūṇa dēha dāṇaṁ kārēi sāhammiyāṇa vacchalaṁ ।

amarapuraṁ pi varāyaṁ rāyagihaṁ atthi taṁ nayaraṁ ॥
tattha nariṁdō nāmēṇa sēṇiō jassa dhāuṇō satta ।
jiṇa vayaṇa-niggaēhiṁ sattahi tattēhi saṁbhinnā ॥
tarasa ya naṁdā dēvīi aṁgaō saṁgaō guru-guṇēhiṁ ।
puttō abhaya kumārō jiṇa dhamma- pabhāvaṇā-sārō ॥

[ dvitīya:

vr̥ttaṁ ēvaṁ । rannā vr̥ttaṁ - sayaṁ kiṁ na paviṭṭhō ? abhaēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - tāraṇa amukkō
kahaṁ pavisāmi । rannā vr̥ttaṁ - mukkō maē । abhaēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - jai ēvaṁ tā alaṁ

iē abhaō pavvaiō । kōṇiyassa rajjaṁ dijihi tti ciṁtiūṇa sēṇiēṇa

paḍhama- patthaḍē caurāsīi-vāsa - sahassāū nāraō jāō । taō uvvaṭṭō ihēva

tiyasē vva savva laṭṭhē tē dahuṁ kūṇiyaṁ bhaṇaha bhajjā ।

sajjō hōsu । paḍivannaṁ jujjhaṁ cēḍagēṇa । kūṇiō vi samagga-sāmaggī-saṁgaō
gaō vēsālīē । pāraddhaṁ juddhaṁ । cēḍagassa rannō kira ēsa niyamō jahā ēkkammi

[ dvitīya:
puvva-kaya- saṁkēyā sōhammiṁdō camariṁdō ya dōvi samīvamāgayā, bhaṇati kūṇi-

tēhiṁ jaṁpiyaṁ parama sammadiṭṭhi cēḍayaṁ kahaṁ viṇāsēmō ?, tujjha puṇa jujjhatassa
pāṇē rakkhēmō । rannā bhaṇiyaṁ - ēvaṁ hōu । taō kūṇiō cēḍagēṇa samaṁ samara-
saṁraṁbha karēi । camariṁda - vihiēhiṁ raha- musala-silā - kaṁṭaka - saṁgāmēhiṁ paḍivakkha-
pakkhaṁ vikkhivaṁtō pattō cēḍaga samīvaṁ । caṁḍa-bhuyadaṁḍa - kuṁḍaliya-cāvēṇa cēḍagēṇa
mukkō karyaṁta dūō vva kūṇiyaṁ paḍucca bāṇō । sō ya aṁtarā rahaūṇa phaliha-silaṁ
paḍikkhaliō sakkēṇa । taṁ daddūṇa ciṁtiyaṁ cēḍagēṇa nr̥ṇaṁ khīṇō mē punna - pasarō
jaṁ paḍikkhaliō amōhō sarō, tā na jujjai aō paraṁ jujjhiuṁ ti
paviṭṭhō purīē vēsālīē cēḍagō ।
taṁ kr̥ṇiō niraṁbhiya ciṭṭhai sā taha vi tuṁga-pāyārā ।
na parēṇa akkamijjai nāri vva visuddha - sīla-guṇā ॥
halla-vihallā caḍi sēyaṇagē nisi haṇaṁti para cakkaṁ ।

[ dvitīyaḥ
ēvaṁ karēmi tti paḍivannaṁ tīē । jāyā sā kavaḍa - sāvigā । vēttūṇa satthaṁ gayā

paralōya - gaē nāhē jiṇabhavaṇāī nama̭samāṇāhaṁ ।

tā ajja diṇaṁ sahalaṁ jaṁ diṭṭhō jaṁgamaṁ tumaṁ titthaṁ ।
saṁpai kuṇasu pasāyaṁ maha muṇivara ! gihiuṁ bhikkhaṁ ॥
labbhaṁti punna-vasaō jamhā tumhārisāī pattāī ।
kiṁ hōi kaṇaya- vuṭṭhī gharaṁgaṇē puṇṇa-rahiyassa ? ॥

jaō-
savvattha saṁjamaṁ saṁjamāu appāṇamēva rakkhaṁtō ।
muca aivāyāō puṇō visōhī nayāviraī ॥

tō uvvattaṇa-dhāvaṇa-nisiyāvaṇa- pamuha- savva-kiriyāō ।
kuṇai samīva-ṭhiyā sā niraṁtaraṁ tassa parituṭṭhā ॥
iya kaivaya-dihāī paḍiyariḍaṁ ōsaha-ppaōgēṇa ।
paguṇī kuṇai sarīraṁ māgahiyā tassa samaṇassa ॥
amari vva maṇaharaṁgī payaḍiya - savvaṁga caṁga- siṁgārā ।
savilāsa-hāsamēsā kayāi samaṇaṁ imaṁ bhaṇai ॥
kiṁ dukkarēṇa imiṇā sattuṁ va tavēṇa tavasi attāṇaṁ ।
suhaya ! sukka nihāṇaṁ maṁ sēvasu gāḍhamaṇurataṁ ॥
jai pāṇa-nāha ! imiṇā tavēṇa tiyasaṁgaṇāō patthasi ।

guruvirādhanāyāṁ kūlavālakathā |
tā tāhiṁtō pavaraṁ maṁ bhayasu tavēṇa pajjataṁ ॥
aha parama- paryaṁ vacchasi tā kēṇa vi muddha ! vippaladdhōsi ।
kā tattha suhāsā jattha natthi ghōra-tthaṇī taruṇī ॥
tā muttūṇa annaṁ sapāva- sāvaya-samūha-saṁkiṇṇaṁ ।
vaccāmō raha-ramaṇīya-ramaṇi-gaṇa-maṇaharaṁ nayaraṁ ॥
jamhā tujjha viyōgaṁ khaṇaṁ pi sahiuṁ ahaṁ na sakkēmi ।
muṁca tavaṁ sēvāmō visaya-suhaṁ jōvvaṇaṁ jāva ॥
iya vayaṇāiṁ sōūṇa tīi paricatta-dhīrimō ēsō ।
millai vayābhimāṇaṁ mahilāhiṁ na gaṁjiō kō vā ॥
citta gayāō vicittaṁ hariṇacchīō haraṁti acaṁtaṁ ।
kiṁ puṇa vilāsa - pēsala caḍḍu-kamma- payāsaṇa-parāō ॥
aha parituṭṭa-maṇā sā tēṇa samaṁ kūṇiyassa pāsammi ।
gaṁtuṁ vihiya-paṇāmā kayaṁjalī vinnavai ēvaṁ ॥
dēva ! maha jīviēsō ēsō sō kūlavālagō samaṇō ।
jaṁ imiṇā kāyavvaṁ ihi taṁ āisau dēvō ॥
bhaṇai nivō - bhadda ! imā jaha bhajjai puravarī taha karē ।
taṁ paḍivajjai samaṇō tō kuṇai tidaṁḍiṇō vēsaṁ ॥
pavisai purīi majjhē muṇisuvvaya-sāmiṇō niyai thūbhaṁ ।
thūbha - pahāvēṇa purī bhajjai na dhuvaṁ ti takkēi ॥
tā taha karēmi dhūbhaṁ avaṇiti jahā jaṇa tti ciṁtēi ।
phieies nayari- rōhō kahaṁ ti pucchaṁti taṁ lōgā ॥
bhai imō jai thūbhaṁ avaṇēha taō avēi para cakkaṁ
annaha nayarī - rōhō na kahaṁ pi hu phiṭṭihī ēsō ॥
avaṇijaṁtē thūbhē ōsariyavvaṁ taē sa-sinēṇa ।
iya saṁkēyaṁ sō kūṇiēṇa saha kuṇai kūḍa-maī ॥
lōgā bhaṇati kō ittha pañcaō tō paryapaē samaṇō ।
ōsarihī para cakka thrubhē thē vē vi avaṇīē ।
ēsō khu paccaō iha, tō lōgā thūbha - siharamavarṇiti ।
para cakka mōsaraṁtaṁ picchaṁti ya tammi samayasmi ॥
aha jāya-paccayā taṁ dhūbhaṁ avaṇiti savvamavi mūḍhā ।

gurusēvāyāṁ sampratinr̥pakathā |
giddhi-vasēṇa siddhiṁ bahuṁ ca uvabhuṁjiūṇa damaga- muṇī ।
majjhattha-bhāva- juttō visūyāē nisāi maō ॥
aha atthi attha-bhara- vilasamāṇa- māṇaṁ va maṇōharaṁ nayaraṁ ।

caṁdō vva caṁdauttō cāṇakkēṇaṁ kaō rāyā ॥

riu-ramaṇi bāha-biṁdūhiṁ vaḍḍiyā jassa kitti-layā ॥
tassa suō saṁjāō rāyā nāri-ppiō asōgasirī ।
pasariya-payāva- kisalō jaṇāṇa phala-dāyagō kiṁtu ॥
tassa vi taṇaō jāō guṇa-vivahālaṁkiō kuṇālō ti ।
bālattaṇē vi ṭhaviō juvarāya-payaṁmi jō piuṇā ॥
sō uvaraya jaṇaṇīō tti iyara - māyā bhaēṇa paṭṭhaviō ।
bahu- pariyaṇa- pariyariō kumārabhuttīē ujjēṇi ॥
anna - samaē kumāraṁ rāyā nāuṁ kalā - gahaṇa - jōggaṁ ।
lihai sahatthēṇa imaṁ lēhami 'adhīyatāṁ kumara' ॥
paḍivāiūṇa lēhaṁ jjhatti aṇuvvāṇa akhkharattaṇaō ।
tatthēva asaṁvattiyamimaṁ vimuttaṁ gaō rāyā ॥
kāuṁ sarīra ciṁtaṁ tō rannō pāsa-sannisannāē ।
ghittūṇa vāiō sō kumarassa savatti-jaṇaṇīē ॥
rajjassa ajuggamimaṁ karēmi iya ciṁtiūṇa sā dēi ।
biṁdu agāra - uvariṁ tahēva taṁ millaē lēhaṁ ॥
khaṇamittēṇa nariṁdō samāgaō hattha milliō lēhō ।
paḍivāiō vi puvvaṁ puṇōvi paḍivāiyavvōti ॥
vayaṇaṁ asaṁbharaṁtō lēhaṁ saṁvattiūṇa muddēi |
appēi lēha-vāhassa sō vi gaṁtūṇa ujjēṇiṁ ॥
daṁsaha kumarassa imō vi gihiuṁ lēhayassa appēi ।
sō vāiūṇa lēhaṁ tuhikkō cēva ciṭṭhēi ||
bhāi kumārō vāēsi kiṁ na lēhaṁ ? na sō bhaṇai kiṁpi ।
tō vēttr̥ṇa sayaṁ ciya kumarō vāēi taṁ jāva ॥

tō tattha lihiyamēyaṁ picchai 'aṁdhīyatāṁ kumāra ' iti ।
sō bhai ahma vaṁsē akhaliya-āṇā nivā savvē ॥
- tā nūṇamahaṁ kāhaṁ hatthaṁ pariyaṇō bhaṇai kumaraṁ ।
puṇa pucchiūṇa kīrai sō jaṁpai kiṁ viyārēṇa ? ॥
tō tatta-salāyāē acchi-juyalaṁ aṁjaē sayaṁ kumarō ।
jāō aṁghō purisō vi kahai savvaṁ imaṁ rannō ॥
rāyā visanna-cittō visamaṁ vihi-vilasiyaṁ ti ciṁtēi ।
rajjēṇa kimaṁdhassa ? tti dēi gāmaṁ ca tassēgaṁ ॥
ujjēṇiṁ puṇa viyarai savvakki - puttassa kumarabhuttīē ।
aha gīya- kalababhāsē kaya-cittō ciṭṭhahna kuṇālō ॥
sō maga - sāhu-jīvō kuṇāla- putō tumaṁ samuppannō ।
tuha rajjaṁ icchaṁtō kusumapurē vaccai kuṇālō ॥
tattha pahiṁ gīyaṁ gāyaṁtō raṁjaē jaṇaṁ sayalaṁ ।
pattō paraṁ pasiddhiṁ rannā saddāviō ēsō ॥
tassa puraō kuṇālō gīyaṁ gāēi javaṇiyaṁta riō ।
tuṭṭhō taṁ bhaṇai nivō magga varaṁ jaṁpai kuṇālō ॥
caṁdagutta - paputtō ya biṁdusārassa nattuō ।
asōgasiriṇō puttō aṁdhō jāyai kākiṇi ॥
tō rannā sō nāō niya-taṇaō javaṇiyaṁ avaṇiūṇa ।
aṁkē ṭhaviḍaṁ bhaṇiō putta । taē maggiyaṁ thōvaṁ ॥
maṁtī bhaṇai na thēvaṁ jēṇa nariṁdāṇa kāgiṇī rajjaṁ ।
bhannai tō bhaṇai nivō putta ! kimaṁdhassa rajjēṇa ? ॥
bhai kuṇālō karihī rajjaṁ maha naṁdaṇō, bhaṇai rāyā ।
jāō kayā tuha suō, saṁpai jāō tti sō bhaṇai ॥
tō ' saṁpai ' tti nāmaṁ tujjha kayaṁ āṇiūṇa samayasmi ।
ṭhaviō rajjammi tumaṁ jāōsi tikhaṁḍa-bharaha - vaī ॥
bhaṇai nivō pattō'haṁ tujjha pasāēṇa ittiyaṁ riddhiṁ ।
ihi pi guru! tumamēva majjha āisasu karaṇijaṁ ॥
bhaṇai gurū jiṇadhammaṁ ubhaya-bhava suhāvahaṁ kuru nariṁda ! |

gurusēvāyāṁ sampratinr̥pakathā |
sammattaṁ bārasaviha- sāvaga-dhammēṇa saṁgayaṁ tattō ।
gives saṁpai - rāō ajjasuhatthissa paya-mūlē ॥
accai jiṇō ti-saṁjhaṁ paṇamai muṇiṇō suṇēi siddhataṁ ।
sō mahi-valayaṁ sayalaṁ jiṇa-bhavaṇa-vibhūsiyaṁ kuṇai ॥
avara- varisē suhatthimmi āgaē tattha jiṇa-bhavaṇa-jattā ।
daviṇa - viṇiōga - vihiujjamēṇa saṁvēṇa pāradvā ॥
tattha suhatthī jiṇa maṁḍavammi nivasai samagga- saṁgha - juō ।
āgaṁtuṁ guru-puraō kayaṁjalī ciṭṭhaē rāyā ॥
kāuṁ jiṇahara-jattaṁ jiṇa-raha jattā jaṇēhiṁ āḍhattā ।
bhamai rahō nayarīē para paē vihiya-sakkārō ॥
rāyabhavaṇammi pattō taṁ dahuṁ saṁpaī phuriya-harisō ।
accai sayaṁ ciya jiṇaṁ aṭṭha- payārāi- pūyāē ॥
takkālamēva hakkāriūṇa rāyā bhaṇēi sāmaṁtē ।
jai imaṁ mannaha sāmiṁ tō jiṇa-bhaktiṁ kuṇaha tubhē ॥
samaṇāṇa sāvagā hōha jēṇa nāhaṁ dhaṇēṇa tr̥sēmi ।
iya vihiē khalu tōsō majjha mahaṁtō kaō hōi ॥
aha tē vi jiṇaharāī rahajattāō jaīṇa bhaktiṁ ca ।
savvē kuṇaṁti ēvaṁ pannaviyā āriyā rannā ॥
viharaṁti jahā jaiṇō aṇāriēsuṁ vi karēmi taha iṇhiṁ ।
iya ciṁtiūṇa rāyā aṇāriē ēvamāṇavai ॥
jaha jaha maggati karaṁ majjha bhaḍā dēha taha tahā tubbhē ।
tō paṭṭaviyā rannā muṇi-vēsa-dharā narā tattha ॥
ēvaṁ aṇāriē tē bhāṁti vatthanna-pāṇamamhāṇaṁ ।
dēyaṁ rahiyamimēhiṁ bayālīsāi - dōsēhiṁ ||
paḍhiyavvaṁ puṇa ēyaṁ tā sāmī tumha tūsihi nūṇaṁ ।
annaha karihī kōvaṁ tahēva taṁ tē vihu kuṇaṁti ॥
iya jai - jaṇōciyācāra - caura - cittēsu tēsu vihiē ।
sūrī ajjasuhatthī saṁpai-rāēṇa vinnattō ॥
viharaṁti kiṁ na muṇiṇō aṇāriēsuṁ ?, guru bhaṇai ēvaṁ ।
tēsu anāṇattaṇaō nāṇāi-guṇā na vaḍr̥ti ॥

kumārapālapratibōghē
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ ! muṇiṇō pēsaha aṇāriēsuṁ pi ।
tō aṁdha- damila - pamuhēsu pēsiyā sāhūṇō guruṇā ॥
dahuṁ aṇāriyā tē muṇiṇō rannō bhaḍa tti mannaṁtā ।
viyaraṁti bhatta-pāṇāi tāṇa puvyutta- sikkhāē ॥
muṇiṇō kahaṁti ēyaṁ gurussa, ēvaṁ aṇāriyā vihiyā ।
jai-jaṇa-vihāra- juggā saṁpaiṇā niyaya-santī ॥
sumariya putrva bhavēṇaṁ purīi rannā karāviyā sattā ।
tēsu sa parāṇavikkhā lahaṁti vara bhōyaṇaṁ lōā ॥
giṇhaṁti mahāṇasiā uvvariyaṁ tēsu bhōyaṇaṁ kiṁ pi ।
tē bhai nivō dējjaha imaṁ samaggaṁ pi sāhūṇa ॥
tumhāṇa dhaṇaṁ dāhaṁ tō bhattaṁ diti tē vi sāhūṇaṁ ।
kaṁdaviya - vaṇiya- pamuhē jaṁpai saṁpai nivō ēvaṁ ॥
maṁḍaga- mōyaga - cōppaḍa - kappaḍa - pamuhaṁ muṇīṇa viyarēha |
tammulamahaṁ dāhaṁ tumha, taō tē vi taṁ diti ॥
jāṇatō vi suhatthī tamajuttaṁ sahai sīsa-rāēṇa ।
jaṁpara mahāgirī - kiṁ suhatthi ! giṇhasi asuddhamiṇaṁ ॥
rannō bhattaṁ ?, tattō bhai suhatthī - muṇiṁda ! kimasuddhaṁ ? ।
rāyāṇuvattaṇa-parā jamhā lōā imaṁ diti ॥
māiti taṁ sa-kōvō mahāgirī bhaṇai - ajja -pabhii tumaṁ ।
maha na havasi saṁbhōgī, saṁgō hi samēhiṁ saha kahiō ॥
bālō vva bhaubtō bhai suhatthī mahāgiriṁ ēvaṁ |
khamaha maha dōsamēghaṁ bhayavaṁ ! na puṇō imaṁ kāhaṁ ॥
jaṁpara mahāgirī ahava na tuha dōsō jaō jiṇidēṇa ।
vīrēṇa bhaṇiyamēyaṁ anaṁtaraṁ thūlabhaddāō ||
titthē imammi samaṇā paḍata-guṇa- pagarisā bhavissaṁti ।
taṁ saccamiṇaṁ jāyaṁ ēvaṁ ṭhaviḍaṁ asaṁbhōgaṁ ॥
ujjēṇī -nayarīō gaō muṇiṁdō gayagga-paya-titthē ।
aṇasaṇa - vihiṇā muttaṁ sarīramamarālayaṁ pattō ॥
kāūṇa sāvagattaṁ mariūṇa samāhiṇā gaō saggaṁ ।
saṁpai-nivō kamēṇaṁ lahihī nivvaṇa-sukkhaṁ pi ॥

aṇṇa-samaē suhatthī ujjēṇīē muṇīhiṁ saha pattō ।

jai sayaṇēsu siṇēhō mukkō saṁjama kaē taē vaccha ! ।

।

vimhiya-maṇēṇa rannā muṇi-nāhō pucchiō kimēyaṁ ti ।

kumārapālapratibōdhē
jaha vi tumaē vimukkā ahaṁ ahannā tahā vi maha nāha ! ।
tuha calaṇa cciya saraṇaṁ ti nicchiuṁ sā ṭhiyā bālā ||
dāūṇa vaccharaṁ dāṇamujjayaṁtē pavanna cārittō ।
ca-pannāsa- diṇaṁtē lahai pahū kēvalaṁ nāṇaṁ ॥
।
tō nagarāgara - gāmāiē paḍibōhiūṇa bhaviya - jaṇaṁ ।
sō-vāsa- sahassāū ihēva ayalē gaō mukkhaṁ ॥
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ bhayavaṁ ! aja vi takkāla-saṁbhavaṁ kimimaṁ ।
cii dasāra- maṁḍava - pamuhaṁ tō jaṁpiyaṁ guruṇā ॥
takkāla- saṁbhavaṁ jaṁ taṁ na imaṁ kiṁ tu thēva - kāla-bhavaṁ ।
tamimaṁ puṇa jēṇa kayaṁ kahēmi taṁ tujjha nara-nāha ! ॥
guru- nāgahatthi - sīsō bālō vi a-bāla-maha-guṇō sukaī ।
kaiyā vi kaṁjiyaṁ ghēttuṁ - māgaō kahai guru-puraō ॥
aba (?) taṁbacchīē apuṣphiyaṁ pupphadaṁta - paṁtīē ।
nava- sāli - kaṁjiyaṁ nava-bahūi kuḍaēṇa mē dinaṁ ॥
guruṇā bhaṇiō sīsō vaccha ! palittōsi jaṁ paḍhasi ēvaṁ ।
sīsō bhai pasāyaṁ kuru maha āyāra dāṇēṇa ॥
ēvaṁ ti bhaṇai sūrī tō pālittō jaṇēṇa sō vr̥ttō ।
jāō ya suya-samuddō āyariō viviha-siddhi - juō ॥
kāūṇa pāya - lēvaṁ gayaṇē sō bhramai namai titthāī ।
suṇai suraṭṭha-nivāsī bhikkhū nāgajjuṇō ēvaṁ ॥
sō patthai pālittaṁ payaccha ! niya-pāya-lēva - siddhiṁ mē ।
giraha maha kaṇaya - siddhiṁ tattō pālittaō bhai ॥
nikkicaṇassa kiṁ kaṁcaṇēṇa kiṁ catthi mē kaṇaya - siddhī ।
tuha pāya - lēva- siddhiṁ ca pāva- hēu tti na kahēmi ॥
tō kaya- sāvaya-rūvēṇa bhikkhuṇā āgayarasa girinayarē ।
guruṇō guru bhakttīē jalēṇa pakkhāliyā calaṇā ॥
paya-pakkhālaṇa-salilassa gaṁdhaō ōsahīṇa nāūṇa ।
sattuttaraṁ sayaṁ tēṇa pāya - lēvō sayaṁ vihiō ॥
tavvasaō gayaṇē kukkuḍō vva uppaḍai paḍai puṇa bhikkhū ।
tō kahai jahāvittaṁ guruṇō tēṇāvi tuṭṭhēṇa ॥

anna dinē bhikkhatthaṁ sugutta-maṁtissa maṁdirē pattō ।

kannāi imīē vikaēṇa hōhī dhaṇaṁ ca tahā ॥

hā haya - vihi maha kā hisi tumamajja vi kēttiyaṁ dukkhaṁ ॥
saṁpattamhi viōgaṁ paṇō guṇa - rayaṇa - jalahiṇō rannō ।
nissīma - samīhiya-kārayassa rajassa cukkamhi ॥
jāyamhi bhāyaṇaṁ sayala - sayaṇa- pariyaṇa-saṭhāṇa - bhaṁsassa ।
iccāi - dukkhamakhilaṁ sahiyamiṇaṁ dussahaṁ pi maē ॥
jaṁ puṇa sīla-viṇāsaṁ maha kāuṁ mahasi taṁ khalu na juttaṁ ।
jaṁ vimala - kulē jāyā jāṇiya-jiṇa vayaṇa - tattāhaṁ ॥
asamaṁjasaṁ pi sōuṁ ajjavi jīvāmi ahaha ! nibbhaggā ।
iya mattu-bhinna hiyayāi tīha pāṇā viṇikkhatā ॥
dahūṇa mayaṁ dēviṁ vicitiyaṁ uṭṭhiēṇa dhī majjha ।
ēsā bhajjā hōhi tti jaṁpiyaṁ taṁ imā sōuṁ ॥
jaha pattā paṁcattaṁ vivajjihī kannayāvi taha ēsā ।
iya ciṁtiūṇa aṇukūlamālavaṁtēṇa tēṇēsā ॥
āṇīyā kōsaṁbiṁ cauppa hē matthaē taṇaṁ dāum̐ ।
āḍhattā vikkiṇiuṁ divva vasā siṭṭiṇā diṭṭhā ॥
ciṁtiyamaṇēṇa ēsā uttama puttī imīi muttīē ।
māi piu parinbhaṭṭhā ēēṇa durappaṇā pattā ॥
-
hariṇi vva luddhaēṇaṁ jūhabhaṭṭhā palaṁ va vikkaṇiuṁ ।
iha ṭhaviyā hā ! kassa vi hīṇassa caḍissai karammi ||
dāum̐ bahuṁ pi davvaṁ giṇhāmi imaṁ jaō na sakkēmi ।
niya-puttiṁ piva ēvaṁ uvikkhiyaṁ duddasā - vaḍiyaṁ ॥
maha maṁdirē imīē ciṭṭaṁtīē aṇattha-cattāē ।
hōhī kamēṇa sayaṇēhiṁ saṁgamō iya viciṁtēuṁ ॥
siṭṭhī ghaṇāvahō uṭṭiyassa dāu maṇicchiyaṁ mulaṁ ।
paramullasaṁta karuṇō niya-gēhē vasumaī nēi ॥
sō
pucchai putti ! tumaṁ kassa suyā sā vi uttamattaṇaō ।
kahiuṁ niya- kulamakhamā ahō suhī mōṇa - mallīṇā ॥
mūlā ghaṇāvaṇaṁ bhaṇiyā ēsā piē । suyā amha ।

puṣpaṁ va pālaṇijjā attēṇa niraṁtaraṁ tumaē ||
ēvaṁ siṭṭi - girāē sā vutthā tattha niyaya-gēha vva ।
jaṇa-ṇayaṇāṇaṁda karā bālā bālēṁdu - lēha vva ॥

187
ēvaṁ itthī - yaṇa-sulahēṇa tucchattaṇēṇa tammaṁta ciṁtā nicaṁ pi ciṭṭhaē
mūlā । annayā gimhumha - pīḍiō haṭṭāō āgaō gihaṁ sēṭṭhī । divva-vasēṇa
na annō kōvi kammayarō asthi tti vāraṁtassa vi sēṭṭhiṇō pāē pakkhā-
liḍaṁ payaṭṭā viṇīyattaṇaō caṁdaṇā । tīē ya nissahaṁgīē akaya-kamma-
babhāsāē lhasiō siddhi kasiṇō kēsapāsō । vacchāē kēsapāsō paṁkilē
khiitalē paḍatō paṁkēṇa mā lippau tti dhariō līlā - laṭṭhīē sēṭṭiṇā । saṁja-
miō ya sāyaraṁ । taṁ dahūṇa gavakkha gayāē mūlāē ciṁtiyaṁ jaṁ maē puvvaṁ
viyakkiyaṁ taṁ saṁvaya savvaṁ । annahā kahaṁ sēṭṭiṇā sayaṁ saṁjamiyā imīē
kēsā । ērisaṁ khu lakkhaṇaṁ na hōi piuṇō । tā maē mūlāō vāhi vva
chiṁdiyavvā ima tti nicchiūṇa ṭhiyā mūlā । sēṭṭhī vi vīsamiūṇa khaṇaṁ puṇō
vi gaō bāhiṁ । mūlāē kāsavaṁ saddāviūṇa muṁḍāviyā caṁdanā | pārasu
nigaḍiūṇa tāḍiyā ciraṁ । khittā uayaraē । tattha dāūṇa kavāḍa saṁpuḍhaṁ
bhaṇiō pariyaṇō । sēṭṭhiṇō pucchaṁtassa vi imaṁ na kēṇāvi kahaṇīyaṁ । jō
uṇa kō vi kahissai, sō majjha vēriō । sēṭṭiṇā vi saṁjhāē āgaēṇa
pucchiyaṁ - kattha caṁdaṇa tti । mūlā-bhayāō na kēṇāvi kahiyaṁ । pacchā gharōvariṁ
ramaṁtī ciṭṭhaha tti ciṁtiyaṁ sēṭṭhiṇā । rayaṇīē vi pucchiyaṁ na kēṇāvi kahiyaṁ । pa-
suttā caṁdaṇa tti ciṁtiyaṁ imiṇā । vīya- diṇē vi na diṭṭhā। tahēva taiya- diṇē taṁ
apēcchaṁ tēṇa tēṇa bhaṇiō pariyaṇō – rērē ! kahēha, kahiṁ mē naṁdaṇā caṁdaṇā ।
jai jāṇaṁtā vi na kahissaha tā niggahissāmi tumhē । imaṁ sōūṇa ēkkāē
buḍḍa-caḍīē ciṁtiyaṁ jīviyā ahaṁ ciraṁ । saṁpayaṁ paccāsannō mē maccū । kahiē
caṁdaṇāē vr̥ttatē kiṁ karissara mē mūlā ।

kāuṁ parōvayāraṁ imēhiṁ jara jajjarēhiṁ pāṇēhiṁ ।
viḍhavaṁti jasaṁ dhammaṁ ca jē jaṇā tē dhuvaṁ dhannā ॥
tō mūlā-vr̥ttaṁtō siṭṭhō siṭṭissa tīē savvō vi ।
taṁ dasiyaṁ ca gēhaṁ asthi jahiṁ caṁdaṇā khittā ॥
ugghāḍiyaṁ duvāraṁ tassa sayaṁ siṭṭiṇā taō tattha ।
chuha- tisa- dūmiya-dēhā dāvānala - pharisiya vva layā ॥
pāya- jugē nigalēhiṁ baḍā takkāla gahiya kariṇi vva ।
muṁḍiya - muṁḍā nava- bhikkhuṇi vva sā caṁdaṇā diṭṭhā ॥
bāha-salilāvilacchō vacchē ! satthā-hava tti jaṁpatō ।
tīē bhōyaṇa - hēḍaṁ jhatti gaō rasavaī siṭṭī ॥
tattha maṇujaṁ bhujaṁ apicchamāṇō imō vihi-vasēṇa ।
appēi caṁdaṇāē kummāsē suppa-kōṇammi ॥
bhuṁja tumaṁ tāva imaṁ jāva ahaṁ nigaḍa-bhaṁjaṇatthaṁ tē ।
āṇēmi lōhakāraṁ iya bhaṇiuṁ niggaō sēṭṭhī ॥
aha caṁdaṇā ruyaṁtī vicitaē ahaha ēsa saṁsārō ।
suviṇidayāla - sarisō nivvēyaṁ kuṇai nahu kassa ॥
jēṇāhaṁ puttī vi hu naravahaṇō tārisassa hōūṇa ।
pattā imaṁ avatthaṁ tā ihi kiṁ karēmi hahā ! ॥
kummāsā saṁpattā saṁpai chaṭṭhassa pāraṇaṁmi maē ।
jai kōvi ēi atihī tā dāuṁ tassa bhuṁjēhaṁ ॥
ēvaṁ vicitayaṁtī dihiṁ dārammi caṁdaṇā dēi ।
taiyā vīrō bhayavaṁ bhikkhatthaṁ āgaō tattha ॥
dhannā ahaṁ ahō ! mē punnaṁ jīviya- phalaṁ maē laddhaṁ ।
dhammō vva muttimaṁ tō jaṁ ēsō maharisī pattō ॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa caliyā kamamēkkaṁ dēhalīi majjhammi ।

bhayavaṁ ! jaivi na juggaṁ bhōyaṇamēyaṁ tahāvi ginha tumaṁ ।

sō vi ya bhuttō ghaya-gula - saṁpunnaṁ annaṁ paramannaṁ । pacchima disā - ramaṇikanna-

[ tr̥tīya:
puttēhiṁ vr̥ttaṁ parikkhaṁ karēha । taō ēkkēkassa battīsā battīsā rūvagā tēhiṁ dinnā,
bhaṇiyā imē—karēha imēhiṁ vāṇijjaṁ । payaṭṭā tē vavahariḍaṁ । dhantrēṇa puṇa savva-ka-
lā- kusalē kiṇiuṁ baliḍō miṁḍhaō । dōṇāra- sahassaṁ paṇē kāūṇa jujjhāviō
rāyaputta - miṁḍhēṇa samaṁ । bhaggō aṇēṇa rāyaputta- miṁḍhō । taō dīṇāra - sahassaṁ vēttū-
ṇa miṁḍhaya - hatthō jhatti āgaō gihaṁ dhannō । annē puṇa akaya-punnā alaḍa-lābhā
vivanna-vayaṇā divasāvasāṇē āgayā । bīya-diṇē bhaṇati tē puṇō parikkhaṁ
karēha । taō ēkkēkassa sahī sahī karisāvaṇā appiyā । tē vi payattēṇa kaya-
vikkayaṁ kuṇaṁtā na lahaṁti lāhaṁ kiṁ puṇa chēyaṁ ।
aha āsi tattha nayarē mahādhaṇō kiviṇa - sēharō sēṭṭhī ।
sō vivihē āraṁbhē kāūṇa uvajjaē davvaṁ ॥
dhammatthamattha-niyaraṁ na dēi na vi dēi sayaṇa-uvayāraṁ ।
na kayāvi kuṇai ēsō dhaṇa-vvayaṁ niya- sarīrē vi ॥
patthitō ēsō kuppaṛa jaṁpēi parusa - vayaṇāī ।
ditē parēvi diṭṭhē satta - muha sē jō ēi ॥
mucchā-vasēṇa khaṇiūṇa tēṇa davvēṇa pūriyā khaḍḍā ।
aṁtō susirā kāuṁ bhariyā rayaṇēhiṁ taha khaṭṭā ॥
khaḍḍāi tīi uvariṁ khahaṁ ṭhaviūṇa suyaha sō tīē ।
na ya muṇai imaṁ mūḍhō na vaccihī para bhavē kiṁ pi ॥
sō millāvijaṁtō na aṁta- samaē vi muyai taṁ khahaṁ ।
aṁta-samaē
tattō maō vi tīē khaṭṭāē piu-vaṇaṁ nīō ॥
taṁ khahaṁ cauṭṭē vikkijaṁtaṁ masāṇa - vālēṇa ।
dakkhō dhannō giust lakkhiuṁ rayaṇa-gabbhaṁ ti ॥
jaō-
dūra-nihittaṁ pi nihiṁ taṇa valli samucchyāi bhūmīē ।
nayaṇēhiṁ apēcchaṁtā niuṇā buddhīi pērhati ॥
sā appiyā piūṇaṁ khaṭṭāō khīliyāō avaṇēuṁ ।
rayaṇāī kaḍḍiyāiṁ tō tēsiṁ vaḍiō vivō ॥
dhannaṁ hētu maṁtaṁti bhāuṇō bhūri-macchara-cchannā |

dhannō ciṁtai na maē imāṇa baṁdhūṇa kiṁci avaraddhaṁ ।

saṁpai asaṁsayaṁ ciya saṁjama bhāraṁ pavajjihī ēsō ।

tāhi bhaṇiyaṁ sahāsaṁ jaṛa giṇhasi saṁjamaṁ tumaṁ sāmi ! |

nāmāī ēgassa vasaṁtadēvō annassa kāmavālō । vivannā dhaṇavai dhaṇēsarā samupannā
vaṇiya- dhūyattāē ēgā saṁkhaurē annā jayaṁtīē । kayāī nāmāī ēgāē maharā
annāē kēsarā ! kamēṇa mayaṇa-viyāruvvaṇaṁ jōvvaṇaṁ saṁpattā tē savvē । kayāi
kaṁpillāō atthōvajjaṇatthaṁ gaō jayaṁtīē vasaṁtadēvō । tattha vi ciṭṭhatēṇa
vasaṁtadavēṇa diṭṭhā aṭṭhamī - caṁda- mahērai naṁdaṇujāṇē rai vva kēsarā, tīē vi
vasaṁtadēvō । putrva bhavanbhāsēṇa siṇēha sāraṁ duṇhaṁ pi miliyā diṭṭhī । kā ēsa
tti pucchiō vasaṁtadēvēṇa jayaṁti vatthavvō saṁjāya-mitta bhāvō piyaṁkarō nāma
vaṇiya- puttō।
kahiyaṁ tēṇaṁ ēsā dhūyā sēṭṭhissa paṁcanaṁdissa ।
bhaiṇī jayaṁtadēvassa kannagā kēsarā nāma ॥
tattō vasaṁtadēvō jayaṁtadēvēṇa saha kuṇai mēti ।
anna dinē sō nīō jayaṁtadēvēṇa niya-bhavaṇē ॥
diṭṭhā vasaṁtadēvēṇa nayaṇa- kumuyāṇa caṁdalēha vva ।
accaṁtī kusuma-saraṁ kusumēhiṁ kēsarā tattha ॥
tīē vasaṁtadēvō jayaṁtadēvassa hattha - kamalāō ।
kusumāī paḍicchaṁtō diṭṭhō garuyāṇurāyāē ॥
iṇamaṇukūlaṁ sauṇaṁ ti dōvi harisaṁ gayāī niya-cittē ।
lakkhēi dhāvidhūyā piyaṁkarā nāma savvamimaṁ ॥
pavaraṁ jayaṁtadēvō vasaṁtadēvassa kuṇai uvayāraṁ ।
tattō piyaṁkarāē payaṁpiyā kēsarā ēvaṁ ॥
tujjha vi jujjai kāuṁ suyaṇassa imassa kāvi paḍivattī ।
jugavaṁ lajjā sambhasa - harisa-parā kēsarā bhāi ॥
piyaṁkarē ! tumaṁ cēva jāṇasi jaṁmittha uciyaṁ ti । piyaṁkarā vi bhavaṇujjā-
gagayassa tarussa piyaṁgumaṁjarīō kakkōlaphalāī ca samappaṁtī jaṁpēi - suṁdara saha-
tthārōviya- rukkha samuppannāī imāī iṭṭha- dēyāī maha sāmiṇīē kēsarāē tujjha pē-
siyāī । iṭṭhō ahaṁ ti harisiēṇa gahiyāī tāī vasaṁtadēvēṇa । dāūṇa nāmamudda
bhaṇiyā ēsā, vattavvā tumaē sāmiṇī, sōhaṇaṁ kathaṁ । tumaē vaṭṭiyanvaṁ sayāvi
idvāṇuruvaṁ । piyaṁkarāē gaṁtr̥̄ṇa savvaṁ kahiyaṁ kēsarāē । parituṭṭhā sā hiyaēṇa ।

[ tr̥tīya:
rayaṇīē carama- jāmē diṭṭhō imīē suviṇō, kilāhaṁ pariṇīyā vasaṁtadēvēṇa । tēṇāvi
suviṇē kayaṁ kēsarā-pariṇayaṇaṁ । tuṭṭha-cittāē kēsarāē kahiō suviṇō piyaṁkarāē ।
itthaṁtarē niya- kajja-gayaṁ jaṁpiyaṁ purōhiēṇa - ēvaṁ cēva ēvaṁ bhavissai ti imaṁ sō-
ūṇa parituṭṭhāō dōvi । jaṁpiyaṁ piyaṁkarāē savvahā vasaṁtadēvō tujjha bhattārō ti
baddha saṇa-gaṁṭṭhī kēsarāē । kahiō suviṇa vr̥ttaṁtō vasaṁtadēvassa । sō vi niya-
suviṇa saṁvāyāō siddhaṁ samīhiyatthaṁ mannatō pattō pamōyaṁ । bhaṇiō piyaṁka-
rāē - dinō tujjha appā sauṇa-gaṁṭṭhi baṁdhaṁtīē sāmiṇīē । tā karēsu vivāha-
saṁjuttiṁ । vasaṁtadēvēṇa vr̥ttaṁ kayā cēva vihiṇā saṁjuttī । ēvaṁ pai-diṇaṁ pavaḍḍūmā-
ṇāṇurāyāṇa aitō kōi kālō । annayā sa-giha-gaēṇēva suō paṁcanaṁdi-gēhē
maṁgala- tūra - saddō vasaṁtadēvēṇa । kimēyaṁ ti gavēsāviyaṁ imiṇā । kahiyaṁ kamma -
yarīē jahā dinnā kēsarā kannaujja - vatthavva-vasudatta sēṭṭhi- puttassa varadattassa ।
tannimittamēyaṁ vaddhāvaṇayaṁ ti । taṁ sōūṇa mucchiō vasaṁtadēvō । ētyaṁtarē
āgayā piyaṁkarā āsāsiō tīē, bhaṇiyaṁ ca - pēsiyā ahaṁ kēsarāē, saṁdihaṁ
tīē, na taē khēō kāyavvō, mama cittaṁ ajāṇatēhiṁ guruhiṁ pāraḍamēyaṁ, ahaṁ
puṇa na puvvāṇurāga - visarisaṁ ciṭṭhāmi । savvahā mama tumaṁ cēva bhattā । annahā
mariyavvaṁ । ēvaṁ sōūṇa parituṭṭhō vasaṁtadēvō । bhaṇiyā aṇēṇa piyaṁkarā - bhaddē !
ēttha vaiyarē mamāvi ēsa nicchaō ।
gaṁtuṁ piyaṁkarāē kahiyamiṇaṁ kēsarāi sā tuṭṭhā ।
tāṇa vivāhōvāyaṁ citaṁtāṇaṁ gayā diyahā ॥
tammi asaṁpattē cēva janna - jattā samāgayā tattha ।
tatō vasaṁtadēvō suē vivāhō tti nisuṇēi ||
sō dūmiō maṇēṇaṁ nayarāō niggaō gaō ya vaṇaṁ ।
ciṁtēi - ahō ! kērisamasuṁdaraṁ vilasiyaṁ vihiṇō ॥
nūṇaṁ maha pariṇayaṇē vihiya- pannā guruhiṁ annēṇa ।
sā pariṇāvijaṁtī karihī jīviya paricāyaṁ ॥

tō baṁdhiūṇa pāsaṁ asōga-rukkhassa sāhāē ॥
jā ubbaḍō appā vasaṁtadēvēṇa tattha uvvatahiṁ ।
baṁdhu vva tāva pattō kō vi narō taru- niujāō ॥

sāntaradānē kr̥tapuṇyakathānakam ।
tē anna-bhavē pāvaṁti sukkhamacchinnamājammaṁ ॥
jēsiṁ puṇa ditāṇaṁ narāṇa dāṇaṁmi aṁtaraṁ hōi ।

taṁ jahā-
asthi purī sāvatthī jattha viyaṁbhaṁta surayagā tuṁgā ।
kaṇayamayā pāsāyā sumēru - putta va rēhati ॥
tattha guṇa-saṁgaō saṁgau ti siṭṭhī mahā-dhaṇō āsi ।
sē baṁdhula tti bhajjā ramaṇō tti maṇōharō puttō ॥
puvva-kaya-kamma- pariṇāma - dōsaō tassa vihaḍiō vihavō ।
jamhā na paḍikhalijjai surāsurēhiṁ pi putra- kayaṁ ॥
kāṇa maō siṭṭhī anivvahatā ya baṁdhulā tattha ।
sulaha-jaliṁghaṇa-dhannaṁmi sālisīsē gayā gāmē ॥
akkhiya- niya-vr̥ttaṁtā gāmīṇa-jaṇēhiṁ abbhuvagayā sā ।
vihiō ya vaccha-vālō sē putō appiraṁ vacchē ॥
sō dāṇa-vasaṇī dēi dāragāīṇa lahaha jaṁ kiṁ pi ।
nahi atthi natthi ciṁtā payaha- udārāṇa saṁbhavai ||
aha māsa-khamaga-sāhū imassa diṭṭhipahamāgaō bāhiṁ ।
jāyā ya tammi bhattī tavēṇa raṁjijjai na kō vā ॥
annamma vāsarē ūsavō tti lōgēṇa pāyasaṁ raddhaṁ ।
taṁ jēmaṁtē ḍiṁbhē dahuṁ ramaṇō bhagai jaṇaṇiṁ ॥
viyarasu mamā vi pāyasamimā vi natthi tti nibharā rui ।
saṁpanna - dayāhiṁ pāḍivēsiyatthīhiṁ sā bhaṇiyā ॥
mā ruyasa pāyasaṁ raṁdhiūṇa ramaṇassa dēsu sigdhaṁ ti ।
tīsē samappiyāiṁ ca khīra - taṁdula - gula - ghayāī ॥
raddhaṁ ca pāyasaṁ tīi dāraō bhōyaṇatthamuvaviṭṭhō ।
ghaya - gula- pāyasa - bhariyaṁ tassa purō bhāyaṇaṁ ṭhaviḍaṁ ॥
aha baṁdhulā paviṭṭhā ghara - majjhē ittha avasarē pattō ।
dhammu vva muttimaṁtō sō bhikkhatthaṁ khamaga-sāhū ॥
ciṁtāmaṇī maha - karē caḍiō jaṁ āgaō muṇī gēhaṁ ।

parivāliūṇa rajjaṁ puvvāṇa tisahi lakkhāī ॥

jēhaṁ puttaṁ bharahaṁ sumaṁgalā - dēvi - aṁgaruhaṁ ||
takkhasilāi purīē bahalī - visayāvayaṁsa- bhūyāē ।
rajjaṁmi sunaṁdā-naṁdaṇaṁ ca ṭhaviūṇa bāhubaliṁ ॥
baṁgaṁga-magaha- kuṁkaṇa - kuṇāla - kuṁtala - avaṁti pamuhāṇa |
sēsa suyāṇaṁ dāūṇa sēsa - dēsāṇa sāmittaṁ ॥
surakaya-nikkhamaṇa - mahō cauhiṁ sahassēhiṁ saha nariṁdāṇaṁ ।
sāmannaṁ paḍivannō chuṭṭa tavēṇaṁ risaha sāmī ॥
bāhubali putta- sōmappahassa puttrēṇa varisa-pajaṁtē ।
sējaṁsēṇikkhurasaṁ dāum̐ pārāviō bhayavaṁ ॥
sāmī pavanna- mōṇō bahu-viha dēsēsu daṁsaṇēṇāvi ।
saṁjaṇai bhaddagattaṁ aṇāriyāṇaṁ pi viharaṁtō ॥
sō varisa - sahastē vaḍa- viḍavi-talaṁmi purimatāla - purē ।
khaviya - ghaṇaghāi - kammō uppāḍai kēvalaṁ nāṇaṁ ॥
aha āsaṇa - kaṁpāō muṇiūṇa jiṇiṁda - kēvaluppattiṁ ।
niya-niya parivāra - juyā surēsarā āgayā savvē ॥
cahu-viha- dēvēhiṁ kathaṁ sāla- ttaya suṁdaraṁ samōsaraṇaṁ ।
bhāvārivāra- vihuriya-jagattaya-ttāṇa- duggaṁ va ॥
tattha nisannō sāmī udaya- giriṁdē ravi vva puvva-muhō ।
paḍibiṁbāī surēhiṁ kayāī sēsāsu tisu disisu ॥
mahi - nihiya- niḍāla-yalā namiūṇa jiṇaṁ parāi bhattīē ।
savvē sura-nara- nivahā niya-niya-hāṇēsu uvaviṭṭhā ॥
ētthaṁtaraṁmi pattā paḍihāra - nivēiyā duvē purisā ।
jamaga- samagābhihāṇā bharaha - nariṁdassa pāsaṁmi ॥
jamagēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ purimatāla -pura-kāṇaṇaṁmi sagaḍa-muhē ।
lōyālōya-payāsaṁ pahuṇō nāṇaṁ samuppannaṁ ॥
samagēṇa puṇō bhaṇiyaṁ chakkhaṁḍa -mahī pasāhaṇa - sahāyaṁ ।
saṁpai āuha- sālāi cakka rayaṇaṁ samuppannaṁ ॥
pasaraṁta pamōya- bharō bharahō ciṁtai karēmi kiṁ pūyaṁ ।
tāyarasa sāhu - sārassa cakka rayaṇassa vā paḍhamaṁ ॥
aha phuriyaṁ hiyaē tassa kattha bhuvaṇābhayaṁkarō tāō।

kattha ca cakkaṁ saṁhāra-kāraṇaṁ pāṇi-cakkassa ॥
ghiḍī ! maē ajuttaṁ vimarisiyaṁ ahaha ! mōha - vivasō'haṁ ।

aha bharahō marudēviṁ jaṁpai dahuṁ samōsaraṇa - riddhiṁ ।
ammō ! taē ruyaṁtīi jaṁpiyaṁ maha purō ēvaṁ ॥

sīunha - vāya- tanhā chuhā- haō bhamai ēgāgī ॥
buttā maē puṇa tumaṁ maṇaṁ pi mā aṁba ! khēyamuccahasu ।
annassa tārisī nahi suyassa tē jārisī riddhī ॥
āsī na paccaō tē maha vayaṇē aṁba ! ēttiyaṁ kālaṁ ।
saṁpai pēccha surēhiṁ vihiyaṁ pahuṇō samōsaraṇaṁ ॥
pahu-vaṁdanāgayāṇaṁ suvvai tiyasāṇa jayajayārāvō ।
pēccha surā pahu-puraō dhuṇaṁti naccaṁti gāyaṁti ॥
jā dēvīē jāyā nīlī nayaṇēsu sāmi-sōēna ।
sā bharaha - vayaṇa-savaṇē āṇaṁda-jalēṇa avaṇīyā ॥

taddaṁsaṇa - harisa-vasēṇa jhanti sā tammayā jāyā ॥
tattō auvva-karaṇa - kamēṇa sā khavaga - sēṇimārūḍhā ।
kammāī aṭṭa jugavaṁ niṭṭaviḍaṁ kēvalaṁ lahai ॥
sā kari - khaṁdha gaya ciya siddhā aṁtagaḍa - kēvalō jāyā ।
taddēhamacciūṇaṁ khittaṁ tiyasēhiṁ khīrōē ॥

puttāṇaṁ paṁcasayāī satta nattuya - sayāī ca ॥
bhī - pamuhāō sāhuṇīō taha sāvayā bharaha- pamuhā ।

tē cunnakhēva putravaṁ bhayavaṁ gaṇahara - paē ṭhavai ॥

sura-
khitta-surahi-vāsō nivēsiō maṇimaē thālē ।

vīsamaha dēvachaṁdē suvanna - pāyāra - majjha gaē ॥

tammi kahaṇāu viraē niya-niya ṭhāṇē jaṇā jaṁti ॥
aha bhaviya vagga paḍibōhaṇatthamannattha vihariō bhayavaṁ ।
mōha - tamōha - nirōhaṁ sahassarassi vva kuṇamāṇō ॥

kiṁ majjha natthi ajjavi jaṁ ēsā dubbalā milāṇa-muhī ।

purisā bhaṇati - dēvassa asthi sakkssa va samaggaṁ ॥
navaraṁ visaya virattā pahu-pāsē āimē samōsaraṇē ।

ēvaṁ bhaṇiyā dūēhiṁ tē vi miliūṇa maṁtaṁti ॥

bharahō puṇa dappa- vasā amhē kāravai niya sēvaṁ ॥
tā kiṁ taṁ sēvāmō kiṁ vā juḍēṇa taṁ nirākaribhō ।
iya pucchiūṇa sāmiṁ jaṁ juttaṁ taṁ karīhāmō ॥
itthaṁtaraṁmi sāmī aṭṭhāvaya-pavvaē samōsariō ।
gaṁtūṇa imē taṁ paṇamiūṇa pucchaṁti putrvattaṁ ॥
bhayavaṁ jaṁpai sēvaha ēvaṁ siva- sukkha sāhagaṁ dhammaṁ ।
iṁdiya - suhaḍē tailukka - dujjaē jigaha jujjhēṇa ॥
kiṁ ca purā na niyattā jā tavhā tumha tiyasa - sukkhēhiṁ ।

aṁgāra - kasenē kavi gaō salila-dii- puḍhaṁ vēttuṁ ।
aṁgārānala-tavaṇāyavēhiṁ sē vaḍḍiyā tavhā ॥
sō piyai dii- puḍa - jalaṁ savvaṁ tēṇa vi atuh-taṇhō sō ।
suttō suviṇē giha-gaya-gaggari-naṁdā - jalaṁ piyai ॥

taha tumha sura- suhēhiṁ acchinnā chijjihī na rajjēṇa ।

kumārapālapratibōdhē
sō paṇamiṇa sāmiṁ kayaṁjalī dhamma- dēsaṇaṁ suṇai ।
dhamma- kahā - pajjaṁtē gahiya vaē baṁdhavē dahuṁ ॥
savisāya-maṇō ciṁtaha ghēttr̥ṇa maē imāṇa rajjāī ।
kiṁ sāhiyaṁ hahā ! mē visayāmisa-lālasā - buddhī ॥
baṁdhūhiṁ viṇā bhōē bhuṁjatōhaṁ dhuvaṁ garahaṇijō ।
hakkāriṇa kāē kāō vi hu bhakkhaē bhakkhaṁ ॥
jai puṇa maha punnēhiṁ ēē bhōē puṇō vi ginhati ।
tō bharahō pahu-pāsē bhōgēhiṁ nimaṁtaē baṁdhū ॥
bhāi pahū puhavīsara ! saralōsi sahōyarā imē tujjha ।
muttūṇa sayaṁ bhōē puṇa vi kimicchaṁti vataṁ va ॥
paṁcahiṁ sagaḍa - saēhiṁ bharahō āṇāviūṇa āhāraṁ ।
puṇa vi nimaṁtai savvē vi sāhuṇō, tō bhaṇai bhayavaṁ ॥
āhākammiyamiṇamāhaḍaṁ ca kappai nariṁda ! na muṇīṇaṁ ।
puṇaravi aka-akāriya- asaṇēṇa nimaṁtara bharahō ॥
bhāi bhayavaṁ na kappara imaṁ pi sāhūṇa rāya - piṁḍōti ।
iya pahuṇā paḍisiddhō bharahō jāō vilakkha-maṇō ॥
uvalakviḍaṁ vilakkhaṁ bharahaṁ pucchara surēsarō sāmiṁ ।
pasiūṇa kahasu bhayavaṁ ! avaggahō kahavihō hōṛa ॥
tō kahai tittha-nāhō avaggahō paṁcahā havai sakka ! |
suravai - cakki nivā-gāri - sāhu- saṁbaṁdhi - bhēēhiṁ ॥
hariṇā vr̥ttaṁ muṇiṇō viharaṁti avaggahaṁmi jē majjha ।
jiṇanāha ! aṇunnāō bhaē niyāvaggahō tēsiṁ ॥
ciṁtēi cakkavahī jai vi na gahiyaṁ muṇīhi maha kiṁpi ।
taha vi hu hōmi kayatthō niyayamavaggahamaṇunnaviuṁ ॥
tō pahu-puraō sakkō vva kuṇai cakkī avaggahāṇunnaṁ ।
pucchara hariṁ kimimiṇā kāyavvaṁ bhōyaṇēṇa maē ? ॥
aha vāgariyaṁ hariṇā guṇuttarāṇaṁ tumaṁ imaṁ dēhi ।
citaha cakkī gihiṇō guṇuttarā sāvayā majjha ॥
dāyavvamiṇaṁ tēsiṁ ti nicchiuṁ sāvagē bhaṇai cakkī ।
maha maṁdiraṁmi tubhē niraṁtaraṁ bhōyaṇaṁ kuṇaha ||

rājapiṇḍē bharatacatri - kathā |
karisaṇa vaṇijja -pamuhaṁ muṁcaha nicaṁ karēha sajjhāyaṁ ।
paḍhaha auvvaṁ nāṇaṁ ciṭṭhaha dhammēkka-kaya-cittā ॥
vajjaraha majjha puraō jiō tumaṁ vaṭṭaē bhayaṁ jamhā ।
tamhā māhaṇa māhaṇa taha cēva kuṇaṁti tē savvaṁ ॥
tavvayaṇaṁ suṇiuṁ sō ciṁtēi jiō ahaṁ kasāēhiṁ ।
tēhiṁ tō majjha bhayaṁ māhaṇihaṁ pāṇiṇō tattō ॥
hā ! pāvōhaṁ visaēhiṁ mōhiō iya khaṇaṁ suhaṁ jhāṇaṁ ।
hōi bharahassa pacchā puṇō vi sō sajjaē rajjē ॥
aha vinnavaṁti bharahaṁ suārā najjaē nahi visēsō ।
sāvaga asāvagāṇaṁ kuṇai parikkhaṁ bhaṇai bhara hō ॥
tē vihu vihiya parikkhē cakkaharō kāgiṇīē laṁcchēi ।
ēē rayaṇa-taya-bhūsiya tti rēhātigaṁ kāuṁ ॥
chaḍē chaṭṭhē māsē parikkhiyā kāgiṇīi kaya- ciṁdhā ।
bhuṁjaṁti, tayā māhaṇa bhaṇaṇāō māhaṇā jāyā ॥
iya guru-vāgariyaṁ bharaha - cariyamāyanniḍaṁ kuṇai rāyā ।
jai maha bhikkhā na muṇīṇa kappaē rāya - piṁḍī ti ॥
tattō bharahō vva ahaṁ pi bhōyaṇaṁ sāvagāṇa viyarēmi ।
guruṇā vr̥ttaṁ juttaṁ aṇusariḍaṁ uttama caritaṁ ॥
aha kārāvara rāyā kaṇa - kōṭṭhāgāra - ghaya- gharōvēyaṁ ।
sattāgāraṁ garuyāi bhūsiyaṁ bhōyaṇa - sahāē ।
tassāsannē rannā kāraviyā viyaḍa-tuṁga-varasālā ।
jiṇa dhamma-hatthi -sālā pōsaha -sālā avisālā ॥
tattha sirimāla -kula- naha - nisi - nāhō nēmiṇāga- aṁgaruhō ।
abhayakumārō sēṭṭhī kaō ahiṭṭhāyagō rannā ॥
itthaṁtaraṁmi kavi - cakkavaṭṭi - sirivāla- rōhaṇa - bhavēṇa ।
buhayaṇa- cūḍāmaṇiṇā payaṁpiyaṁ siddhavālēṇa ॥
dēva-guru- prayaṇa- parō parōvayārujaō dayā-pavarō ।
dakkhō dakkhinna-nihī saccō saralāsaō ēsō ॥
kiśca -
kṣitvā tōyanidhistalē maṇigaṇaṁ ratnōtkaraṁ rōhaṇō

kumārapālapratibōdhē
rēṇvāvr̥tya suvarṇamātmani dr̥ḍhaṁ baddhā suvarṇācalaḥ ।
kṣmāmadhyē ca dhanaṁ nidhāya dhanadō bibhyatparēbhyaḥ sthitaḥ
kiṁ syāttaiḥ kr̥paṇaiḥ samō'yamakhilā rthibhyaḥ svamarthaṁ dadat ॥
tā juttaṁ dēva ! kayaṁ tumaē jaṁ ittha dhamma-ṭhāṇaṁmi ।
abhayakumārō sēṭṭhī ēsō savēsarō vihiō ॥
ghaya - kūra - mugga- maṁḍaga- vaṁjaṇa- vaḍayāi-kaya- camakkāraṁ ।
sakkāra- puvvagaṁ sāvayāṇa sō bhōyaṇaṁ dēi ||
vatthāī pasatthāī kuṭuṁba-nitthāraṇatthamatthaṁ ca ।
ēvaṁ sattāgāraṁ kathaṁ nariṁdēśa jiṇa dhammē ॥
iti santrāgārava kavyatāyāṁ bharata kathā |
iya jīva dayā hē saṁsāra samuha saṁtaraṇa - sēuṁ ।
dāṇaṁ mōkkha-nidāṇaṁ kahiūṇa gurū bhaṇai ēvaṁ ॥
jīva-dayaṁ kāumaṇō maṇuō sīlaṁ nariṁda ! pālija ।
jamhā jiṇēhiṁ aṇiō sēhuṇa-sannāi jīva-vahō ।
ramaṇīṇa saṁgamē hōi mēhuṇaṁ taṁ dhaṇaṁ viṇā na havē ।
hōi ghaṇaṁ āraṁbhāō tattha puṇa natthi jīva-dayā ॥
agaṇiya- kajākajjā niraggalā galiya- ubhaya- lōya-bhayā ।
mēhuṇa- pasatta-cittā kiṁ pāvaṁ jaṁ na kuvvaṁ ti ॥
jalaṇō vi jalaṁ jalahī vi gōpayaṁ pavvaō vi sama-bhūmī ।
bhuyagō vi hōi mālā visaṁ pi amayaṁ susīlāṇa ॥
āṇaṁ tāṇa kuṇaṁti jōḍiya-karā dāsa vva savvē surā
māyaṁgā hi - jalaggi- sīha-pamuhā varhati tāṇaṁ vasē ।
hujjā tāṇa kuō vi nō paribhavō saggāpavagga- sirī
tāṇaṁ pāṇi-talaṁ uvēi vimalaṁ sīlaṁ na luṁpati jē ॥
vipraha tāṇa kittī lahaṁti tē sagga- mōkkha- sukkhāī ।
sīlaṁ saṁsaṁka- vimalaṁ jē sīlavaha vva pālaṁti ॥
taṁ jahā-
-
itthēva jaṁbudīvē bhāraha - vāsaṁmi vāsavapuraṁ va ।
kaya- vibuha - jaṇāṁ naṁdaṇapuramatthi vara-nayaraṁ ॥

śīlavratapālanē śīlavatīdr̥ṣṭāntaḥ ।
paḍiya - paḍivakkha-balō hari vva ari-maddaṇō tahiṁ rāyā ।
guṇa-rayaṇa-nihī rayaṇāyaru tti siṭṭhī tahiṁ asthi ॥
tassa sirīnāma - piyā rūva-guṇēṇaṁ siri vva paccakkhā |
tīē na atthi puttō tēṇa dr̥ḍhaṁ tammaē sēṭṭhī ॥
221
annayā bhaṇiō bhajjāē -ajautta ! atthi itthēva nayarujāṇē ajiya-
jiṇiṁda-maṁdira-duvāra - dēsē ajiyabalā dēvayā aputtāṇa puttaṁ, avittāṇa vittaṁ,
arajāṇa rajjaṁ, avijāṇa vijjaṁ, asukkhāṇa sukkhaṁ, acakkhūṇa cakkhu, sarō-
yāṇa rōya-kkhayaṁ dēha ēsā । kayaṁ sēṭṭhiṇā tīē ōvāiyaṁ । kamēṇa jāō puttō ।
tassa kayaṁ 'ajiyasēṇō tti nāmaṁ । jāō jiṇadhara gujjuō siṭṭhī । jaṇaya-
maṇōrahēhiṁ saha vaḍiō ajiyasēṇō । sivi vaya- kalā - kalāvō lāvanna-
lacchi - punnaṁ pavannō tārunnaṁ । tassa ya sayala - jaganbhahiē ruvāi - guṇē picchiūṇa
ciṁtiyaṁ sēṭṭhiṇā - jai ēsa maha naṁdaṇō niya-guṇāṇurūvaṁ kalattaṁ na lahai tā
imassa akayatthā guṇā ।
jaō-
--
sāmī avisēsannū aviṇīō pariyaṇō para-vasattaṁ ।
bhajā ya aṇaṇurūvā cattāri maṇassa sallāī ॥
itthaṁtarē āgaō ēgō vāṇiuttō। paṇamiūṇa siddhiṁ niviṭṭhō samīvē ।
puṭṭhō ya sēṭṭhiṇā vavahāra- sarūvaṁ । kahiyaṁ tēṇa savvaṁ । annaṁ ca, tuhāēsēṇa gaōhaṁ
kayaṁgalāē nayarīē । jāō mē jiṇadatta - siṭṭiṇā samaṁ vavahārō । nimaṁtiō
'haṁ tēṇa bhōyaṇatthaṁ । diṭṭhā maē taggihē caṁdakaṁtēṇaṁ vayaṇēṇaṁ paōmarāēhiṁ hattha-
pāēhiṁ pavālēṇaṁ aharēṇaṁ dippamāṇēhiṁ rayaṇēhiṁ rayaēṇaṁ niyaṁvēṇaṁ suvannēṇaṁ aṁgēṇaṁ
mayaṇa- mahārāya bhaṁḍāra - maṁjūsa vva saṁcāriṇī ēgā kannagā । puṭṭhō maē siṭṭī kā
ēsa tti । siṭṭiṇā vr̥ttaṁ bhadda ! maha vūyā - misēṇa muttimaī ēsā ciṁtā ।
jaō-
kiṁ laṭṭha lahihī varaṁ piyayamaṁ kiṁ tassa saṁpajihī
kiṁ lōyaṁ sasurāiyaṁ niya-guṇa-ggāmēṇa raṁjissaē ।
kiṁ sīlaṁ paripālihī pasavihī kiṁ puttabhēvaṁ dhuvaṁ
ciṁtā muttimaī piūṇa bhavaṇē saṁvaṭṭaē kannagā ॥
ēsā ya sarīra-suṁdarima- daliya - dēva- ramaṇī-maḍappā aṇappa-guṇa-sōhiyā
hipāhiya- vicāra - kusalā salāhaṇija - sīlā sīlamai tti guṇa-niṣpanna nāmā

kumārapāla pratibōdhē

[ tr̥tīya:
bālattaṇaō vipuvva-kaya-sukaya-vasēṇa sauṇa ruya pajjaṁtāhiṁ kalāhiṁ sahīhiṁ
va paḍivannā । imīē aṇurūvaṁ varaṁ alahaṁtassa mēṁ acaṁtaṁ ciṁtā । aō maē ēsā
viciṁta tti vr̥ttā । maē bhaṇiyaṁ siṭṭi ! mā saṁtappa, atthi naṁdaṇapurē rayaṇāyara-
siṭṭiṇō visi - ruvāi - guṇō, puttō ajiyasēṇō sō tuha dhūāē aṇuruvō varō
tti । jiṇadattēṇa vr̥ttaṁ bhadda ! tunaē mē mahaṁta ciṁtā samuha - maggassa pavara- varō-
vaēsa-bōhitthēṇa nitthārō kaō tti bhaṇiūṇa tēṇa ajiyasēṇarala sīlamaī
dāu pēsiō jiṇasēharō niya-puttō bhaē samaṁ । sō ihāgaō ciṭṭhai । tā jahā
juttāisa siṭṭhī । juttaṁ kathaṁ tumaē tti bhaṇiūṇa hakkārāviō jiṇasēharō
siṭṭiṇā । sagōravaṁ dinnā tēṇa ajiyasēṇassa sīlamaī । ajiyasēṇēṇāvi tēṇēva
saha gaṁtr̥ṇa kayaṁgalāē pariṇīyā sīlamaī । ghittr̥ṇa taṁ āgaō sa-nayaraṁ aji-
yasēṇō । bhuṁjaē bhōē | annayā majjha-ratē ghaḍaṁ vittr̥̄ṇa gihāō niggayā
sīlamaī । kittiya - vēlāē āgayā dihā sasurēṇa । ciṁtiyaṁ nūṇaṁ ēsā kusīla
tti gōsē gahiṇī- samakkhaṁ vr̥ttō pattō vattha ! tuhēsā ghariṇī kusīlā, jaō
ajja majjha-rattē niggaṁtr̥̄ṇa katthavi gayā āsi, tā ēsā na jujjai
gihē dhariḍaṁ ।
jaō-
ghaṇa-rasa- vasaō ummagga- gāmiṇī bhagga-guṇa-dumā kalusā ।
mahilā dō vi kulāī kūlāī nai vva pāḍēi ॥
tā parāṇēmi ēvaṁ pii-haraṁ । puttrēṇa vr̥ttaṁ - tāya ! jaṁ juttaṁ taṁ karēsu ।
bhaṇiyā bahuyā - bhaddē ! āgaō 'sīlavaī sīgdhaṁ pēsijjasu 'tti tuha jaṇaya-
saṁdēsaō । tā calasu jēṇa tumaṁ sayaṁ parāṇēmi । sā vi ' rayaṇi-niggamaṇēṇa
mamaṁ kusīlaṁ saṁkamāṇō ēvamāisai sasurō, picchāmi tāva ēvaṁ pitti ciṁti-
ūṇa caliyā rahārūḍhēṇa siṭṭiṇā samaṁ । vacaṁtō sēṭṭhī pattō nahaṁ । sēṭṭiṇā
vr̥ttā vahū - pāṇahāō muttūṇa naī ōyarasu । tīē na mukkāō tāō । sēṭṭiṇā
ciṁtiyaṁ aviṇīya tti । aggaō dihaṁ paḍhama-vattā - pannaṁ accaṁta - phaliyaṁ mugga-
khēttaṁ । sēṭhṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ - ahō ! suphaliyaṁ mugga-khēttaṁ । savva-saṁpayā khētta-
sāmiṇō । tīē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvamēyaṁ, jai na khaḍaṁ ti । sēṭṭhiṇā ciṁtiyaṁ akkhayaṁ
pēkkhaṁtī vikhaddhaṁ ti akkhaha । aō asaṁbaddha - palāviṇī ēsā । gaō ēgaṁ
samiddha-pamuiya jaṇa saṁkulaṁ nagaraṁ । sēṭṭiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ ahō ! rammattaṇaṁ imassa ।
tīē bhaṇiyaṁ jai na uvvasaṁ ti । sēṭṭiṇā ciṁtiyaṁ ullaṁṭha bhāsiṇī imā ।

=== Kumara1output-223-to-223.json ==========================
prastāva: ]
śīlavratapālanē śīvalatīdr̥ṣṭāntaḥ ।
223
aggaō gacchaṁtēṇa sēṭṭhiṇā diṭṭhō parūḍhāṇēga-ppahārō paharaṇa karō kula-puttaō ।
sēṭṭiṇā vr̥ttaṁ - ahō ! sūrō ēsa purisō । bahuē vr̥ttaṁ asthi tāva kuhiō ।
sēṭṭiṇā ciṁtiyaṁ kiṁ na sūrō jō satthēhiṁ kuhijjai, paraṁ ajutta-jaṁpirī imā |
gaō aggaō naggōha-talē vīsaṁtō sēṭṭhī । vahū uṇa naggōha-cchāyaṁ chaḍḍiūṇa
ṭhiyā dūrē । sēṭṭiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ acchasu chāyāē, na tattha ṭhiyā । sēṭṭhiṇā
ciṁtiyaṁ savvahā vivarīya tti । pattō gāma mēkaṁ । bahuē vr̥ttō sēṭṭhī, ēttha asthi
mē māulagō taṁ jāva pēcchāmi tāva tubhē paḍivālēha tti gayā sā majjhē ।
diṭṭhā māulagēṇa sasaṁbhramaṁ bhaṇiyā vacchē ! kattha patthiyāsi ? । tīē bhaṇiyaṁ-
sasurēṇa saha piiharaṁ patthiyamhi । tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kattha tē sasurō ? । tīē vr̥ttaṁ
bāhiṁ cihna | gaṁtr̥̄ṇa māulēṇa hakkāriō sāyaraṁ sēṭṭhī । sakasāu tti aṇi-
cchaṁtō vi nīō nibbaṁdhēṇa gēhaṁ । bhōyaṇaṁ kāūṇa āgaō bāhiṁ । majjhaṇha-
samaō tti vīsamiō rahanbhaṁtarē । sīlamaī vi nisannā raha cchāyāē । ētthaṁ-
tarē karīra - tthaṁbāvalaṁbī puṇō puṇō vāsaē vāyasō । bhaṇiyaṁ aṇāē - arē !
kāya ! kiṁ na thakkasi karayaraṁtō ।
ēkkē dunnaya jē kayā tēhiṁ nīhariya gharassa ।
bījā dunnaya jai karauṁ tō na milauṁ piyarassa ॥
suyamiṇaṁ sēṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyā sā-cacchē! kimēvaṁ jaṁdasi ? bahuē bhaṇiyaṁ
na kiṁci । sēṭṭhiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ - kahaṁ na kiṁci । vāyasamuddisiūṇa 'ēkkē dunnaya '
tti jaṁ paḍhiyaṁ taṁ sāhippāyaṁ । bahūē vr̥ttaṁ - jai ēvaṁ tā suṇēu tāō ।
sōrubha-guṇēṇaṁ chēya-gharisaṇāīṇi caṁdaṇaṁ lahai ।
rāga- guṇēṇaṁ pāvai khaṁḍaṇa - kaḍhaṇāī maṁjiṭṭhā ॥
ēvaṁ mamāvi guṇō sattū saṁjāō । jaō --sayala - kalā - sirōmaṇi-bhūyaṁ
sauṇa rūyaṁ ahaṁ suṇēmi । taō aikaṁta-dina- rayaṇīē sivāē vāsaṁtīē
sāhiyaṁ, jahā – naīē pūrēṇa vubbhamāṇaṁ maḍayaṁ kaḍḍiūṇa sayaṁ āharaṇāṇi
giṇhasu । mama bhakkhaṁ taṁ khivasu । imaṁ sōūṇa gayāhaṁ vēttūṇa ghaḍagaṁ । taṁ hiyaē
dāūṇa paviṭṭhā nahaṁ । kaḍḍiyaṁ maḍayaṁ । gahiyāṇi ābharaṇāṇi । khittaṁ sivaṁ
sivāē | āgayā ahaṁ gihaṁ । ābharaṇāṇi ghaḍaē khiviūṇa nikhiyāṇi khōṇīē
ēvaṁ ēkka- dunnayassa pabhāvēṇa pattā ēttiyaṁ bhūmiṁ । saṁpayaṁ tu vāsaṁtō vāyasō
kahaha, jahā — ēyassa karīra - tthaṁbassa hēṭṭhā dasa- suvaṇṇa- lakkha-ppamāṇaṁ nihāṇa-
masthi ttaṁ ghēttūṇa mama karaṁbayaṁ dēsu ti । imaṁ sōūṇa sahasā uḍiō sēṭṭhī

=== Kumara2output-1-to-1.json ==========================
224
kumārapālapratibōdhē
[ tr̥tīya:
bhaṇai - vacchē ! sacamēyaṁ ? bahūē jaṁpiyaṁ— kiṁ aliyaṁ jaṁpijjaē tāya - pāyāṇaṁ
puraō | ahavā hatthatthē kaṁkaṇē kiṁ dappaṇēṇaṁ ti nihālēu tāō । taō tatthēva
ṭhiō sēṭṭhī gahiyaṁ nihāṇaṁ rayaṇīē । ahō ! muttimaṁtī imā lacchitti jāya
bahu-māṇō vahuṁ rahē ārōviūṇa niyattō sēṭṭī । pattō naggōhaṁ । pucchaē vahuṁ-
kiṁ na tumaṁ imassa chāyāē ṭhiyā ? bahūē akkhiyaṁ - rukkha mūlē ahi-daṁsāi-
bhayaṁ, cirāsaṇē cōrāi bhavaṁ, hēṭṭaō kāga-bagāi- viṭṭhā paḍaṇa-bhayaṁ, dūra-ṭṭhiyāṇaṁ
tu na savvamēyaṁ । puṇō puṭṭhē sēṭṭhiṇā sūramuddissa - atthi tāva kuṭṭiō tti ta
jaṁpiyassa kō paramatthō ? tīē vr̥ttaṁ - nahi kuṭṭiō tti sūrō, kiṁtu paḍhamaṁ jō
na paharai । nagaraṁ dahūṇa sēṭṭhiṇā vr̥ttaṁ -kahamēyamuvvasaṁ ? tīē vr̥ttaṁ - jattha
natthi sayaṇō sāgaya-parivatti kāraō taṁ kahaṁ vasimaṁ । khēttaṁ daṭṭhaṇa sēṭṭhiṇā
puṭṭhē – kahamēyaṁ khaddhaṁ ti ? tīē vr̥ttaṁ vavaharagāō davvaṁ vuṭṭīē kahiūṇa khētta-
sāmiṇā khaḍaṁ ti khaddhaṁ | naī dahūṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sēṭṭiṇā - kiṁ taē naīē pāṇahāō
na mukkāō ? tīē jaṁpiyaṁ— jala- majjhē kīḍa - kaṁṭagāi na dīsaha tti । pattō
gihaṁ sēṭṭhī । daṁsiyāī tīē mahi-nihittāharaṇāī । tuṭṭēṇa sēṭṭhiṇā bhajāē
suyassa savvaṁ kahiūṇa kathā sā ghara - sāmiṇī ।
aha jīviyassa taralattaṇēṇa paṁcattamuvagaō sēṭṭhī ।
nihaṇaṁ gayā sahayarī sirī vi chāya vva tavvirahē ॥
ajiyasēṇō vi jipa-dhamma-parō kālaṁ bōlēi । annayā arimaddaṇa-nariṁdō
ēgūṇa-paṁca-sayāṇaṁ maṁtīṇaṁ pahāṇaṁ maṁtiṁ maggēmāṇō nāyaraē pattēyaṁ pucchai-
bhō ! bhō ! jō maṁ pāēga pahaṇai tassa kiṁ kīrai ? tē vi avinnāya - paramatthā
jaṁpati - dēva ! kimannaṁ sārōrō niggahō kīraha । pucchiō ajiyasēṇō । tēṇa
vr̥ttaṁ - paribhāṣiūṇa kahissaṁ । gihāgaraṇa pucchiyā tassuttaraṁ sīlavaī । tīē
caḍavviha- buddhi-juttāē jaṁpiyaṁ jahā -- tassa mahaṁtō sakkārō kīrai । bhantuṇā
bhaṇiyaṁ -kahamēyaṁ ? tīē uttaṁ-vallahāē viṇā natthi annassa rāyāṇaṁ pāēṇa
pahaṇēmi ti citiuṁ pi jōggayā, kiṁ puṇa pahaṇiuṁ । taō gaō sō rāya-
sahāē, kahiyaṁ puvvr̥ttaṁ । tuṭṭō rāyā । kaō aṇēṇa savva-maṁtīṇa sirōmaṇī
sō । annayā rannō viutthiō sīharahō paccaṁtō rāyā । tassōvariṁ calaṁta-maya-
gala-maya-jalāsāra - sitta-mahi-yalō tarala-turaya-khurukkhaya-khōṇi-rēṇu-ghaṇa-
paḍala - pūriya- nahaṁgaṇō saṁcaraṁta-raha- dhavala dhayavaḍāyā valāya-paṁti-maṇōharō gahi-
khajjirāujja-gajji-jajjariya- baṁbhaṁḍa-bhaṁḍōyarō nava- pāusu vva caliō rāyā ।

tannāmāī ghaḍē pattarasu lihiūṇa chūḍhāī ॥
nīharai jassa nāmaṁ paivarisaṁ tēṇa cittiyacvō sō ।
ēvaṁ vaccai kālō aha kōsaṁbīē nikkhaṁtō ॥
cittayara - dāraō tattha āgaō citta - sikkhaṇa-nimittaṁ ।
sō ya hiō ēkkāē gēhē cittayara thērīē ॥
jāyā tapputtrēṇaṁ saha mēntī tattha tammi varisaṁmi ।
thērī suyassa nāmaṁ viṇiggayaṁ tō ruyaha thērī ॥
kiṁ rōyasi tti iyarēṇa pucchiyā kahai jakkha-vr̥ttaṁtaṁ ।
niya putta-vārayaṁ taha pāhuṇaō bhaṇai mā ruyasu ॥
ciṭṭhala tuha putō jakvamēyamahamēva cittahassāmi ।
thērī jaṁpai maha vaccha ! naṁdaṇō hōsi kiṁ na tumaṁ ॥
cittēmi tahavi jakkhaṁ acchaō maha baṁdhavō suhēṇaṁ ti ।
vōttūṇa kuṇai chaṭuṁ sō rahāō caṁdaṇa-vilintō ॥
sui-vattha- niyatthaṁgō aṭṭha-guṇa-paḍaṁcalēṇa baddha-muhō ।
nava-vannaēhiṁ nava- kucaēhiṁ sō cittaē jakkhaṁ ॥
namiūṇa paṁjalī sō jaṁpai niggaha-aṇuggaha-samattha ! |
khamasu sura- ppiya bhayavaṁ ! avaraddhaṁ jaṁ maē kiṁpi ॥
iya bhattīē tuṭṭhō jakkhō jaṁpaṛa varaṁ varasu bhadda ! |
sō bhaṇai jakkha ! tuṭṭōsi jai tumaṁ tā paraṁ ēntō ॥
tumaē viṇāsiyavvō na kō vi, jakkhō payaṁpaē ēvaṁ

śīlē tārākathānakam ।
vasaṇa-dasā pattā vi hu jē paripālaṁti sīlamakalaṁkaṁ ।
ubhaya-bhavubbhava-sukkha bhāgiṇō huṁti tāra vva ॥
taṁ jahā -
atthi sayalāmarahiyā nayarī vāṇārasī sura-puri vva ।
cōjaṁ vasaṁti jīē na kē vi lōyā avajjakarā ॥
sēṭṭhī puraṁdarō tattha asthi atthāha-attha- vitthārō ।
suṁdara - dēhā sura-suṁdari vva sē suṁdarī bhajjā ॥
kaya-sayala - jaṇāṇaṁdō caṁdō caṁdu vva naṁdaṇō tēsiṁ ।
racchuga-vaṇiṇō dhūyā tārā nāmēṇa sē ghariṇī ॥
tīē puraō rūvēṇa rēhaē kiṁkari vva kāma - piyā |
para- purisa - nivitti-vayaṁ paḍivannaṁ tīê gurupāsē ॥
caṁda - piyāē tārāi rōhiṇīē buhō vva atthi suō ।
pallaviya - lōya- lōyaṇa - pariōsō saṁkhacūḍō tti ॥
anna- diṇē cauhaṭṭē diṭṭhā caṁdēṇa kannagā ēkkā |
dāūṇa taṇaṁ sīsē niya-piuṇā vikkiṇijjaṁtī ॥
accaṁta - maṇaharā kā ima tti caṁdēṇa pucchiyā mittā ।
tē biṁti daridda-diō ēyaṁ vikkiṇai niya-dhūyaṁ ॥
mittā bhaṇati ghittuṁ ghariṇī kijjaḍa imā surūvanti ॥
tēṇuttaṁ hariṇacchī racchuga-dhūya tti maha ghariṇī ॥
tāhaṁ kimēyamicchāmi baṁbhaṇiṁ kiṁ tu iṇamajuttaṁ ti ।
dēmi dayāē mulaṁ imassa jaṁpaṁti tō mittā ॥
pavaṇuḍuya-dhaya- caṁcalaha vihavaha ēttiu sāru ।
vasaṇa - mahannava - nivaḍiyaha jaṁ kīrai uvayāru ॥
akaya-vvaō na sōhai vihavō vivō vva aṁgaṇā - nivahō ।
kattha vi apatta-bhōgō suvanna tārunnaō jai vi ॥
tō pucchiō imīē mulaṁ kiṁ baṁbhaṇō bhaṇai lakkhaṁ ।
muhayāi giraha lakkhaṁ karijja mā puṇa vi tumamēvaṁ ॥
iya jaṁpiūṇa caṁdō diyassa diṇāra- lakkhamappēi ।
jaṁpai bhaṭṭō duhaṁ pi bhōyaṇaṁ dēsu amha gihē ॥
lakkhaṁ lahiuṁ pi ahō sō maggaha bhōyaṇaṁ vigaya- lajjō ।

taṁ sōuṁ sā tuṭṭhā suvanna thālēsu dēi duhaṁ pi ।
ghayasāli-dāli-mōyaga - dahi-duḍa-ppamuhamāhāraṁ ॥
accatamatittēhiṁ piyarēhim̐ va tēhi bhuttamākaṁṭhaṁ ।

aha atthamiē sūrē bhuvarṇami viyaṁbhiē timira - pūrē ।

lakkhō puṇa dammāṇaṁ na viḍhappai varisa - lakkhē vi ॥
tō sēṭṭhī akkōsaha caṁdaṁ rē rē kuputta ! guṇa-mutta ! |
mēllasu nillakkhaṇa ! lakkha- dāṇa- dullaliya ! maha gēhaṁ ॥

tahā-
atthi maha ōsahi-dugaṁ guru dinnaṁ tattha nimmiē tilaē ।
ēkāē thī purisō bīyāē sō havāi itthī ॥
taṁ sīla- rakkhaṇa - kaē ginha tumaṁ giṇhaē taō tārā ।

caṁdō taṁ kuṇai paraṁ pāvai na tahāvihaṁ lāhaṁ ॥

gāruḍiō jaṁpaḍa saṁkhacūra ! tuha baccha ! jaṇaōhaṁ ॥
sō bhai na majjha piyā tumaṁ jaō kasiṇa - vanna - dēhō si ।
kaṇaya-cchavī piyā mē tā daṁsaha caṁdarūvaṁ sō ॥
taṁ dahuṁ parituṭṭhō puttō caṁdassa caḍai ucchaṁgē ।
tārā vi vihiya maṇā jaṁpai piyayama ! kimēyaṁ ti ॥
sō bhāi pōya bhaṁgē phalaga - vilaggō vilaṁghium̐ jalahiṁ ।
pattō mhi āsamaṁ tattha tāvasō bhaṇai maṁ dahaṁ ॥
dinnō diyassa lakkhō jamsa taē sō ahaṁ gahiya- dikkhō ।
vasaṇa- vaḍiyassa tuha kiṁ karēmi uciyaṁ ti tēṇa taō ॥
dinnō gāruḍa maṁnō rūva parāvattiṇī tahā vijjā ।
tō gāruḍiō hōuṁ pattō mhi tumaṁ gavēsaṁtō ॥
ēyassa imā bhalā imō ya puttu tti jāṇaē rāyā ।
tārāi ruva - sīlēhiṁ vimhiō ciṁtaē ēvaṁ ॥
dhannā ēsā jā mīlamujjalaṁ vahaha vasaṇa - pattā vi ।
ahamō ahaṁ tu ēkkō jō para mahilā hilāsa - parō ॥
hā ! kaha nillajō'haṁ jaṇassa daṁsēmi attaṇō vayaṇaṁ ।
tō gaṁtuṁ guru- pānē jiṇa dikkhaṁ giṇhaē rāyā ॥
tagguṇa-raṁjiya-cittā caṁṁ kula dēvayā ṭhavai rajjē ।
sō jiṇa dhammaṁ kāuṁ tārā-sahiō gaō sugaī ॥
iti śīlē tārā - kathā |

[ tr̥tīya:

sēṭṭhī dhūyāi maṇaṁ suṇiuṁ taha jāṇiuṁ jiṇamuhāō ।
nayara - kula-ppamuhaṁ suṁdarassa taṁ jaṁpaē ēvaṁ ॥
suṁdara ! maha dhūyāē imīē saṁmōhaṇē sadapyassa |
sapparasa va kaṁdayassa pasama-dakkhō tumaṁ cēva ॥
tā pariṇēsu ēyaṁ । suṁdarēṇa suttaṁ--guru-yaṇāyattō ēsa atthō । sēṭṭhiṇā
vr̥ttaṁ -vaccha ! ēsa tē viṇaō kulīṇataṁ kahēi । gaccha niyāvāsaṁ । ahaṁ puṇa
patthuyatthē tuha jaṇaṇīē aṇunnaṁ gihissaṁ । taō lēhaṁ samappiūṇa pēsiyā

purisā jayaṁtīē । daṁsiō lēhō dhaṇasirīē । vāiō sō tīē jahā - bhaddē !
kaṁcanaurē kaṇayasārō sēṭṭhī tuha suyassa niya-dhūyaṁ dēha, jai tumaṁ aṇumannasi ।
dhaṇasirīē bhaṇiyaṁ kō kallāṇē virōhō । jayasuṁdarī- sammaēṇa samappiō
tēsiṁ paḍilēhō । tēhiṁ gaṁtr̥̄ṇa daṁsiō sēṭṭhissa ।
jahā-
savvattamō tumaṁ suṁdarassa jai dēsi dēsu niya kannaṁ ।
bhavaṇaṁ pavisaṁtīē siriē kō jhaṁpa dēi ॥
taō sēṭṭhiṇā taṁ daṁsiūṇa pariṇāviō kaṇayasuṁdaraṁ suṁdarō । niya-nayaraṁ
gaṁtu kāmō vi sō āsannō pāusō tti ṭhiō tatthēva । patthiyā kē vi satthiyā ।
tattha mē jaṇaṇi ghariṇīṇaṁ imāṇi appējasu tti bhaṇiūṇa suṁdarī dāmōyara-
vippassa samappaē satta rayaṇāī । sō vi pattō jayaṁtīē । lōbha-dōsaō tēṇa
avalattāī tāī । anna- vaṇiēṇa apiō dāmōyara- pāsāō satta rayaṇāī
ghēttavvāiṁ ti lēhō । taṁ ghēttūṇa gayā dāmōyara - pāsaṁ dhaṇasirī । daṁsiūṇa lēhaṁ
maggiō sō rayaṇāṇi । tēṇa vr̥ttaṁ na mama hatthē pēsiyāṇi, ēsa puṇa kaō
kēṇāvi kūḍa - lēhō । āgayā gihaṁ dhaṇasirī bhaṇiyā bahuyā -bacchē ! caliya-
cittō baṁbhaṇō, tā kassa vi pahāṇa- purisamma kahiūṇa ginha rayaṇāṇi । jaṁ
aṁbā āṇavē ttittr̥ṇa bhuttuttaraṁ gayā sēṭṭhi samīvaṁ jayasuṁdarī । kahiō tassa
rayaṇa - vr̥ttaṁtō| tēṇāvi tīē rūva-luḍēṇa bhaṇiyā sā-bhaddē ! jai maē saha
ēkkasō vi visaē sēvēsi tō tē kajjaṁ karēbhi । tīē vr̥ttaṁ - jai ēvaṁ tā jā-
miṇī- puḍhama-jāmē āgaṁtavvaṁ ti । gayā purōhiya-pāsē । tassa vi sēṭṭhi - sarisō
samullāvō । vīya- jāmē āgaṁtavvaṁ ti । gayā maṁti-sagāsaṁ । sō vi purōhiēṇēva
pāḍhiō । taṁ caiva jaṁpai taiya- jāmē ijjasu ti bhaṇiūga gayā rannō pāsē । rannā
vitaṁ caiva vr̥ttaṁ, cauttha- jāmē jāmiṇīē sāmiṇā āgaṁtavvaṁ ti bhaṇiūṇa
gayā niya- gēhaṁ । sāhiō sāsuyāē tavvuttaṁtō । jattha kāraṇa- purisā vi ēri-
sā tattha kērisī rayaṇāsā । vahuē vr̥ttaṁ-- atthi cau- disa-ṭṭhiya- purisa - pamāṇā
ca - kōṇā maṁjūsā । sā rittī kāūṇa gihēga - dēsē muccala । sāsuyāē tahēva kayaṁ ।
sajjiyaṁ jayasuṁdarī maṁdiraṁ । nisāē viṣphuraṁtē mōhē vva vihiya- diṭṭi - paḍirōhē
timirōhē āgaō sēṭṭhī । paviṭṭhō bhavaṇabhaṁtaraṁ । kayaṁ tīē calaṇa - sōhaṇāi |

risiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ naravara ! na dēvayā māṇusī ēsā ॥
kahō jaṁpai kiṁ māṇusīi saṁbhavai ērisaṁ rūvaṁ ।

rāmēṇa saha rahārūḍhō sō pattō kuṁḍiṇīē paṁcāṇaṇō vva kāṇaṇē nibhaō
ciṭṭhaha । taṁmi diṇē ruppiṇī piucchāē bahu-dhāī - buḍḍha-nārī- parigayā nāgāi-
pūyaṇatthaṁ gayā ujjāṇē । kāūṇa nāga-pūyaṁ pūēisuṁ iṁdāṇī- pamuha - dēvēsu kahiya
carēhiṁ ēyāsiṁ jahā pattā ēē rāma kēsavā । taō rahāō uyariūna kaṇhēṇa
abhivāiyā piucchā । bhaṇiyā ya ruppiṇī-
kaṇhō haṁ tujjha kaē ihāgaō, tō samīhasē jai maṁ ।
tā āruha rahamēyaṁ hiyaē puṇa putrvamārūḍhā ॥
piucchā aṇunnāyā kaṇhēṇa ārōviyā rahaṁ ruppiṇī । ēsā ruppiṇī
kēṇāvi nijaiti pariyaṇēṇa kaō kōlāhalō । taṁ sōūṇa miliō bahuō
lōgō । bhaṇiō sō kaṇhēṇa-gaṁtūṇa kahēha ruppiṇō, tuha bhaiṇī kaṇhēṇa ni-
jaha, jai asthi kāvi sattī tā mēllāvasu tti bhaṇiūṇa āūriyā rāma- kaṇhēhiṁ
palaya-kāla-ghaṇa- ghōsāṇukāriṇā sarēṇa kaya-asaṁkha -

turaṁgāṇaṁ saṭṭhīē sahassēhiṁ rahāṇaṁ bahūhiṁ lakkhēhiṁ pāikkāṇaṁ pariyariyā ruppisa -
supālā । laggā aṇumaggēṇaṁ rāma- kaṇhāṇaṁ । tē āgacchaṁtē dahūṇa bhaubbhaṁta-hi-

tumhē puṇa sēna- rahiyā । tā tumha saṁgamaṁ vihalaṁ va takkēmi tti kaṁpai mē hiyayaṁ ।

[ tr̥tīyaḥ
mukkāī nāḍayāī rayaṇīē buddhēṇa tittāī tāī bhakkhiūṇa mayā kammavasēṇa ।
jāyā imassa vipparasa puttā । karisagō vi kālēṇa maō jāō niya- suhāē
naṁdaṇō । jāī sariūṇa kahaṁ niya-taṇayaṁ jaṇayaṁ sunhaṁ vā jaṇaṇi jaṁpēmi ti
sūyattaṇaṁ pavatō । jai natthi paccaō, tō sadēha taṁ mūyaṁ jēṇa savvamēyaṁ sāhai ।
ō vāharāviō mūō bhaṇiō sō muṇiṇā ।
rāyā vi hōi bhicō bhicō vi narēsarattaṇaṁ lahai ।
māyā vi hōi bhajjā bhajjā vi hu hōi māyati ॥
jaṇaō vi hōi taṇaō taṇaō vi hu ēttha jāyaē jaṇaō ।
suhāvi hōi māyā māyā vi hu hōi sunha tti ॥
tā vaccha ! saṁsāra - sarūvamēyaṁ paribhāviūṇa muttūṇa lajjaṁ kahēsu
attaṇō puvva bhavaṁ । sō vi saharisō lōyassa niya- puvva-bhavaṁ sāhai । saṁvi-
gga-maṇō muṇi-pāsē pavvaiō pāmarō । tē vi diya-dārayā siyālā baṁbhaṇā
jāyatti uvahasiyā avivēgiṇā lōēṇa । vilakkha-cittā kōvamuvvahaṁtā
rayaṇīē khagga- vagga hatthā vahatthaṁ sāhūṇaṁ āgayā ujjāṇaṁ । thaṁbhiyā sumaṇa-
jakkhēṇa । pabhāē diṭṭhā khīliyā lōgēṇa । muṇiya- vr̥ttaṁtā āgayā tēsiṁ
māyā- piyarō । akkhiyaṁ jakkhēṇa muṇi-māraṇujjayā imē maē ēvaṁ kayā ।
tō jai jiṇadhammaṁ paḍivajaṁti tā millēmi, na annahā । tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ
dukkarō sāhu-dhammō sāvaga-dhammaṁ puṇa karissāmō । ēvaṁ karēha tti bhaṇi-
ūṇa mukkā tē jakkhēṇa । gahiyaṁ sāvagattaṁ bhāvaō suēhiṁ sāhu- samīvē, na
uṇa jaṇaṇi-jaṇaēhiṁ । kālēṇa agginūi-vāubhūiṇō mariūṇa samuppannā
sōhammē paṁca - paliōvamāū dēvā । taō cuyā hatthiṇāurē arihadāsamsa
sāvayassa punnabhadda- māṇibhadda-nāmāṇō jāyā naṁdaṇā । jiṇasāsaṇāṇurattā
kuṇaṁti sāvagattaṁ । annayā mahiṁda cāva-cavalaṁ jāṇiūṇa jīviyaṁ mahiṁda-muṇi-
samīvē pavannō arihadāsō dikvaṁ । tassa suyā rahārūḍhā sāhu-namaṇatthaṁ
patthiyā । pēcchati maggē suṇahī-saṇāhaṁ caṁḍālaṁ । jāō tēsiṁ taduvari si-
hō । gayā sāhu- samīvē । vaṁdiūṇa pucchaṁti sāhuṁ- bhayavaṁ ! kiṁ kāraṇaṁ jēṇa
amhāṇaṁ suṇahiṁ caṁḍālaṁ ca daṭṭhūṇa siṇēha - nivbharaṁ maṇaṁ jāyaṁ । sāhuṇā kahiyaṁ-
tumbhē aggibhūi-vāubhūī pubva-bhavē huṁtā । tumha puṇa māyā-piyarō akaya-dhammā
yā saṁsāraṁ hiṁḍiūṇa māyā suṇahī jāyā piyā puṇa ēsō sōvāgō ।
laō tē saṁjāya - jāisaraṇā saṁsāra - sarūvaṁ sumaraṁtā gayā gēhaṁ । tēhiṁ kahiūṇa

tēsiṁ rai - vigdha kaē kumarēṇaṁ vāiyā bhērī ॥

kari-turaya-rahārūḍhēhi suhaḍa - lakkhēhi pariyariō ॥

garuya-gaya-kvaṁdha-gaō nīharai maṇippabhō bāhiṁ ||
aha dhāriṇīi ajāi ciṁtiyaṁ jāva niravarāhāṇa ।

tapasi dharmmayaśōdharmmaghōṣa - kathā |
jīvāṇa hōi na khaō imāṇa baṁdhūṇa juddhēṇa ॥
tāva nivārēmi imē tattō jaṁpai maṇippabhaṁ ajjā ।
vaccha ! mamēgaṁ taṁ dēhi jēṇa jaṁpēmi kiṁ pi hiyaṁ ॥
taṁmi vinnē rannā rāyāṇaṁ bhaṇai dhāriṇī ajjā ।
kiṁ niya-sahōyarēṇaṁ samaṁ tumaṁ kuṇasi saṁgāmaṁ ॥
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ - bhayavai ! kahaṁ asacaṁ tumaṁ imaṁ bhaṇasi ।
tō dhāriṇīi kahiō savvō vihu niyaya- vr̥ttaṁtō ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ ca jai na pattiyasi vaccha ! pucchasu tumaṁ niyaya-jaṇaṇiṁ ।
taha pēccha raṭṭhavadvaṇa - nāmaṁkaṁ kaḍriḍaṁ muddē ॥
rāyā tava kāuṁ gaya-saṁkō bhaṇai jai vi sacamiṇaṁ ।
taha vi hu niyattamāṇō ajē ! lajjāmi ahamihi ॥
tō ajāē bhaṇiyaṁ ciṭṭha khaṇaṁ jāva uvasamāvēmi ।
tuha bhāyaraṁ pi tattō pattā ajjā duiya kaḍagaṁ ॥
sā jaṁpai paḍihāraṁ kārāvasu rāya - daṁsaṇaṁ majjha ।
sō kahai imaṁ rannō, rāyā jaṁpai pavēsēsu ॥
tēṇa vi pavēsiyā sā nivēsiyā āsaṇē nariṁdēṇa ।
dahūṇa pariyaṇō taṁ ciṁtiumēvaṁ samādattō ॥
ajjā ēsā dīsaha amhāṇaṁ sāmiṇīi sarisitti ।
sammaṁ nirūyamāṇō muṇai dhuvaṁ dhāriṇī ēsā ॥
tō paṇamiūṇa ajjaṁ rōyaṁtō pariyaṇō kahai rannō ।
aha jaṇaṇī khalu ēsā, ruyamāṇō namai taṁ rāyā ॥
pacchā niya-vr̥ttaṁtaṁ kahēi sā jaṁpara puṇō vi imaṁ ।
bhāyā tuhēsa rāyā tā viramasu vaccha ! jujjhāō ||
iya dhāriṇi ajjāē sahōyarā dō vi uvasamaṁ nīyā ।
tē pariōsa-vasēṇaṁ miliyā viyasaṁta-muha - kamalā ॥
ullasiya-siṇēhāṇaṁ duṇha vi baṁdhūṇa saṁgamē tēsiṁ ।
taṁ kiṁ pi suhaṁ jāyaṁ tailukkaṁ saṁkaḍaṁ jassa ॥

gandhaḥ srajāṁ bhrātr̥samāgamaśca ।

muṇi- aṁga-saṁgi-salilaṁ ravi vva timiraṁ harēi rōga-bharaṁ ।

sakkāīhiṁ vi dusaha muṇiṇō garimā-guṇēṇa garuyattaṁ ।

issariya-guṇēṇa puṇō cakkiṁda-siriṁ khamō kāuṁ ॥
sāhu- vasitta-guṇēṇaṁ pasamaṁ kūrō vi jaṁtuṇō jaṁti ।
appaḍighāyatta guṇēṇa sēla-majjhē vi kamai suṇī ॥

rūvēhiṁ kāmarūvittaṇēṇa pūrai jayaṁ pi muṇī ॥
ēgattha- vīyaō gaattha- bīyāim̐ jattha jāyaṁti ।
sā bīya- buddhi- riddhī saṁpajjai nicchiyaṁ muṇiṇō ॥
sā dharai kuṭṭa - buddhī kuṭṭē dhannaṁ va akkhayaṁ muttaṁ ।
ēga-payāu vi ginhai gaṁthaṁ pi payāṇusārī sō ॥

anna- nivai-pahāṇaṁ hi āgayaṁ āyaraṁti nivā ॥

pahu ! dēsu mamāēsaṁ jēṇa uvāyaṁ phalēṇa daṁsēmi ।

labdhiprakaṭa viṣṇukumāra kathā |
jēṇamhē givhāmō dikkhaṁ kammukkhaṇaṇa dakkhaṁ ॥
sō bhai tāya ! rajjē viṇhukumāraṁ ṭhavēsu maha jēhaṁ ।
patti vva vihiya bhattī tassāhaṁ hōmi juvarāō ||
bhai nivō ēsa maē bahupi bhaṇiō na givhaē rajjaṁ ।

tō kaya- mōṇō paumō rajjē cakkittaṇē ya ahisittō ।
paumuttarēṇa gahiyā viṇhukumārēṇa saha dikkhā ||
jaṇaṇi karāviya rahajattaṁ kāūṇa cakkiṇā nayarē ।
jiṇasāsaṇassa jaṇiyā samunnaī niya- kulassēva ॥
nagarāgara - gāmāisu kāraviyā tēṇa jiṇa-gihā garuyā ।

garuḍō vva bhramai gayaṇē jāō sōṇēga-satti- juō ॥
anna samayaṁmi hatthiṇapuraṁmi caṁdō vva tārayā variō ।
sō muṇi alaṁkiō kuṇai pāusa suvvayāyariō ॥
taṁ jāṇiūṇa namuī sumaraṁtō puvva- vēra-saṁbaṁdhaṁ ।

tumhē puṇa maṁ niṁdaha ahiṇaṁdaha na uṇa daṁsaṇēṇāvi ।

kumārapālapratibōdhē
tā maha rajjaṁ muṁcaha nihaṇissaṁ annahā tunbhē ॥
bhai gurū amha imō kappō ti na āgayā tumaṁ dahūṁ ।
niṁda kassa vi amhē na karēmō kiṁ puṇō tumha ॥
namuī jaṁpa kuḍō kiṁ bahuṇā ittha satta diṇa-uvariṁ ।
jō ciṭṭhissai tumhāṇa sō bhaē māriyavvōti ॥
iya jaṁpiuṁ gaō sō gurū bhaṇai bhō ! kimitya kāyavvaṁ ।
suṇiṇō kahēha tumhē niya-niya mai satti- aṇuruvaṁ ॥
tatthēkkō bhaṇai muṇī sahiṁ vacchara-sayāī vihiya-tavō ।
paumassa jēḍa-bhāyā viṇhu- muṇī maṁdarē asthi ||
sō uvasamihī ēvaṁ paumō vtra pahū imassa jō jamhā ।
naha- gamaṇa - satti juttō jō sō vaccau tamāṇēuṁ ॥
tō bhai muṇī ēkkō gaṁtuṁ santō mama tthi nāgaṁtuṁ ।
bhaṇai gurū gaccha tumaṁ sō cēva tumaṁ ihāṇēhī ॥
sō uppaiō garuḍō vva viṇhu sāhussa saṁnihiṁ pattō ।
taṁ dahaṁ saṁbhaṁtō viṇhumuṇī ciṁtaē ēvaṁ ॥
muṇi-āgamaṇamiṇaṁ kahai saṁgha- kajjaṁ uvaṭṭiyaṁ kiṁ pi ।
kahamannahā vihārō sāhūṇaṁ pāusē hōi ॥
iya ciṁtaṁtaṁ taṁ vaṁdiūṇa sāhai
vaṁdiūṇa sāhai paōvaṇaṁ sāhū ।
taṁ vēttūṇa khaṇēṇaṁ viṇhū hatthiṇapuraṁ pattō ॥
sō diuṁ niya-guruṁ muṇi-pariyariō gaō namui-pāsaṁ ।
namiō ya namui-vajraṁ nariṁda-lōēṇa savvēṇa ॥
sō dhamma- kahaṁ kāuṁ kōmala vayaṇēhiṁ jaṁpaē namuī ।
cihaṁtu tāva muṇiṇō puraṁmi iha pāusō jāva ॥
ēgattha na cirakālaṁ vasaṁti sayamēva sāhuṇō ēē ।
dahuṁ bahu-jīva- vahaṁ viharaṁti na pāusammi puṇō ॥
garuē imaṁmi nayarē jai bhikkhā vittiṇō imē bhikkhū ।
māsa - caukkaṁ ciṭṭhēti tujjha kiṁ nassaē tattō ॥
jē bharaha - niva-puṁgadēhiṁ puvvaṁ narmasiyā muṇiṇō ।
tē jai tumaṁ na paṇamasi taha vi ṭhiyaṁ dēhi tāṇa purē ||
iya viṇhukumārēṇa bhaṇiō namuī sakōvasullavai ।

labdhiprakaṭanē viṣṇukumāra- kathā |
kiṁ vayaṇa- vittharēṇaṁ na dēmi vasiuṁ purē tumha ॥
jaṁpai puṇō vi vihū vasaṁtu muṇiṇō varṇami pura-bāhiṁ ।
kuviō namuī sāhai na sahē'haṁ tumha gaṁdhaṁ pi ॥
majjhē vā bāhiṁ vā purassa saṁvāsa - patthaṇāi alaṁ ।
tā mēllaha maha nayaraṁ nihaṇissaṁ annā tumbhē ॥
taṁ sōuṁ viṇhu- muṇī pajjaliō pāvaō vva ghaya- sittō ।
taha vi namuī papai paya-ttayaṁ dēhi maha vasiuṁ ॥
namuī jaṁpai dinnaṁ paya-ttayaṁ tō imāu jai bāhiṁ ।
ṭhāhisi taō haṇissaṁ ēvaṁ hōu tti bhaṇai muṇī ॥
aha vaḍiuṁ payahō kirīṭa - kuṁḍala gharō kusuma- mālī ।
dhaṇu vajja- kivāṇa karō bhayaṁkarō tihuyaṇassāvi ॥
vikiraṁtō gaha cakaṁ cakkara-niyaraṁ va niya-karaggēhiṁ ।
kaṁpāvatō payadaddarēṇa pattaṁ va mahivīḍhaṁ ॥
ucchālaṁtō jalanihi-salilaṁ cira-bhuttamudavāū vva ।
vēla vva nai - pavāhē paḍilōma-pahē vahāvaṁtō
pāḍatō khayara-gaṇaṁ taṇaṁ va phārēṇa phukka-pavaṇēṇa ।
vahṷ̄tō sō jāō mēru- samō kaya- viviha-rūvō ॥
dāḍaṁ siraṁmi pāyaṁ dhariṇīē pāḍiō imō namuī ।
ciṭṭhaha calaṇē ṭhaviḍaṁ puvvāvara - jalahi- majjhami ॥
taṁ ti-jaya-kkhōbha-karaṁ daṭṭhūṇa suraṁgaṇāu sakkēṇa ।
paṭṭaviyāō gāyaṁti mahuramarahaṁta - bhaṇiyatthaṁ ॥
kōvō jalaṇō vva varṇa dahai tavaṁ pannagō v kuṇai bhayaṁ ।
jīyaṁ pakkhivai bhavē ranē dussikkha turaō vva ॥
iya kōvōvasama - kaē taha kinnara - khayara pamuha - mahilāō ।
gāyaṁti savaṇa-mūlē muṇissa puraō ya nacaṁti ॥
paumō vi āgaō niya- pamāya - sacivāvarāha-bhīya-maṇō ।
namiūṇa calaṇa- laggō khamāvaē viṇhu- muṇi-nāhaṁ ॥
bhayavaṁ ! na maē muṇiyā kīraṁtī duṭṭha maṁtiṇā imiṇā ।
āsāyaṇā muṇīṇaṁ kahiyā ya na majjha kēṇāvi ॥
taha vi imō maha dōsō jaṁ namuī majjha saṁtiō bhicō ।
chippaṁti bhicca dōsēṇa sāmiṇō nīi vayaṇamiṇaṁ ॥

=== Kumara2output-61-to-61.json ==========================
284
kumārapālapratibōdhē
taha tuha ahaṁ pi bhiccō tumaṁ pahū majjha majjha dōsēṇa ।
chippasi tumaṁ pi bhayavaṁ ! tā uvasaṁhara imaṁ kōvaṁ ॥
ēvaṁ khāmijaṁtō sō tailōkkēṇa vajjiuṁ kōvaṁ ।
jāō sahaja-sarīrō vēlā - mukkō samuddō vva ॥
iya kāuṁ jiṇa pavayaṇa- pahāvaṇaṁ guru- samīva-kaya-suddhī ।
tivva tava khaviya - kammō viṇhukumārō gaō mōkkhaṁ ॥
iti labdhaprakaṭa viṣṇukumāra - kathā ।
ēvaṁ tava - māhāppaṁ muṇiūṇa tavō nariṁda ! kāyavvō ।
sō bajjhō cha--bhēō abhitaraō ya cha-bhēō ॥
taṁ jahā-
aṇasaṇamūṇōyariyā vittī- saṁkhēvaṇaṁ rasa-cāō |
kāya - kilēsō saṁlīṇayā ya bajjhō tavō hōi ॥
pāyacchittaṁ viṇaō vēyāvacaṁ tahēva sajjhāō ।
jhāṇaṁ ussagō vi ya abhitaraō tavō hōi ॥
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ aṭṭhami - cauddasī - pamuha-pavva- diyahēsu ।
jiṇa kallāṇa-tihīsu ya sattīi tavaṁ karissāmi ॥
ēvaṁ bārasa - bhēyaṁ tava dhammaṁ akkhiuṁ gurū bhai ।
bārasavihaṁ narāhiva ! suṇa saṁpai bhāvaṇā - dhammaṁ ॥
suha-bhāvaṇā- parigaō jīva dayaṁ pāliḍaṁ khamai jīvō ।
sō asuha- bhāvaṇāē gahiō pāvaṁ na kiṁ kuṇai ॥
vaṁjhaṁ biṁti jahitya satya-paḍhaṇaṁ atthāvabōhaṁ viṇā
sōhaggēṇa viṇā maḍappa karaṇaṁ dāṇaṁ viṇā saṁbhamaṁ ।
sanbhāvēṇa viṇā puraṁdhi- ramaṇaṁ nēhaṁ viṇā bhōaṇaṁ
ēvaṁ dhamma - samujjamaṁ pi vibuhā ! suddhaṁ viṇā bhāvaṇaṁ ॥
sattama - naraya - nimittaṁ kammaṁ baddhaṁ pasannacaṁdēṇa ।
asuhāi bhāvaṇāē suhāi puṇa kēvalaṁ pattaṁ ।
taṁ jahā-
atthittha pōyaṇapuraṁ ramaṇīhi vibhūsiyaṁ pi savattō ॥
jaṁ naramaṇīhiṁ rēhai tattha nivō sōmacaṁdōtti ।

bhāvanāyāṁ prasannacandra-kathā |
riu-ramaṇi - nayaṇa-nīra - ppavāha-saṁbaṁdha-laḍa-ullāsō ।
chajjai samujjalō tassa jasa-bharō rāyahaṁsō vva ॥
dēvī ya dhāraṇī sē jīi hasaṁtīi ōṇaya-muhīi |
du-guṇē daṁta-kaṁtī thaṇa vaṭṭē hāra-laṭṭhīō ॥
annayā gavakkhē ṭhiyassa kēsē nivassa vivaraṁtī ।
paliyaṁ dahaṁ jaṁpai samāgaō dēva! dūō ti ॥
daḍuṁ disāu rāyā jaṁpai kiṁ dēvi ! dīsai na dūō ।
sā bhai nāha ! nāhaṁ maṇussa dūyaṁ tuha kahēmi ॥
navaraṁ paliyaṁ daṇa dhamma- dūō maē samakkhāō |
dēvīi daṁsiyaṁ paliyamiṁdu-kiraṇujjalaṁ rannō ||
taṁ daṭṭhūṇa nariṁdō hima-saṁgama-daḍḍū-kamala- sama-vayaṇō ।
jhatti taraṁgiya- nayaṇō saṁjāō bāha-salilēṇa ॥
taṁ phusamāṇā cēlaṁcaṇēṇa hasiūṇa jaṁpaē dēvī ।
jai lajjasē jarāē tō paḍahaṁ dēva ! dāvēmi ॥
buḍḍō tti jō bhaṇissaha dēvaṁ tassaṁga-niggahaṁ kāhaṁ ।
rāyā jaṁpara suṁdari ! juttamiṇaṁ nivvivēyāṇaṁ ॥
jamhā jayammi jīvā mūḍhā buḍattaṇēṇa lajjaṁtā ।
puṇa vi taruṇatta luḍā khijvaṁti rasāyaṇa - nimittaṁ ॥
bali-paliya-nāsa- hēḍaṁ kuṇaṁti taṇu-maddaṇōsahāīṇi ।
cakammati salīlaṁ puraō taruṇīṇa taruṇa vva ॥
puṭṭhā parēṇa bahuyaṁ pi biṁti tē thēvamattaṇō jammaṁ ।
gaya- juvvaṇā vi mūḍhā kuṇaṁti hī juvvaṇa- viyārō ॥
juvvaṇa-viyārō
dēvi ! maha putrva - purisā a-diṭṭha-paliyā palitta - pūlaṁ va ।
rajjamiṇaṁ paricaiuṁ para lōya-samujjayā jāyā ॥
jaṁ puṇa ēyāṇa karma vilaṁghiḍaṁ rajjamēttiyaṁ kālaṁ ।
vihiyaṁ maē mahaṁtaṁ taṁ jāō maha maṇē mannū ॥
tā vajjiūṇa rajjaṁ vaṇa-vāsa vayaṁ ahaṁ pavajjissaṁ ।
puttaṁ pasannacaṁdaṁ bālaṁ paripālasu tumaṁ ॥
dēvī jaṁpai pacchā na acchiuṁ ucchahē viṇā tumaē ।
mēha - rahiyaṁmi gayaṇē kayāvi kiṁ phurai vijjaliyā ॥

kumārapālapratibōdhē
bālaṁ pi sōmacaṁdō pasannacaṁdaṁ nivēsiuṁ rajjē ।
dēvīē dhāīē ya saṁgaō tāvasō jāō ॥
aha dēvī payaṭṭō pavaḍhiḍaṁ puvva-saṁbhavō ganbhō ।
samayaṁmi samuppannō samatta - lakkhaṇa-dharō puntō ॥
vakkalacīritti kayaṁ sē nāmaṁ vakkalēhiṁ pihiō ti ।
pattā paṁcattaṁ jhatti dhāriṇī pasava - pīḍāē ||
caṁda - vimāṇē jāyā dēvī sā puvva- nēha-paḍibaḍā ।
kaya-vaṇa-mahisī - rūvā duī pāēi taṁ puttaṁ ॥
-
-
taṁ kiṁ pina cōjjamadiṭṭha - māiō jaṁ nirakkharō ēsō ।
dhāī vi kamēṇa mayā natthi hi bhaviyavvayā-nāsō ॥
kicchēṇa pāliō sō piuṇā jāō ya juvvaṇābhimuhō ।
kuṇai phala- kaṁda - kusumāṇayaṇēṇa piussa sāhējjaṁ ॥
aha taṁ pasannacaṁdō vaṇē vasaṁtaṁ sahōyaraṁ muṇiuṁ ।
ciṁtēi kuṇau tāō thavirō tāvasa vayaṁ visamaṁ ॥
jaṁ puṇa vaṇavāsa-duhaṁ dusahaṁ bālō vi sahai maha bhāyā ।
rajjaṁ tu karēmi ahaṁ taṁ mahaī maha maṇē pīḍā ॥
tō bhaṇiyāu gaṇiyāu tēṇaṁ gaṁtuṁ muṇīṇa vēsēṇa ।
niya - kōsalēṇa uvalōbhiūṇa āṇēha maha baṁdhuṁ ॥
tatthāsamē gayāō muṇi- vēsa dharāu tāu sō dahum̐ ।
abhivāhaūṇa muddhō pucchara kō āsamō tumha ॥
jaṁpaṁti tāu amhē pōyaṇa - āsama-nivāsiṇō risiṇō ।
tuha āgayā atihiṇō tā ātitthaṁ tumaṁ kuṇasu ॥
sō bhai khāha tubhē billāi phalāim̐ āṇiyāim̐ maē ।
tāhi bhaṇiyaṁ imāim̐ virasāim̐ na kōvi bhakkhē ॥
jē amha āsama-dumā tēsiṁ phalavattiyaṁ tumaṁ piccha ।
tō bhuṁjāvaṁti imaṁ khaṁḍamaē mōyagē tāō ॥
tō bhakkhiūṇa ēsō jāō billāi-phala- virakta-maṇō ।
tāō niya- dēha-pharisaṁ kaya- harisaṁ kāravaṁti imaṁ ॥
thōra-dhaṇa-kalasa-kaliē niya-vaccha-yalē ṭhavaṁti tassa karaṁ ।
sō jaṁpa maharisiṇō kiṁ aṁgaṁ kōmalaṁ tumha ॥

bhāvanāyāṁ prasannacandra - kathā |
kiṁ vā thalāī hiyaē ēyāī samunnayāī tumhāṇa |
tāō niya-kara-yalēhi taṁ parisaṁtīu jaṁpati ॥
amha vaṇa-rukkha-phala-bhakkhaṇēṇa iṇamaṁga-maddavaṁ hōi ।
uvacaya-vasēṇa hiyaē thalāim̐ thūlāim̐ taha huṁti ॥
tā muttuṁ ēyamasāramāsamaṁ amha-āsamaṁ ēhi ।
tō
kuṇai sō kumārō tāhiṁ samaṁ gamaṇa-saṁkēyaṁ ॥
saṁṭhaviuṁ tāvasabhaṁḍamāgaō jāva sō kahiya-ṭhāṇē ।
taru-caḍiyā vara - purisā tā duhuṁ sōmacaṁda -risiṁ ॥
āgacchaṁtaṁ tāsi kahati tāō vi sāva-bhīyāō ।
vāhāgamē migīō va savvāō disōdisaṁ jaṁti ॥
ṭhāṇaṁ gayammi jaṇaē sayala-vaṇē tāō sō gavēsaṁtō ।
paribhamaha jāva muddhō tā pēcchai raha gayaṁ purisaṁ ॥
tāya ! abhivāyayāmi ti taṁ pi jaṁpaṛa risitti mannatō ।
rahiṇā paryapiō sō kumāra ! tē kattha gaṁtavvaṁ ॥
sō bhāi pōyaṇē āsamammi tatthēva gaṁtukāmēṇa ।
rahiṇā sō saṁlattō ēhi samaṁ cēva vaccāmō ॥
rahiṇō bhajjaṁ tāyatti sō bhagai tīē pucchiō bhattā ।
kō ēsō uvayārō rahiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ piē ! ēsō ॥
itthī - rahiyammi vaṇē vasiō tti tumaṁ pi mannaē purisaṁ ।
kiṁ vāhijjaṁ ti imē migi tti turagē ya vāgarai ॥
vakkala - cīrī rahiṇā bhaṇiō ēēhiṁ kajamiṇamēva ।
rahiṇō vi mōyagā sē dinnā tō jaṁpaē ēsō ॥
dinnāī ērisāī phalāī mē pōyaṇāsama - risīhi ।
aha rahiṇō saṁjāyaṁ cōrēṇēkkēṇa saha juddhaṁ ॥
rahiṇā viṇijiō sō daḍha - ppahārittaraṁjiō bhaṇai ।
ētthasthi majjha atthō vitthinnō taṁ tumaṁ ginha ॥
bhariō rahō dhaṇēṇaṁ rahiṇā sō pōyaṇammi saṁpattō ।
dāūṇa kiṁ pi mulaṁ vakkala-cīriṁ imaṁ bhaṇai ॥
imiṇā maggasu uḍavaṁ iha tti savvattha sō paribhamaṁtō ।
gaṇiyā-gihaṁ gaō bhaṇai tāya ! abhivādyāmi tumaṁ ॥
maharisi ! imiṇā mullēṇa dēsu uḍavaṁ ti dēmi givha imaṁ ।

=== Kumara2output-65-to-65.json ==========================
288
kumārapālapratibōdhē
iya jaṁpatī akkā hakkārāvara divākittiṁ ॥
tassa aṇicchaṁtassa vi taha kammaṁ kāravēi sā haviraṁ ।
avaṇīya vakkalaṁ taṁ parihāviya-vattha- ābharaṇaṁ ॥
pariṇāvai niya-dhūyaṁ rūvēṇa suraṁgaṇaṁ va pañcakkhaṁ ।
gāyaṁtīō bahū-varamasēsa vēsāō citi ॥
muṇi vēsā vēsāō jāō gayāō kumāramāṇēuṁ ।
tāō kahaṁti rannō ēvaṁ uvalōbhiō kumarō ॥
āgamaṇē saṁkēyaṁ kāraviō kiṁ tu tāya-daṁsaṇaō ।
amhē nahāō taō na sakkiō saddiuṁ kumarō ॥
amhē gavēsamāṇī aḍaviṁ ciya uvagaō na piu-pāsaṁ ।
taṁ sōūṇa visannō pasannacaṁdō bhaṇai ēvaṁ ॥
ahaha ajuttaṁ jaṁ sō pattō pāsaṁ na majjha piuṇō ।
mīṇō vva jalāō sō jaṇayāō vijōjiō marihī ॥
iya dukkhēṇa nariṁdō sayaṇija gaō raī apāvaṁtō ।
tīē gaṇiyāi gihē muraya-ravaṁ nisuṇiuṁ bhaṇai ॥
ma dukkhaē vi suhiō kō ēsō jassa maṁdirē ēvaṁ ।
suvvai muraya-ravō taṁ paraṁparāē suṇai gaṇiyā ॥
sā āgaṁtuṁ vinnavai naravaī dēva ! maha purā kahiyaṁ ।
nēmittiēṇa jō tuha ēi gihaṁ tāvasō taruṇō ॥
tassa tumaṁ niya-dhūyaṁ dijasu tassa pabhāvaō hōhī ।
sā sukha bhāgiṇī ajja majjha sō āgaō gēhaṁ ॥
pariṇāviō ya dhūyaṁ mahsavō tēṇa vahai gihē mē ।
dēvō dukkhī na maē muṇiō tā khamasu maha dōsaṁ ॥
tō rannā paṭṭaviyā puvva-narā taduvalakkhaṇa-nimittaṁ ।
gaṁtumuvalakkhiuṁ taṁ āgaṁtuṁ vinnavaṁti nivaṁ ॥
paritumaṇō rāyā vaha samēyaṁ karēṇu - khaṁdha gayaṁ ।
vakkala - cīriṁ āṇēi niya-gēhaṁ garuya - riḍīē ॥
pariṇīya - rāya - kannō sō kumarō muṇiya-sayala - vavahārō ।
saṁpanna - vaṁchiyatthō tiyasō vva suhaṁ gamai kālaṁ ॥
jaṇaō vi vaṇē kumaraṁ apēcchamāṇō daḍhaṁ kuṇai sōyaṁ ।
niva paṭṭaviyā purisā kahaṁti sē kumara vr̥ttaṁtaṁ ॥

bhāvanāyāṁ prasannacandra - kathā |
sō hōi kiṁci satthō suya- virahē taha vi tassa maharisiṇō ।
accaṁta - rōaṇāō kamēṇa aṁdhattaṇaṁ jāyaṁ ॥
annēhiṁ tāvasēhiṁ kayāṇukaṁpēhiṁ pāraṇa-dinēsu ।
vihiya-phala- saṁvibhāgō tatthēva vaṇē vasai ēsō ॥
bārasasu vaccharēsuṁ gaēsu kaiyāvi aḍarattammi ।
kumarō vakkalacīrī paḍibuddhō ciṁtaē ēvaṁ |
jamma- samaē vi māyā majjha mayā tō mahākilēsēṇa ।
paripāliōmhi piuṇā pavanna - tāvasa-vaēṇāvi ॥
nicaṁ kaḍi caḍiēṇaṁ piuṇō tava caraṇa- pīḍiyaṁgassa ।
kaṭṭhē kathaṁ maē nivaḍiyassa pahi-ppahāra - samaṁ ॥
paccuvayāra - samatthō jāō'haṁ jāva juvvaṇārūḍhō ।
vihi-vasaō iha pattō pāvō ajiiṁdiō tāva ॥
iya ciṁtiūṇa kumarō nivaī vinnavai dēva ! maha cittaṁ ।
tāya - calaṇāraviṁdaṁ duhuṁ ukkaṁṭhiyaṁ bāḍhaṁ ॥
Jain Education International
rāyā bhaṇai mamāvi hu accaṁtaṁ tāya-daṁsaṇē vaṁchā ।
tō dōvi gayā tatthāsamammi tē rāya - juvarāyā ॥
kumarō jaṁpada dahūṇa āsamaṁ maha taṇaṁ va rajja-sirī ।
tāī imāim̐ sarāim̐ ramiō haṁsō vva jatthāhaṁ ॥
phala-bhakkhaṇaṁ jahicchaṁ kayaṁ maē jāṇa tē imē rukkhā ।
ēē tē hariṇā bhāyara vva maha khēllaṇa sahāyā ॥
maha duddha-pāṇa-pavaṇāu tā imā māyarō vva mahisīō ।
rajjē vi majjha kattō piu sussā kahaṁ tu imaṁ ॥
āsamaṁ paviṭṭhā tuṭṭhā hūṇa sōmacaṁda -risiṁ ।
jaṁpai pasannacaṁdō tāya ! tumaṁ namai jēha-suō ॥
piuṇā pasannacaṁdō savvaṁgaṁ pāṇiṇā parāmuṭṭhō ।
puttaya ! nirāmaōsi tti jaṁpamāṇēṇa maharisiṇā ॥
kumarō jaṁpai ēsō vakkalacīrī tumaṁ namaha tāya ! |
sō risiṇā savvaṁgaṁ tuṭṭēṇāliṁgiō gāḍhaṁ ||
nayaṇēsu tayā risiṇō vāha - jalaṁ pasariyaṁ siṇēhēṇa ।
taṁ cēya tassa aṁdhatta - vigama paramōsahaṁ jāyaṁ ॥

kumārapālapratibōdhē
tō dunnivi maharisiṇā tē diṭṭhā pucchiyā kusala vattaṁ ।
tē biṁti amha kusalaṁ savvattha tuha ppasāēṇa ॥
taṁ aṇapēkkhitaṁ tāvasa-bhaṁḍa khu kērisaṁ jāyaṁ ।
iya ciṁtaṁtō pattō vakkalacīrī uḍava-majjhē ॥
tāvasa - bhaṁḍaṁ vatthaṁca lēṇa paḍilēhaē sayaṁ ṭhaviyaṁ ।
sō pāyakēsarīē jai vva pattāi uvagaraṇaṁ ॥
puvvaṁ kahiṁ pi karaṇaṁ kayaṁ maē ērisaṁ ti ciṁtaṁtō ।
sō jāya jāisaraṇō sāmannaṁ sarai puvva kayaṁ ॥
visa-dāruṇēsu visaēsa hā ! kahaṁ mucchiōmhi mūḍha tti ।
pasariya- suha- bhāvō bīya sukka-jjhāṇaṁ aikaṁtō ॥
vakkalacīrī cūriya mōha-balō jhatti kēvalī jāō ।
jaṇassa baṁdhavarasa ya jahaṭṭhiyaṁ kahai sō dhammaṁ ॥
amhāṇa mukkha-maggō suha taē daṁsiō tti jaṁpatā ।
taṁ dēvayā samappiya- liṁgaṁ tē dō vi paṇamaṁti ॥
tammi samayammi pōyaṇa- pura-āsannē maṇōramujjāṇē ।
sayala- tailuka - pujjō vīrajiniṁdō samōsariō ||
pattēyabuddha-samaṇō vakkalacīrī pavanna- jiṇadhammaṁ ।
niya jaṇayamapiḍaṁ jiṇavarassa viharēi annattha ॥
gaṁtuṁ pasannacaṁdō pōyaṇapura mullasaṁta-vēraggō ।
bālaṁ pi suyaṁ rajē ṭhaviḍaṁ paḍivajjaē dikkhaṁ ॥
sō ahigaya-suttatthō kamēṇa dukkara-tavaccaraṇa-niraō ।
vīrajiṇidēṇa samaṁ samāgaō rāyagiha-nayaraṁ ॥
sāmissa vaṁdaṇatthaṁ viṇiggaō sēṇiō saparivārō ।
tassa puṇa aggasēnē saṁti duvē sumuha- dummuhā ॥
ēga-calaṇē paiṭṭiya- mūsiya-bhuya· juyalamacala - thira-kāyaṁ ।
ravi - biṁba- nihiya- nayaṇaṁ ēgaṁ pēcchati tē samaṇaṁ ॥
ēkkēṇa tattha bhaṇiyaṁ -ahō ! mahappā muṇī imō kō vi ।
sayala-jaṇa-vaṁdaṇijō jō ēvaṁ kuṇai tivva- tavaṁ ॥
ciṭṭhēja ēga-calaṇēṇa kō raviṁ kō khaṇaṁ pi pēkkhējja ।
ēyassa sagga mōkkhā dukkarakārissa hattha gayā ॥

bhāvanāyāṁ prasannacandra-kathā |
bīēṇa puṇō bhaṇiyaṁ - pasannacaṁdō narāhivō ēsō !
ēyassa natthi dhammō vihalaṁ tivvaṁ pi tava -kammaṁ ॥
bālō puttō rajjammi ṭhāviō jō aṇēṇa sō ihi ।
mōyāvijjai rajjaṁ arīṇa miliūṇa maṁtīhi ॥
maṁtīṇaṁ tāṇa rajaṁ samappiyaṁ rakkhaṇatthamēēṇa |
tē bhakkhati khalā taṁ luddhā duī va majjārā ॥
bālē hayammi puttē hōhī ēyassa vaṁsa-viddhaṁsō ।
aṁtēuraṁ aṇāhaṁ imaṁ viṇā kaṁ dasaṁ lahihī ॥
tā ēsō pāva-nihī na hīṇa- cariō dhuvaṁ adaṭṭhavvō ।
ēvaṁ sōuṁ caliyaṁ pasannacaṁdassa suhajhāṇaṁ ॥
sō ciṁtiuṁ pavattō-ahō ! aṇajā kumaṁtiṇō ēē ।
maha puttassa viḍiyā bahusō sammāṇiyā vi maē ॥
jai tattha ahaṁ huṁtō tēsiṁ vīsattha-ghāyagāṇa taō ।
aṇusāsaṇaṁ karaṁtō nava-nava- niggaha-payārēhiṁ ॥
iya kalusa - jjhāṇa- parō rāyarisī rōsa rakkhasārūḍhō ।
pēkkhai putta-vivakkhē tē paccakkhē vva duramacē ||
puvvaṁ piva tē samarē maṇasā
1
ētthaṁtarammi rāyā samāgaō sēṇiō tattha ॥
taṁ jhāṇa-niccalaṁ pikkhiūṇa rāyā phuraṁta pariōsō ।
uttariūṇa kariṁdāō vaṁdaē mahi-nihitta - sirō ॥
tava - sāmatthamauvvaṁ pasannacaṁdassa iya vicitaṁtō ।
rāyā gaṁtuṁ paricatta - rāyaciṁdhō namai nāhaṁ ॥
sō parisāha nisannō samaē pucchara jayā maē nāha ! |
namiō pasannacaṁdō karijja jai sō tayā kālaṁ ॥
kā tassa gai hujjā vīrajiṇō bhaṇai tammi samayammi ।
sō kālaṁ kuṇamāṇō sattama-narayammi gacchija ॥
saralāsaō nariṁdō ciṁtai muṇiṇō kahaṁ niraya-gamaṇaṁ ? |

tō kattha vacai ?; jiṇō jaṁpai savvahasiddhami ॥

bhāvanāyāṁ śāla- mahāśāla-kathā |
sāla- mahāsālā dō vi tassa pattā paṇamaṇatthaṁ ॥
tariūṇa bhava-samudda dhamma- taraṁḍēṇa lahaha mōkkha-taḍaṁ ।
iya vīrajiṇēsara - dēsaṇāi tē dō vi paḍibuḍā ||
sālēṇa mahāsālō rajjaṁ paḍivajasu tti bhaṇiō vi ।
jāva na taṁ ginhai tāva gāgalī bhāiṇijjō tti ॥
jasavai-piṭharaya puttō ṭhaviō rajjammi garuya - riddhīē ।
sāla-mahāsālēhiṁ gahiyā dikkhā jiṇa-samīvē ॥
samayaṁtarammi sāmī viharatō āgaō puriṁ caṁpaṁ ।
saha sāla - mahāsālēhiṁ gōyamō pahu- aṇunnāō ॥
pattō ya piṭṭhacaṁpa kaṁcaṇa-kamala-ṭṭhiō kahai dhammaṁ ।
sōūṇa gāgalī taṁ paḍibuddhō jaṇaṇi jaṇaya-juō ॥
ṭhaviūṇa suyaṁ rajjē giṇhai dikkhaṁ piūhiṁ pariyariō ।
paṁcahi vi tēhiṁ kaliō caliō gōyama-gurū caṁpaṁ ॥
tāṇa jiṇa-vaṁdaṇatthaṁ vaccaṁtāṇaṁ pahammi paṁcapahaṁ |
subha- bhāvaṇā- parāṇaṁ uppannaṁ kēvalaṁ nāṇaṁ ॥
savvē vi gayā caṁpa kamēṇa ti-payāhiṇaṁ ti tē sāmi ।
vaṁdēha iṁdabhūī iyarē paṁca vi gayā parisaṁ ॥
tē bhai gōyamō ēha sāmiṇaṁ vaṁdaha tti tō sāmī ।
taṁ jaṁpai mā gōyama ! kēvali - āsāyaṇaṁ kuṇasu ॥
khāmēi gōyamō tē visanna-cittō ya ciṁtaē ēvaṁ ।
afer kēvalamahaṁ kiṁ sijjhissāmi ēttha bhavē ॥
puvvaṁ jiṇēṇa kahiyaṁ maṇuō aṭṭhāvayammi jō caḍiḍaṁ ।
caḍavīsa -
jiṇē namihī sō sijjhissai ihēva bhavē ॥
taṁ jaṁpatē tiyasē muṇiuṁ aṭṭhāvayaṁ giriṁ gaṁtuṁ ।
vaṁchēha gōyamō vaṁdaṇatthamarahaṁta - parimāṇaṁ ||
tāvasa- paḍibōhaṁ jāṇiūṇa sō bhayavayā aṇunnāō ।
cāraṇa- laḍi balēṇaṁ pavaṇō vva khaṇēṇa taṁ pattō ॥
ēttōya mōkkha- hēḍaṁ sōuṁ aṭṭhāvayaṁ samāruhiuṁ ।
tinni payaṭṭā kōḍinna dinna - sēvāla - kulavaiṇō ॥
paḍhamō cauttha- pāraṇaya- adda - kaṁdāi bhōyaṇō nicaṁ ।
paṁca-saya-tāvasa-juō ārūḍhō mēhalaṁ padamaṁ ॥

chaṭṭha-tava-pāraṇē raiya-sukka - kaṁdāi - bhōyaṇō duiō ।

bhāvanāyāṁ śāla-mahāśāla-kathā ।
khaṁḍiya vipakva - muṁḍō juvarāō kaṁḍarīō tti ॥
aha tattha naliṇa-vaṇa-kāṇaṇammi guṇiṇō samāgayā muṇiṇō ।
tāṇa samīvē dhammaṁ suṇaṁti tē rāya- juvarāyā ॥
vēragga-magga- laggō sagihaṁ gaṁtr̥̄ṇa puṁḍarīya-niyō ।
juvarāya - kaṁḍarīyaṁ maṁti- samakkhaṁ imaṁ bhaṇai ||
vaccha ! kamāgayamēyaṁ giṇhasu rajaṁ ahaṁ tu bhaya-bhīō ।
bhava- dukkha lakkha-khaṁḍaṇa - dakkhaṁ dikkhaṁ gahissāmi ॥
tō bhai kaṁḍarīō - kiṁ bhava kūvammi khivasi maṁ nāha ! |
tumamēva kuṇasu rajjaṁ ahaṁ tu kāhāmi pavajjaṁ ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ rannā - rēhai dhammō vi kamēṇa vaccha ! kīraṁtō ।
kumarēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ - dēva ! natthi maraṇassa kō vikamō ॥
tō bhai puṁḍarīō jaha vi imaṁ tahavi juvaṇaṁ visamaṁ ।
kāmō jakka- vāmō niraggalō iṁdiyaggāmō ॥
dupariccaō pamāō parīsahā dussahā calaṁ cittaṁ ।
huyavaha-jālā-pāṇaṁ va dukkaraṁ vaccha ! cāritaṁ ॥
tā sāvaya-dhammaṁ ciya pavajiō rajja - pālaṇaṁ kuṇasu ।
paḍivanna anivvahaṇaṁ ubhaya-bhava duhāvahaṁ jamhā ॥
vajjaraha kaṁḍarīō saccamiṇaṁ tahavi nāha ! niya-vayaṇaṁ ।
kīrai kimannahā tō ghittavvā nicchyaṁ dikvā ॥
iya bhaṇiuṁ pavvaiō kumarō rāyā u bhāvaō sāhū ।
gēhammi ṭhiō maṁtīhiṁ vāriō dikkha-gahaṇāō ॥
tō kuṇai kaṁḍarīō ciraṁ tavaṁ niccamaṁga-niravēkkhaṁ ।
dasa - viha- sāmāyāriṁ pālai muṇi vallahō hōi ॥
aha annayā vasaṁtē viyaṁbhiē bhuvaṇa - khōha -saṁjaṇaṇē ।
cāritta mōha - vasaō calai maṇaṁ kaṁḍarīyassa ॥
-
sō ciṁtēi alaṁ mē pavajāē kilēsa - bahulāē ।
gaṁtuṁ karēmi rajjaṁ jaṁ maha niya-baṁdhuṇā dinnaṁ ||
tō pattō puṁḍarigiṇi-nayarīē sō ṭhiō ya ujjāṇē ।
uvagaraṇaṁ ṭhaviḍaṁ taru-layāi hariyammi uvaviṭṭhō ॥
sō appāṇaṁ rannō jāṇāvai vaṇa- niutta- purisāō ।

rāyā vi pahāṇa-juō āgaṁtuṁ namai taṁ jhatti ॥
rukkhē ṭhaviōvagaraṇō ēgāgī hariya-kāya - luḍhiyaṁgō ।
vaya - nivvinnō mannē imō tti muṇiuṁ bhaṇai rāyā ॥
bhō ! bhō ! sumaraha tumbhē jaṁ vāraṁ tassa majjha taṁmi diṇē ।
rahasa-vasēṇa pavannā bālēṇa aṇēṇa pavajjā ॥
tattō rāyā dāūṇa kaṁḍarīyassa rāya - ciṁdhāī ।
muṇi-liṁgāṇiya-gahium̐ nīharai sayaṁ gahiya- dikkhō ॥
aha vaya-bhaṭṭhō raṁkō vva kisa-taṇū ēsa bhōyaṇatyō ti ।
garahitō lōēhiṁ kaṁḍarīō kuṇai kōvaṁ ॥
bhuṁjāmi tāva paḍhamaṁ pacchā ēyāṇa niggahaṁ kāhaṁ ।
iya ciṁtaṁtō cittammi kaṁḍarīō gaō gēhaṁ ॥
uttama majjhima- ahamō ti-vihō laddhō cirāu āhārō ।
bhuttō tava tivvachuṇa kaṁḍarīēṇa ākaṁṭhaṁ ||
tassa bahu- bhōyaṇāō ya bhōga-jāgaraṇaō ya rayaṇīē ।
jāyā visuiyā vēyaṇā ya mahaī samutpannā ॥
bhatthi vva anila - punnā viyasiyamuyaraṁ niruṁbhiō pavaṇō ।
tassulasiyā tahā savvaṁgaṁ pasariō dāhō ॥
bhaṭṭa - pannō pāvō ēsō ti vibhāvi niōgīhiṁ ।
sō akaya-cikicchō kicchamuvagaō ciṁtaē ēvaṁ ॥
jaha kahavi imaṁ rayaṇi aikkamissāmi tō pabhāyammi ।
nihaṇissaṁ sa kuṭuṁbē savvē vi niōgiṇō ēē ॥
ēvaṁ rudda jjhāṇēṇa kaṇhalēsā - samanniō mariḍaṁ ।
sattama - puḍhavīē imō uppannō appaiṭṭhāṇē |
aha puṁḍarīya- sāhū ahō suladdhaṁ cirāu muṇi dhammaṁ ।
kāhāmi guru- samakkhaṁ ti ciṁtiuṁ calai gurupāsē ॥
sō vēlā - laṁghiya - sīya-rukkha bhōyaṇa- kilāmiō maggē ।
kōmala-kama-tala - nīhariya- ruhira - saṁsitta-mahivaṭṭhō ॥
gāmē uvassayaṁ maggiūṇa taṇa-sattharammi uvaviṭṭhō ।
guru-pāsē gihissaṁ kaiyā dikkhaṁ ti ciṁtēi ॥
garahiya-niya duccariō pai samaya-samullasaṁta-suha-jhāṇō ।
pīṇaṁgō vi vivannō sō savaṭṭhē surō jāō ॥

-
tā dēhassa kisattaṁ pīṇattaṁ vā muṇīṇa apamāṇaṁ ।
kiṁ tu suha-jhāṇamēkkaṁ nivvāṇa-nibaṁdhaṇaṁ biṁti ॥
gōyama - bhaṇiyaṁ ēttha - saṁgayaṁ puṁḍarīya ajjhayaṇaṁ ।
frost ēkka-vārēṇa dhaṇaya - sāmāṇiō dēvāṁ ॥
vēsamaṇō uṇa namiūṇa gōamaṁ gihiūṇa sammattaṁ ।
saṁpatta-ti-jaya- rajjō vva raṁjiō jāi niya-dvāṇaṁ ॥
iya dēsaṇāi gamiṇa gōyamō rayaṇimuttaraha jāva ।
aṭṭhā vayāu pēcchati tāvasā tāva taṁ tuṭṭhā ॥
jaṁpati paṇamiuṁ tē maharisi । tava lacchi - kula-bhavaṇa ! amhē ।
tuha sīsā hōhāmō tumaṁ tu amhāṇa hōsu guru ॥
tō gōyamō payaṁpai savvanna maha gurū mahāvīrō ।
sōcia surāsuracciya-calaṇō tumhaṁ pi hōu gurū ॥
puṇarutta- patthaṇa-parē dikkhai tāvasa-gaṇē gaṇahariṁdō ।
tēsiṁ samappiyaṁ dēvayāi savvaṁ pi muṇi- liṁgaṁ ॥
jūhāhivō vva kalahēhiṁ tēhiṁ saha gōyamō pahu-samīvē ।
caliō gaō ya gāmaṁ bhikkhā-kālē bhaṇai ēē ॥
kiṁ
tumha pāraṇa- kaē maṇa- iṭuṁ kahaha jēṇa āṇēmi ।
tē pāyasaṁ ti jaṁpati vimhaō phulla- muha kamalā ॥
taṁ ēga- kukkhi- pūraṇa- pamāṇamāṇai paḍiggahē kāuṁ ।
laddhi-samiddhō bhayavaṁ jaṁpaha muṇiṇō nivisaha tti ॥
amhāṇa pāraṇaṁ ēttiēṇa naṇu pāyasēṇa kiṁ hōhī ।
tahavi gurū jaṁ jaṁpai taṁ kāyavvaṁ ti ciṁtaṁtā ॥
tē savvēvi niviṭṭhā akkhīṇamahāṇasāha ladvīē ।
jēmāviūṇa savvē sayaṁ ca pacchā jimai bhayavaṁ ॥
aha amhēhiṁ pattō dēvō paramēsarō mahāvīrō ।
jaṇaya-samō ēsa gurū dhammō ya bhavannava - taraṁḍō ॥
tā kayapunnā amhē tti bhāvayaṁtāṇa bhuṁjamāṇāṇa ।
sēvāla - bhakkhagāṇaṁ saṁjāyaṁ kēvalannāṇaṁ ॥
dinnāīṇaṁ niyaḍē gayāṇa pahu- pāḍihēra - daṁsaṇaō ।
kōḍinnāīṇaṁ puṇa pahu- picchaṇaō tamupapannaṁ ॥

sāmi tipayāhiṇiuṁ kēvali - parisāē patthiyā ēē ।
ēha narmasaha sāmi ti bhaṇai tō gōyamō bhayavaṁ ॥
mā kuru kēvala āsāyaṇaṁ ti vāgarai gōyamaṁ sāmī ।
micchādukkaḍa pucvaṁ tē khāmai gōyamō namiuṁ ॥
-
ciṁtēi gōyamō puṇa vi garuya kammō kimēttha jammē'haṁ ।

pattā kēvala nāṇaṁ ahō mahaṁtō imāṇa punna- bharō ।
ēvaṁ ciṁtāvannaṁ paryapaē gōyamaṁ sāmī |
saccaṁ surāṇa vayaṇaṁ jiṇāṇa vā kiṁ ti gōyamō bhaṇai ।
nāha ! jiṇāṇaṁ sāmī jaṁpai tā mā kuṇasu adhiraṁ ॥
taṇa-vaṁsa-camma-unnā kaha tullā huṁti jēṇa iha nēhō ।
cira-saṁsaggā tuha mai unnā kaḍa-saṁnihō nēhō ॥
sō daḍhayarō jayā tujjha tuhihī kēvalaṁ tathā hōhī ।
tā tumamahaṁ ca gōyama ! aṁtē tullā bhavissāmō ॥
iti bhāvanāyāṁ śāla - mahāśāla-kathā ।

taṁ jahā-
itthēva bharahavāsē visiha-sara- vāvi - kūva -kaya- sōhaṁ ।

purisā parattha-luddhā sarōya- nayaṇāu jattha itthīō ।
bhavaṇāī bhōgi - ruḍāī tattha kiṁ vaṇṇimō annaṁ ॥
tattha nivō jiyasattū karāla -karavāla- rāhuṇā jassa ।
nicaṁpi sūra-rāyāṇa kavalaṇaṁ kīraē cōjaṁ ॥

jaō-

cōjjaṁ amaya-phalōvamamavacca muha daṁsaṇaṁ ēkaṁ ॥

jaha amha suō hōhī tā tuha bhaktiṁ karissāmō ॥

kalasaṁti apijjaṁtaṁ puvvaṁ satyaṁ ti jammi pijjaṁtaṁ ।
savvō vi hōṛa satyō piō tti lōyāṇa kahai jalaṁ ॥
maliṇā vi ghaṇā khittēsu varisiuṁ jammi ujjalā jāyā ।
khittēsu riddhi-dāṇaṁ visuddhi-hēu tti jaṁpaṁti ॥
vāsāsu āsi harisō sihīṇa haṁsāṇa jammi saṁjāō ।
sāsūē kēvi diṇā kēvi vaha tti payaḍēi ॥
vahūi
sārasa - mihuṇa- ghaṇatthala- maṇōharā viyasamāṇa-kamala-muhī ।
pasaraṁta-kāsa- hāsā jammi viyaṁbhai bhuvaṇa - lacchī ॥
tammi saraē sa-mittō pahi-cittō gaō ilāputtō ।
naṁdaṇa-vaṇābhirāmē ārāmē kīlaṇa nimittaṁ ॥

jaṁ asamatthō purisō paharēi paraṁ chalaṁ lahiuṁ ॥
aha thaṁbhiō vva sahasā ṭaṁkukkinō vva citta-lihiō vva ।

tujjha visuddhā buddhī sattha-rahassaṁ taē paḍhiyaṁ ॥
juttājutta-vimarisaṁ na khamō kāuṁ viṇā tumaṁ annō ।

savvēsimuvakhittī kimasajjhaṁ maha - pagarisassa ॥
taṁ bhai puṇō vinaḍō niya-sikkhaṁ payaḍiuṁ bahu suvannaṁ ।
viḍhavasu tumaṁ vivāhaṁ karēmi riddhīha tuha jēṇa ॥
tō vinnāya - naḍa-nayarē naḍa-pēcchaṁ maggiō nivō tēṇa ।
saṁpattā nāgarayā nivō niviṭṭhō sa dēvīō ॥

haṁtumilāputtaṁ bhaṇai bhadda ! bhō ! kuṇasu vaṁsa- paḍaṇaṁ ti ।
tō raṁga - bhūmi-nikkhaya-vaṁsaggē ṭhāviyaṁ phalayaṁ ॥
pāsēsu dōsu kīlā tassa kayā tattha sō samārūḍhō ।
pārasu pāuāō sacchidāō parihiūṇa ॥
asi-phalaya vagga- hatthō aggaddhē satta satta pacchaḍē ।
karaṇāraṁ kuṇai gayaṇē uppayamāṇō ilāputtō ॥
chiddēsu kīlaē sō pavēsiuṁ jāva ciṭṭhaē udghō ।
tā raṁjiō pura-jaṇō jaṁpēi ahō mahacchariyaṁ ॥
annassa natthi sattī ima tti sō davvamicchaē dāu ।
kiṁ tu nivammi aditē na dēha ēyassa kiṁci jaṇō ॥
rāyā u ciṁtai imaṁ imāu ṭhāṇāu kahavi jai ēsō
paḍiūṇa marai tā hōja nahiyā mē imā bhajjā ॥
tō bhai nivō na maē tuha vinnāṇaṁ nirūviyaṁ sammaṁ ।
tā kuṇasu puṇō vi imaṁ tēṇa kayaṁ taṁ duiya vāraṁ ॥
tuṭṭhō ya jaṇō bāḍhaṁ gaya-lajjō jaṁpai puṇō rāyā ।
na maē sammaṁ dihaṁ tā payaḍasu puṇa vi vinnāṇaṁ ॥
taṁ tēṇa taiya- vāraṁ kathaṁ nivō tahavi dēi na hu kiṁci ।
ahaha ! ajuttamajuttaṁ ti kuṇai hāhāravaṁ lōō ॥
lakkhēi laṁkhiyākhitta- māṇasaṁ khiivaī ilāputtō ।
tō ciṁtiuṁ pavattō dhiḍī ! visayāṇa visamattaṁ ॥
jēṇēsa nivō raṁgō va jīviyāē imīi aṇurattō ।
mama maraṇa- nimittaṁ kāravēi karaṇāī puṇaruttaṁ ॥
saṁtē virūva-lāvanna - kaṁtimaṁtē mahaṁta suddhaṁtē ।
