akuluggayāi kimimīi patthivō ēsa aṇurattō ॥
ahavā kimaṇēṇa ahaṁ pi ērisō cēva jēṇa vahāmi ।
dūrē niyai jalataṁ tā lōō na uṇa pāya-talē ॥
dhiddhī ! maha jammamiṇaṁ jēṇa na lajjā kayā guru-jaṇassa ।
jaṇaṇi-jaṇayāṇa dukkhaṁ maṇaṁ pi na nirūviyaṁ jēṇa ॥
paribhāviyaṁ na cittē lōē lahuyattamattaṇō jaṇa ।
jēṇōbhaya- lōya-bhayaṁ na thēvamēttaṁ pi saṁbhariyaṁ ॥
umagga- vilaggēṇaṁ mattagaṇa va miṁṭha rahiēna ।
para- puṭṭhē-vālaēṇa va para- ghara - saṁcaraṇa - sīlēṇa ॥
bhakkhābhakkha vibhāgaṁ apēkkhamāṇēṇa huyavahēṇēva ।
giri - naha-paya-pūrēṇa va nīyaṁ cia vaccamāṇēṇa ॥
visa rukkhēṇa va nīsēsa-lōya uvvēya-karaṇa dakkhēṇa ।
sayala -
jaṇa-garahaṇijjaṁ laṁkhaya - kulamaṇusaraṁtēṇa ॥
-
ahaha ! maē mūḍhēṇaṁ kaō kalaṁkō kulammi sasivimalē ।
sayaṇāṇaṁ vayaṇa- sarōruhēsu masi kuccaō dinnō ||
uḍūliyaṁ samaggaṁ tailōkaṁ ayasa-paṁsu-pasarēṇa ।
appā aṇappa- duggai-dukkhāṇaṁ bhāyaṇaṁ vihiō ॥
hā ! rūvamētta - daṁsaṇa-lōla - sahāvattaṇēṇa salaha samē ।
pāviḍi- diṭṭhi-raṁḍē paṁca imē maṁḍayā tujjha ॥
iya vēragga-gaēṇaṁ aṇēṇa kassavi gimmi dhaṇavaiṇō ।
paṁca-samiyā ti guptā dr̥ḍha vvayā sāhuṇō diṭṭhā ॥
niya - rūva - vijiya-tiyasaṁgaṇāu taruṇīō dhaṇavai-bahūō ।
bhattīha bhatta-pāṇaṁ tēsiṁ ditīō diṭṭhāō ॥
tē dahuṁ sō ciṁtai imē kayatthā suladdha- jammāṇō ।
jē ērisē pi dhīrā na diti diṭṭhi juvai-vaggē ॥
ahaha ! ahaṁ puṇa pāvō aṇajja-cariō vivēya-parihariō ।
jō akulīṇa - jatthē aṇatthamēvaṁ aṇuhavāmi ॥
iya ciṁtaṁtassa imassa mōhaṇijjaṁ gayaṁ khaōvasamaṁ ।
ullasiō suha bhāvō phuriō cārita-pariṇāmō ॥
cittēṇa catta-saṁgō mukka-mamattō sarīramēttē vi ।

aṇuvattiya-naya-dhammō ājamma-parōvayāra-kaya-kammō ।
mayaraḍaō vva rammō nara-nāhō tattha jayavambhō ॥
samarammi jō samaggē vipakkha-vaggē palāyamāṇammi ।

bhava- nivvēya- pahāṇā pāraḍā dēsaṇā guruṇā ||

dhaṇa-muccha-maccha- riṁchōli-saṁkulaṁ pāva-paṁka- paḍihatthaṁ ।
rāgōraga-saṁruddhaṁ vivihāmaya-mayara- duppēcchaṁ ॥
aṇavaraya-paḍaṁta-mahaṁta - āvayā -saya-sahassa- saṁkiṇṇaṁ ।
duḍara- visaya pivāsu cchalaṁta - vēlā-pasara-visamaṁ ॥
tariūṇa bhava-samuddaṁ jai vaṁchaha mōkkha- pāramubalahuṁ ।
tā paḍivajaha cāritta pavahaṇaṁ pavara-guṇa- kaliyaṁ ॥
aha bhaṇai sumai-maṁtī - bhayavaṁ । cārittamēva jīvāṇaṁ ।
nivvāṇa lābha hēu tti nicchaō vaṭṭaē na imō ॥

bhāvanāyāṁ jayavarmma - vijayavarmma- kathā |
maṁ kuṭṭaṇi vva bhuyagaṁ tumaṁ payārēsi aliya-vayaṇēhiṁ ।
divva-sarūvaṁ tu naī payāriḍaṁ kassa sāmatthaṁ ॥

aha atthāṇa- nisannō sivakumara- aṇēya - svayara - pariyariō ।
ēkkēṇāgaṁtuṁ khēyarēṇa pavaṇaṁjaō bhaṇiō ॥
sūrapura - pahuṇō sūratēya - khayarēsarassa dūō'haṁ ।
sō bhaṇai na maha dinnā maggaṁtassavi taē dhūyā ॥
bhūgōyarassa dinnā tā jaṁpissasi tumaṁ na mē kahiyaṁ ।
ajjavi taṁ maha appasu vayarāṇaṁ chaḍḍiyaṁ kiṁtu ॥
haṇiūṇa annahā bhūmigōyaraṁ taṁ sayaṁ vi gihissaṁ ।
pavaṇaṁjaēṇa bhaṇiō dūō-bhō ! kahasu niya-pahuṇō ॥
dhūyāi nābhiruiutti jai maē taṁ vivāhiō na tumaṁ ।
tattha uvālaṁbha vihiṁ jēṇa tumaṁ maṇaharō na kaō ॥
saṁpai puṇa para bhajjaṁ taṁ vaṁchaṁtō na lajjasē kīsa ।
bhaṇṇaṁti mahāpurisā paradāra- paraṁmuhā jamhā ॥
sivakumarēṇa bhaṇiō dūō-jai bhūmi gōyaraṁ haṇiuṁ ।
faraha maī tuha pahuṇō sō āgacchau taō turiyaṁ ॥

jēṇēsa appaṇō bhūmigōyarassa ya viyāṇai visēsaṁ ।
taha sēsa - khērēhiṁ kharaṁṭiō niggaō dūō ॥
gaṁtūṇa sūratēyassa taṁ kahai sōvi kōva - duppēcchō ।
bahu - khayara -suhaḍa - sahiō kaṇayapuraṁ jhatti saṁpattō ||
tassāgamaṇaṁ muṇiḍaṁ kumarō pavarṇajayaṁ bhagai ēvaṁ ।
imiṇā saha jujjhataṁ maṁ piccha tumaṁ saparivārō ॥
tō pavaṇaṁjaya - sahiō sivakumarō niggaō rahārūḍhō ।
vajaraī sūratēyaṁ paviḍaṁ khēyaraṁ dūyaṁ ॥
tuha mama ya viggahō ēsa sēsa- lōyassa kiṁ viṇāsēṇa ।
ēkaṁgā jujjhāmō dunni vi pēcchau jaṇō sēsō ॥
dappēṇa sūratēō taṁ paḍivajai taō imē dōvi ।

tō sūratēya-bāṇā taruṇi kaḍakkha vva vīyarāyammi ।
savvēvi niṣphalattaṁ paḍivannā sivakumārammi ॥
sivakumara - sara-samūhō aḍa- pahē sūratēya - sara-paṁtiṁ ।
nippunna- jaṇa-maṇōraha-mālaṁ chiṁdēha dēvvō vva ॥
tō niṭṭhiya-sara-nicaō cāvaṁ caiūṇa gahiya-karavālō ।

vēttr̥ṇa sūratēō churiyaṁ paharēi sivakumaraṁ ॥
laggaha na sō pahārō dēhē thēvaṁ pi sivakumārassa ।
cittammi sajjaṇassa va dujjaṇa ḍuvvayaṇa-saṁghāō ॥

iya annēhiṁ vi vijjāharēhiṁ dinnāu tassa kannāō ।

sthūlaprāṇātipātaviratau sivakumāra kathā |
bhajjāhiṁ tāhiṁ sahiō khayara samēō vimāṇamāruḍhō ।
sō pattō niya-nayaraṁ tuṭṭhā jaṇayāiṇō savvē ॥

bahirō vāyā - rahiō jammaṁdhō rōga-saya-gahiō ॥
kami pi akhamō visiitara - cēyaṇāē paricattō ।
tibva-duhakkatō nāraō vva nicaṁ gamai kālaṁ ॥
dahuṁ tahāvihaṁ taṁ karuṇā - paravasa-maṇō sivakumārō ।
kuṇai vivihē uvāē taddukkha nivāraṇa- nimittaṁ ॥
tu kayā uvayāra vva dujjaṇē tammi huṁti tē vihalā ।
ciṁtai sivō purākaya- pāva - phalaṁ bhuṁjai varāō ॥
anna- diṇē caunāṇī samāgaō tattha nāṇabhāṇu-gurū ।
taṁ namaṇatthaṁ rāyā gaō samaṁ sivakumārēṇa ॥
bhr̥-miliya - niḍāla - yalā dōvi guruṁ vaṁdiūṇa uvaviṭṭhā ।
bhava- nivvēya- pahāṇā pāraḍā dēsaṇā guruṇā ॥
kiṁ
-
samayammi pucchara sivō-bhayavaṁ ! maha dhāvi-sūṇuṇā imiṇā ।
kiṁ puvva-bhavē vihiyaṁ jaṁ ēsō dukkhiō ēvaṁ ॥
kiṁ vā uvayāricchā mahaī ēyammi vaṭṭaē majjha ।
guruṇā bhaṇiyaṁ -suṇa rāya putta ! savvaṁ kahēmi imaṁ ॥
vaḍauragāmē dō āsi baṁdhavā aṁba-niṁba - nāmāṇō ।
anna- diṇē tē dunnivi muṇīṇa pāsammi saṁpattā ॥
tēhiṁ ahiṁsā - dhammō kahiō tēsiṁ samagga-muha-hēū ।
taṁ sōuṁ lahu-kammō aṁbō saṁvēyamāvannō ||
sō thūla- jīva-vaha-viraī- rūva - dhammassa kuṇai paḍivattiṁ ।
niṁbēṇa pāvamaiṇā na dhamma- nāmaṁ pi saddahiyaṁ ॥

taṁ paśyan kautukēnaiṣa yāvat tatra kṣaṇaṁ sthitaḥ ।

kumārō vismayasmērō natvā'pr̥cchattapōdhanam ।
bhagavan ! kastavāgrē'sau vyadhānnr̥tyaṁ ka vā gataḥ ॥
muninōktamayaṁ yakṣaḥ kānanasyāsya nāyakaḥ ।
vasatyāyatanē'muṣminnāśritya pratimāmimām ॥
atrāgatasya mē sthānādanyatō'nēna bhaktitaḥ ।
nijāṅgādaṅganāṁ kr̥tvā cakrē saṅgītakaṁ kṣaṇam ||
saṁhr̥tya sarvarūpāṇi sō'dhunā pratimāṁ śritaḥ ।
kumārō vismitaḥ prōcē śaktirasyādbhutā munē ! ॥
sādhunōktamidaṁ stōkaṁ yasmādēvā maharddhikāḥ ।
atyutkr̥ṣṭatapaḥ śaktiyuktāśca munipuṅgavāḥ ॥
kurvanti vaikriyai rūpairjambūdvīpasya pūraṇam ।
idaṁ tvatparddhikasyāsya vyantarasya vijr̥mbhitam ॥
kumārō'vōcadētēna bhagavan ! kiṁ purā kr̥tam ।
sañjātō'yaṁ yadaparḍistataḥ sādhuracīkathat ॥
mr̥ṣāvādvrataṁ pūrvajanmanyādīyatāmunā ।
tacca bhagnamabhāgyēna paranyāsāpahārataḥ ॥
tēnātparddhirasau jāta iti śrutvā nr̥pātmajaḥ ।
yāvajjīvaṁ mr̥ṣāvādaviratiṁ pratyapadyata ॥
atha kṣapākṣayaṁ prāpa tatō natvā tapōdhanam ।
parituṣṭamanā gēhaṁ jagāma makaradhvajaḥ ॥
taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā bhrātaraḥ prōcuḥ sōpahāsaṁ śubhaṁ vyadhāḥ ।
svapuṇyamānamālōcya yadvadhāvr̥ttō'si bāndhava ! ॥

yatrōtpēdē padaṁ vācāṁ satyānāṁ makaradhvajaḥ ।

ityuktvānyadapi dravyaṁ datvā'smai vyantarō yayau ॥

dr̥ṣṭvā hr̥ṣṭō nr̥paḥ prōcē sacivānnikhilānidam ॥
ayamēva mahāsattvaḥ satyavāk sukr̥tāspadam ।

astēyavatē datta-saṁkhāyaṇa kathā |
saṁkhāyaṇō payaṭṭō anna- diṇē niyaya-dēsamāgaṁtuṁ ।
dattō uṇa akayatthō tti ṭhāumahilasai tatthēva ॥
sāhāraṇāim̐ duhavi imāim̐ rayaṇāim̐ amha iya bhaṇiuṁ ।

satthēṇa sahāgacchaṁti dōvi tē rayaṇa-saṁbalatthaiyaṁ ।
maggē vahati kamasō jā pattā niya-purāsannaṁ ॥
tā tattha bhilla dhāḍī paḍiyā dattēṇa niya-karatthāī ।
khittāim̐ aṇuvalakkhaṁ rayaṇāī rukkha - gahaṇammi ॥
aha tāḍiūṇa dattaṁ tassa sayāsāu saṁbalatthaiyā ।
bhilēhiṁ jama bhaḍēhiṁ va gahiyā saṁkhāyaṇa- samakkhaṁ ॥
nīyā palli bhillēhiṁ kavi diyahāī tattha dhariūṇa ।
mukkā ananna- disāhi dōvi pattā paḍḍāṇaṁ ॥
jai kahavi rayaṇa -
lābhō na hōi tā hōhamaliyavāi ti ।
saṁkhāyaṇassa kahiō dattēṇa na rayaṇa-vr̥ttaṁtō ॥
anna- diṇē tattha gaō dattō pattāiṁ tēṇa rayaṇāī ।
na samappiyāī saṁkhāyaṇassa ēsō parōkkhō ti ॥
aha kittiyammi kālē gayammi piyarō imāṇa kāla - gayā ।
jāyā pamāṇa-bhūyā ēē cciya dōvi savvattha ॥
saṁkhāyaṇō ghaṇō dēvva-vasēṇaṁ na tārisō dattō ।
sō ciṁtaha rayaṇa- kaē khijjai saṁkhāyaṇō na imō ॥
kuṇai paralōga-kiriyāō ēsa tattō ahaṁ pi ēyāō ।
ēyaṁ ciya uddisiuṁ karēmi ēēhiṁ rayaṇēhiṁ ॥
ēvaṁ kaē na hōhī mitta- dōhō vi tō kuṇai dattō ।
paralōga - kiñcamatthi ya sēnēhō dhamma- buddhī ya ॥
ēvaṁ niyājyaṁ pāliūṇa āu-kkhayē mayā dōvi ।
jatthuṣpannā taṁ vāgarēmi nara-nāha ! nisuṇēsu ॥
ciṭṭhati dunni nayarīō uttarā dāhiṇā ya mahurāō ।
mahurāu suyaṇa - vāṇīu jattha dakkha vva vilasati ॥
patta- ghaṇa-cchāyāō bhamarahiyāō lasaṁta-sumaṇāō ।
jattha vaṇēsu layāō bhavaṇēsu vasaṁti vilayāō ॥

pāviḍḍī pāvijjai phalēṇa pāvassa puvva vihiyassa ।

iha āsi vasaṁtapurē parōpparaṁ nēha - nivbharā mittā ।

vimhiya-maṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ aṇēṇa sō ēsa atthōti ॥

jaggai cauttha-
jāmē suvaṇṇadhārō suvaṇṇa- purisaṁ taṁ ।
dahūṇa vihiya-maṇō bhāi imaṁ ēsa atthōti ॥
purisēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ ēsa atthi atthō paraṁ aṇattha - juō ।

khaḍḍāē pakkhittō suvaṇṇa-purisō suvaṇṇayārēṇa ।
gōsammi patthiyā tē suvaṇṇayārēṇa tō bhaṇiyā ||
kiṁ dēnaṁtara - bhramaṇa atthi ētthavi imō kaṇaya - purisō ।
khaḍḍāi maē khitō taṁ giṇhaha vibhajiraṁ savvē ॥
tō savvaivi niyattā aṁguli-kaṇagēṇa bhattamāṇēuṁ ।
vaṇiō suvaṇṇayārō ya dōvi pattā nayara - majjhē ॥
citiyamimēhiṁ haṇimō khattiya māhaṇa-suē uvāēṇa ।
amhaṁ ciya dōnhaṁ jēṇa hōi ēsō kaṇaya- purisō ॥
bhuttūṇa sayaṁ majjhē samāgayā gahiya - kusuma- taṁbōlā ।
vattiya māhaṇa-juggaṁ visa missaṁ bhōṣaṇaṁ vēttuṁ ॥

astēyatratē datta-saṁkhāyaṇa kathā |
bāhiṁ ṭhiēhiṁ taṁ caiva ciṁtiyaṁ kiṁ ciraṁ ṭhiyā majjhē ।
tunbhēti bhaṇatēhiṁ dunnidhi khaggēṇa niggahiyā ॥
visa missaṁ bhattaṁ bhuṁjiūṇa diya-khattiyāvi vāvannā ।
ia ēsā pāviḍī pāvijjai pāva-pasarēṇaṁ ॥
savvā asāsaya ciya riddhī paramatthaō bhava- nimittaṁ ।
mōkkhō akiṁcaṇāṇaṁ jīvāṇa jiṇēhiṁ jaṁ bhaṇiō ॥
iya dhamma - dēsaṇāē paḍibuddhō ēsa gaṁṭhi-bhēēṇa ।
cāritta - mōhaṇijjaṁ imassa pattaṁ khaōvasamaṁ ॥
pavvaiō para - paḍibōhaṇatthamavimukka thālakhaṁḍō sō ।
ahigaya-samatta-suttō karēi tivvaṁ tavaccaraṇaṁ ॥
anna- samayammi ēsō uttaramahuraṁ gaō viharamāṇō ।
bhikkhā kaē bhamaṁtō pattō saṁkhāyaṇassa gihaṁ ॥
niya - riddhi-vittharaṁ taṁ daṭṭhaṇa imassa majjamāṇassa ।
puṇṇō kimūṇagō vatti kōugēṇa ḍiō tattha ॥
dinnā imassa bhikkhā tahavi na niharai ēsa tō bhōttuṁ ।
saṁkhāyaṇō pattō bahiṇīē vīyaṇa karāē ||
bhaṇiō aṇēṇa sāhū — kiṁ jāsi tumaṁ na laddha bhikkhō vi ।
kiṁ bāliyaṁ palōyasi ?, muṇiṇā saṁkhāyaṇō bhaṇiō ॥
visaē visaṁ va visamē viyāṇi jē pavanna pavvajjā |
tē jiya-mayaṇā muṇiṇō taṇaṁ va taruṇīō mannati ॥
kiṁtu ṭhiō riddhi-kuūhalēṇa ahamēttha iliyaṁ kālaṁ ।
saṁkhāyaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ riddhiṁ giṇhāhi dēmi ahaṁ ॥
jaṁpai muṇī na kajjaṁ dhayavaḍa-cavalāi majjha riddhīē ।
saṁkhāyaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jai ēvaṁ tā kahaṁ kuḍuṁ ॥
muṇiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ tuha āgayassa basahīi taṁ kahissāmi ।
saṁkhāyaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ ti taō gaō sāhū ||
samaē vasahiṁ gaṁtuṁ namiuṁ saṁkhāyaṇō rahasi sāhuṁ ।
kaha kōugaṁ ti pucchai muṇī bhaṇai tuha kuō riddhī ||
saṁkhāyaṇō payaṁpai kamāgayā mē imā, muṇī bhaṇai ।
saccaṁ sāhasu, saṁkhāyaṇēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ amuga- diyahē ॥

parigrahaparimāṇē harivikrama-kathā |
jaṁ imiṇā saha juddhaṁ pāraddhaṁ taṁ maē kayabhajuttaṁ ।
jō appa-para-visēsaṁ na muṇai sō hōi haṇijō ॥
hā daṁsiuṁ asakkō jaṇassa vayaṇaṁ ahaṁ ajasa - kalasaṁ ।
tā kiṁ karēmi saṁpai huṁ nāyaṁ jāmi vaṇa- vāsaṁ ॥
tō harivikkama puraō āgaṁtuṁ ginha majjha rajjamiṇaṁ ।
iya bhaṇiuṁ vana- vāsaṁ saṁpattō caṁḍasēṇa - nivō ॥
harivikkamō siriuraṁ gaṁtr̥̄ṇa karēi tattha rajja-ṭhiiṁ ।
aha purisā kusumapurāu āgayā jaṇaya- paṭṭaviyā ॥
vaccha ! ahaṁ tuha virahē duhaṁ ṭhiō saṁpayaṁ gilāṇōmhi ।
tā niya-rajjaṁ ginhasu imaṁ ti purisēhiṁ vinnantaṁ ॥
tō tattha rajja-sutthaṁ kāuṁ harivikamō jaṇaya- pāsaṁ ।
caliō cauraṁga camūcamaḍhiya - phaṇirāya - phaṇacakkō ॥
sō pattō kusumapuraṁ paṇaō jaṇayassa tēṇa ahisittō ।
rajjē guru-riḍīē aha para lōyaṁ gaō jaṇaō ॥
sō bhūri kaṇaya - kōsaṁ payāva paḍihaya-payaṁḍa - paḍivakkhaṁ ।
kari-turaya-raha- samaggaṁ tivagga-sāraṁ kuṇai rajjaṁ ॥
aha annayā nisāē pacchima jāmammi suha - viuddhassa ।
jāyā rannō ciṁtā puvva-bhavē kiṁ maē vihiyaṁ ॥
jaṁ rajjāṇa caunhaṁ imāṇa sāmittamuttamaṁ pattaṁ ।
iya ciṁtaṁ kuṇamāṇassa nivaiṇō uggaō sūrō ॥
ujjāṇa - vālaēṇaṁ vinnattaṁ tāva dēva ! ujjāṇē ।
sura-kaya-kamala- nisannō kēvala - nāṇī kahai dhammaṁ ॥
tō parituṭṭhō rāyā jayalacchī saṁgaō gaō tattha ।
namiḍaṁ guruṁ nisannō dhammakahaṁ sōumādattō ॥
samaē puṭṭhē rannā nisāi jaṁ ciṁtithaṁ carama- jāmē ।
kēvaliṇā bhaṇiyaṁ suṇa nariṁda ! jaṁ pucchiyaṁ tumaē ॥
puvva bhavē āsi tumaṁ sirinayara - purammi sāvagō nāgō ।
nāgasiri sē bhajjā duṇhavi nēhēṇa jaṁti dinā ॥
anna- diyahammi tēsiṁ puraō purisēṇa bhaṇiyamēkēṇa ।
jaṁ acchariyaṁ vittaṁ ihēva nayaraśmi taṁ suha ॥

parigrahaparimāṇē harivikrama - kathā |
tā piu-davvaṁ giṇhasu tumaṁ imaṁ tō paryapaē nāgō ।
jaivi maha jaṇaya- davvaṁ tahāvi gēṇhāmi nāhamiṇaṁ ॥
jaṁ imiṇā gahiēṇaṁ khaṁḍijjai maha pariggaha- pamāṇaṁ ।
tēṇa bhaṇiō vi puṇa puṇa jāva na gēṇhai dhaṇaṁ nāgō ॥
tā rayaṇa-bhūsaṇa-dharō tiyasō hōūṇa sō bhai ēvaṁ ।
tumamēva nāga ! dhannō pasaṁsiō jō suriṁdēṇa ॥
nāgō jaṁpai kaha tattha maha pasaṁsāi avasarō jāō ।
kahiyaṁ surēṇa ēvaṁ sakkssa sahā - nisannassa ॥
paya- paṇamatthamēkkō pattō tiyasō imassa sīsāō ।
paḍiyaṁ cūḍārayaṇaṁ taṁ gahiyaṁ anna- tiyasēṇa ॥
tō jhanti kaṇharāīē pavisaṇatthaṁ palāyamāṇō sō ।
vajrēṇa haō hariṇā sirammi annāyakāriti ॥
taṁ kaṁdataṁ dahuṁ maē harī aṁpiō jai surā vi ।
lōbha-ggahēṇa gahiyā giṇhaṁti parassa rayaṇāī ॥
tā muttūṇa muṇidē naralōē natthi kōvi nillōbhō ।
hariṇā bhaṇiyaṁ ciṭṭhai sirinayarē sāvagō nāgō ॥
nillōbha cakkavahī jō sapariggaha- pamāṇa-bhaṁga-bhayā ।
tuha saṁtiyaṁ ti bhaṇiyaṁ pi ḍhōiyaṁ giṇhai na davvaṁ ॥
taṁ sōuṁ rayaṇasihō surō ahaṁ tuha parikkhaṇa-nimittaṁ ।
itthāgaōmhi hariṇā pasaṁsiō bhadda ! tumamēvaṁ ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ surēṇa maha kahasu kiṁ pi kicaṁ karēmi jaṁ tujjha ।
nāgēṇa jaṁpiyaṁ bhadda ! natthi maha kiṁ pi karaṇijjaṁ ॥
tiyasō gaō saṭhāṇaṁ kālēṇa sabhāriyāi saha nāgō ।
sa- pariggaha- parimāṇaṁ ṇihōsaṁ pāliūṇa maō ॥
sōhammē saṁpattō tattō caviḍaṁ tumaṁ samuppannō ।
nāgasirī tujjha piyā jāyā naranāha ! jayalacchī ॥
tō jāya - jāisaraṇāī dōvi jaṁpaṁti sacamēyaṁ ti ।

savvaṁ pariggahaṁ vajjiūṇa gēṇhaṁti dōvi pavvajjaṁ ।
kāūṇa tavaṁ tivvaṁ gayāī saggaṁ ca mōkkhaṁ ca ॥
iti parigrahaparimāṇē harivikramakathā ।

jō gōmaīi cariyaṁ dahuṁ dikkhaṁ pavannōsi ॥
visaya - vivasō ahaṁ puṇa pavajjaṁ gihiuṁ na sakkēmi ।
kiṁci kaya-kusala - lāhaṁ kāhaṁ disi gamaṇa- parimāṇaṁ ॥

bhadda ! tumaṁ kiṁ disasi visanna-cittō vva mē kahasu ॥

aha jōiēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ - ihatthi pavvaya - talē vivaramēkaṁ ।
tatthatthi jakkhiṇī sā tuṭṭhā dhaṇamicchiyaṁ dēi ॥
tattha maē saha pavisasu, subaṁdhuṇā jaṁpiyaṁ maē vihiō ।
vivara - ppavēsa- niyamō jāvajjīvaṁ guru- samīvē ॥

siharammi kūviyāē sahassa- vēhō rasō atthi ॥
girimāruhiuṁ taṁ dōvi gihimō tēṇa sāhimō kaṇagaṁ ।
bhāi subaṁdhū – uḍḍuṁ jōyaṇa- paraō maha nivittī ॥
jōgī jaṁpa - pavahaṇamāruhiuṁ jalahi-para-taḍaṁ jāmō ।

digotē subaṁdhu - kathā |
puvvaṁ paccakkhāyaṁ, tō bhaṇiyaṁ jōgiṇā ēvaṁ ॥
ṭhāṇāu imāu jōyaṇēhiṁ bārasahiṁ atthi vitthinnaṁ ।
sūrapuraṁ nāma puraṁ tatthatthi mahābalō jakkhō ||
sō maggiō samappaṛa thēvēṇa kalaṁtarēṇa bhūri dhaṇaṁ ।
gaṁtūṇa tattha vavaharasu tēṇa jēṇēsarō hōsi ॥

taṁ puṇṇamittha tattō aō paraṁ jāmi na payaṁ pi ॥
kuviēṇa va bhaṇiyaṁ jōiēṇa jaṁ jaṁ uvāyamakkhēmi ।
taṁ taṁ tumaṁ nisēhasi ahō ahannōsi nibbhagga ! ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ subaṁdhuṇā tō pasiūṇa suṇēha nicchayaṁ majjha ।
niyamēṇa abhaggēṇaṁ dhaṇaṁ na jai hōi mā hōu ||
sukkha - nibaṁdhaṇu paṁca-diṇa dhaṇa-lavu ahilasamāṇu ।
jamma-paraṁpara- sukkhakaru niyama ku bhaṁjai jāṇu ॥
aha catta- jōgi rūvō ravi-maṁḍala - bhāsurō surō hōuṁ ।
sō jaṁpiḍaṁ pavattō tumaṁ mahāsatta ! dhannōsi ॥
jammi samayammi tumaē muṇi-paya-mūlē disi vvayaṁ gahiyaṁ ।
jakkhō gōmuha - nāmō ahaṁ pi tatthēva āsi tayā ॥
kiṁ acattha-dhaṇatthī niya-niyamaṁ pālihī navā ēsō ।
iya ciṁtiūṇa vihiyā maē parikkhā imā tujjha ॥
tō avicalēṇa sattēṇa tujjha tuṭṭhō ahaṁ imaṁ dēbhi ।
kaṇayassa lakkhamikkaṁ givha tumaṁ jaṁpai subaṁdhū ॥
kaha nēmi niyaya-gēhaṁ ikkōhaṁ kaṁcaṇaṁ imaṁ jakkha ! |
tō jakkhēṇukkhiviḍaṁ khaṇēṇa sō niya-gharaṁ nīō ॥
kaṇagaṁ samappi sē jāmiti payaṁpiyaṁ gaō jakkhō ।
vimhiya-maṇō subaṁdhū dahuṁ dhamma-ppabhāvamiṇaṁ ॥
pujjara jiṇaṁ tisaṁjhaṁ muṇīṇa dāṇaṁ niraṁtaraṁ dēha |

iya disi parimāṇa vayassa pēkkhiḍaṁ sō ihāvi māhaṣpaṁ ।

pajjata - kayāṇasaṇō cittabhaṁtara phuraṁta para mēṭṭhī !

dvitīyē'hni kumārēṇa sā pr̥ṣṭā sādaraṁ pragē ॥
svasaḥ ! kimadya rātrau tvaṁ na dr̥ṣṭā'tha jagāda sā ।
mamāsti śrīmatī nāma bhrātarbhūpasutā sakhī ||
tatpārśvē'haṁ sthitā rātrau sō'vōcannaya tatra mām ।
sā'vadadvīkṣatē naiṣā puruṣadvēṣiṇī naram ॥
tēnōktaṁ ramaṇīrūpaṁ kariṣyē sā'bhyadhāttataḥ ।
ēvamastviti tat kr̥tvā sō'gāt tatra tayā samam ॥
uvāca śrīmatī kēyaṁ sakhi ! śrēṣṭhisutā'vadat ।
matsakhīyaṁ kalāstasyāḥ kāpītyūcē nr̥pātmajā ॥
śrēṣṭhiputrī jagādaivaṁ vētyēṣā sakalāḥ kalāḥ ।
tadā ca śrīmatī haṁsīṁ viyuktāṁ phalakē' likhat ॥
tāṁ jayadratha ityūcē tvayā virahapīḍitā ।
likhitēyaṁ paraṁ nāsyāstādr̥g dr̥ṣṭyādi dr̥śyatē ॥
tarhi tvamālikhētyuktvā phalakaṁ varṇakaiḥ saha ।
jayadrathakumārāya rājaputrī samarpayat ॥
likhitvā tādr̥śīṁ sadyō rājahaṁsīṁ jayadrathaḥ ।
śrīmatyai darśayāmāsa tāṁ sā dr̥ṣṭvaivamabravīt ॥

annayā viutthiō tassa patthivō bhīmō । tassōvari caliō cauraṁga-
camūcamaḍhiyāsēsa- sēsa- cūchā- rayaṇa-cakkō purisacaṁdō । pattō bhīma-nayaraṁ ।
bhīmō vi kāūṇa jaṁtāi- dugga-sāmariṁga niggaō nayarāō । purisacaṁdēṇa vi-
samaṁtaō rōhiyaṁ nayaraṁ । bīya- pāyārō vva kaō kuṁjara - parikkhēvō ।
tassa kaḍagassa vāhiṁ salilaṁ tuhaṁ kimēttha acchēraṁ ।
bahuyattaṇēṇa jalahiṁ pi sōsiuṁ taṁ khamaṁ jamhā ॥
sinnaṁ visannamēyaṁ jala-virahē tattha ṭhāumacayaṁtaṁ ।
vaccii sayaṁ ciya satta - sinnamiya harisiō bhīmō ॥
pahāṇēhiṁ vinnattō rāyā — dēva ! jalābhāvaō ittha na tīraē ṭhāuṁ, tō
saṁpayaṁ avakkamiumuciyaṁ ti । purisacaṁdēṇa vr̥ttaṁ mā vaccaha visāyaṁ । ihi cēva
bhavissaha vuṭṭhī । taō takkhaṇā tūla-lavō vva lahuō pāunbhūō gayaṇaṁgaṇē
ghaṇō । suyaṇa - siṇēhō vva savvaō vitthariō sō । samarē suhaḍa vva
khagga- laṭṭhi payaṭṭō payāsiuṁ vijjalēhaṁ । matta gaō vva laggō gahiraṁ gajiuṁ ।
supurisō vva vittaṁ ādattō varisiuṁ samaṁtaō salilaṁ । sēnna- jaṇa-maṇōrahē
vva sara - nivahē paya-pūrēṇa pūriūṇa viraō । imaṁ ca vaiyaraṁ muṇiūṇa amōha-
vayaṇō purisacaṁdōtti bhīyō bhīmō । parihiya-kaṁbalō kaṁṭha-kaya- kuhāḍō uva-
ṇīya pahāṇa - pāhuḍō paḍivannō sēvaṁ । samāgaō niya-nayaraṁ purisacaṁdō । atthi
ya tassa sōhaggasundarī - ganbha-saṁbhavō sura- kumārō vva sayala-lōya- lōyaṇā-
ṇaṁdaṇō sēṇō ṇāma ṇaṁdaṇō । gāhiō kalā-kalāvaṁ visēsaō । sayala - sattha- pā-
ragō tti pattō pasiddhiṁ । kuṇai bahūṇaṁ savvattha- saṁsaōcchēyaṁ । kayāi bharaha-
rahassa-vakkhāṇa-visaē duṇhaṁ gaṁdhavviyāṇa jāō vivāō । tanniṇṇaē pamāṇa
bhūō kaō kumārō । samāgayā dōvi tassa pāsaṁ । miliō viyaḍū- lōō ।

sattiṁ ca sattu - vijaē imassa rajjaṁ maē dinnaṁ ॥
tā jō imassa āṇaṁ vilaṁghihī tassa niggahaṁ kāhaṁ ।
iya sayala-jaṇa - samakkhaṁ bhaṇiūṇa tirōhiā dēvī ॥
appaḍiya-ppayāvēṇa tēṇa paripāliyaṁ ciraṁ rajaṁ ।
puvvaṁ pi jē na siddhā tē vi nivā sāhiyā tēṇa ॥

savvattha vittharēṇaṁ jiṇa-raha- jattāu vihiyāō ||
sammāṇiūṇa savvō muṇīṇa bhakti karāviō lōō ।

thēva kaē kavaḍa - parō niviḍaṁ niviḍaṁ tamāvayā - lakkhaṁ ।
lakkhai na jaṇō laguḍaṁ payaṁ piyaṁtō biḍālō vva ॥
māyā- vasēṇa kavaḍa - ppaōga-kusalā akiccamāyariḍaṁ ।
pattā iva sayamēva lajjiḍaṁ nāiṇī nihaṇaṁ ॥
taṁ jahā-
iha jayapuraṁ puraṁ asthi jattha vitthinna- panna- punnāō ।
pavarāvaṇa- vīhīō bāhiṁ majjhē ya rēhati ॥
tatthāsi vijayadhammō rāyā sūrassa jassa na samatthō ।
dahuṁ pi maṁḍalaggaṁ bhaēṇa riu - kōsiya-samūhō ||
rannō tassa bahu-maō mayaṁka - nimmala-guṇāgarō siṭṭī ।
tatthāsi gaṁgadattō taggihiṇī gaṁgilā nāma ॥
nāgōti tāṇa puttō visiddha-rūvō sahāvaō saralō ।
sayala - kalā-kula-
nilaō kamēṇa sō jutrvaṇaṁ pattō ॥
īsara-vaṇiṇō dhūyā pariṇīyā tēṇa nāgiṇī nāma ।
sā nāgiṇī vva duṭṭhā kuḍila-sahāvā viyaḍa-bhōgā ॥
mahuraṁ jaṁpatīē tīē aṇukūlamāyaraṁtīē ।
sāsu-sasurāṇa maṇaṁ paramaṁ pariōsamāṇīyaṁ ॥
bhattā hiyā viṇīyā ēsā amhaṁ ti tē vicitaṁti ।
kō vā kavaḍa - paōgēṇa kīraē na dhuvamappavasō ॥
iṁtassa bhattaṇō sā abbhudvāṇaṁ sasaṁbhramaṁ kuṇai ।
sayamāsaṇaṁ samappaṛa pakkhālai appaṇā pāē ।
paya pakkhālaṇa-salilaṁ dēha sirē dēva-nhavaṇa-salilaṁ va ।
ciṭṭhai aṇanna-diṭṭhī puraō āṇaṁ paḍicchaṁtī ॥
bhuttammi tammi bhuṁjai suyai pasuttammi jaggaē puvvaṁ ।
iya kavaḍa - paraṁ taṁ ciya mannai nāgō sughariṇitti ।।
aha annayā vasaṁtō viyaṁbhiō jaṇiya-jaṇa-maṇāṇaṁdō ।
tammi gaō nayara - jaṇō savvō kīlatthamujjāṇē ॥
nāgō vi tattha gaṁtuṁ kaṁduga- kīlaṁ karēi mitta- juō ।
aha tattha kā'vi gaṇiyā hariyā khayarēṇa ēkkēṇa ॥
gaṇiyā-parivārēṇaṁ pukkariaṁ atthi kō vi sappurisō ।

svayarēṇa nijjamāṇi jō rakkhai sāmiṇi amha ॥
tō saṁjāya-daēṇaṁ nāgēṇa nahaṁgaṇammi gacchaṁtō ।
taha kaṇaya - kaṁdugēṇaṁ mamma-paēsē haō khayarō ॥
khayarassa jahā paḍiyā pahāra - pīḍā - vihattha - hatthassa ।
sā saravarassa majjhē amuṇiya-gayaṇāvaḍaṇa - dukkhā ॥
nāgēṇa pavisiuṁ saravarammi ghariyā jhaḍa ti buḍuṁtī ।
tīraṁ suhēṇa nēuṁ jaṇaṇīē appiyā gaṇiyā ||
parituṭṭhāē tīē bhaṇiō sō siṭṭi putta ! maha dhūyaṁ ।
rakkhaṁtēṇaṁ jīvāviyamhi tumaē saparivārā ॥
sō nīō niya-gēhaṁ kāuṁ sammāṇamuttamaṁ bhaṇiō ।
gharamēyamēsa vibhavō ahaṁ ca savvaṁ tuhāyattaṁ ॥
niya - vikkamēṇa kiṇiyā jā tumaē rakkhiūṇa vasaṇāō ।
mayaṇalayāē tīē kiṁ puṇa vattavvamēyāē ।
mayaṇalayāē vr̥ttaṁ suhaya ! jahā nivasiō si amha maṇē ।
bhavaṇē vi imammi tahā tumaē nicaṁ pi vasiyacvaṁ ॥
ēvaṁ siṇēha vayaṇēhiṁ tāhiṁ uvarōhiō tahā nāgō ।
jaha mayaṇalayāē saha ciṭṭhai bahuviha viṇōēhiṁ ||
jāṇiya- vr̥ttaṁtēṇaṁ nāgō jaṇaēṇa jaṁpiō ēvaṁ ।
vaccha ! vaṇiyāṇa amhaṁ na pōrisaṁ ērisaṁ sarisaṁ ॥
ghaḍiō khu vikkamō khattiyāṇa sō sōhaē na vaṇiyāṇa ।
karahassa jaṁ na ghaḍiyaṁ na rēhaē nēuraṁ taṁ sō ॥
kiṁ ca-
purisassa hiyāhiya-ciṁtagassa jujjai na sēviuṁ vēsā ।
muṇiṇō akhama vva tavaṁ jā vihavaṁ sudda niṭṭavai ॥
bhāi suō tāya ! tayā tumulaṁ sōūṇa maha maṇaṁ jāyaṁ ।
taha karuṇā-rasa- vivasaṁ jaha vaṇiō'haṁ ti vīsariyaṁ ॥
niuṇa mahaṇō vi sahasā narassa taṁ kiṁ ci āvaḍai kajaṁ ।
uciyāṇuciya-vivēgō na jamhi hiyaē pariṣphurai ॥
vēsā-saṁgō'ṇuciō tti jaṁ ca āisasi tāya ! taṁ juttaṁ ।
kiṁ tu na dhaṇatthiṇī sā kuṇai kannu tti mai nēhaṁ ॥

aha kittiē vi kālē gayammi athirantaṇēṇa jīyassa |
paralōyaṁ saṁpattō jaṇaō jaṇaṇī ya nāgassa ||
sāsū-susarē divaṁ gaēsu gaṇiyā-giha-ṭṭhiē nāgē ।
para - purisēhi saha dhaṇaṁ niraggalā nāgiṇī khāi ॥
cōrēhi hariyamēyaṁ ti kuṇai kavaḍattarāī nāgassa ।
sōūṇa sarala-sahāvō taha tti paḍivajaē savvaṁ ॥
aha bhaṇai nāgiṇī taṁ su ciya salahijjaē jaē purisō ।
niya bhuya-vidatta vittō kitti dhammaṁ ca jō kuṇai ॥
dēsaṁtara-gamaṇēṇaṁ viṇā na pukkhala-dhaṇāgamō hōi ।
tā juvvaṇammi jujjai tuha piya ! dēsaṁtaraṁ gaṁtuṁ ॥
taṁ hiya-vayaṇaṁ nāgō mannatō bhaṇai bhaṇasi muhu piē । ।
taṁ puṇa mayaṇalayāē akkhai sā jaṁpaē nāgaṁ ॥
piyayama ! annā sattā tuha bhajjā tē uvaisai ēvaṁ ।
nahi dē saṁtara-gamaṇaṁ piyassa mahilā mahai kahavi ॥
nāgō bhai ma ciya aṇurattā nāgiṇī saī pavarā ।
maha
para - purisē ramaṇa-maṇaṁ vi kuṇai na kayā vi sīya vva ॥
gaṇiyā jaṁpai piyayama ! na muṇasi itthīṇa kavaḍa - cariyāī ।
jāu kuṇaṁti akajjaṁ tahā paraṁ pattiyāvaṁti ॥
kiṁ ca-
siṭṭhi - suyāē kavarḍa ihi ciya jaṁ kayaṁ ihēva purē ।
taṁ suṇasu bhai nāgō kahasu piē ! taṁ kahai gaṇiyā ||
itthēva purē siṭṭhī maṇōrahō nāma atthi atthīṇaṁ ।
astha-payāṇa-samatthō lacchī nāmēṇa tassa piyā ॥
tāṇa cauṇhaṁ putāṇa uvari jāyā maṇōraha-saēhi ।
suṁdarima- viṇijiya-tiyasa- suṁdarī suṁdarī dhūyā ॥
tīē pariṇayaṇāō anaṁtaraṁ cēva uvaraō bhattā ।
bhaṇiyaṁ piuṇā vacchē ! virasō ciya ēsa saṁsārō ॥
pahavaṁti maccu pāsā akhaliya-pasarā surāsurāṇaṁ pi ।
tā ciṭṭha catta- khēyā giha-kammaṁ kiṁ pi akuṇaṁtī ॥
annadiṇammi gavakkhē ṭhiyāi tīē pahammi vacatō ।

lōbhavipākē sāgara-kathā |
bhajāi maraṁtīē tattō nāgēṇa saṁlasaṁ ॥
lēkkhai cōkkhai jō marai niya- duccariya-vasēṇa ।
suṁṭhi - saṁcala kiṁ karēi tasu dinnaṁ avarēṇa ॥
iya nāgiṇīē cariyaṁ pavaṁca bahulaṁ palōiuṁ nāgō ।

rajjai kara calaṇāhara dalēsu taruṇīṇa nicca rattēsu ।
khaṇa-ratta viraktaṁ puṇa mūḍhō muṇai maṇaṁ tāsiṁ ॥

tucchaṁ majjhaṁ kaḍhiṇaṁ thaṇa-tthalaṁ caṁcalaṁ ca nayaṇa - juyaṁ ।
para - mōhatthaṁ mahilā payaḍaṁti na ērisaṁ tumaṇaṁ ॥
tuṁga-thaṇa-tthala-visamē asaṁbhavaṁ ramaṇi - dēha - maru-dēsē |
sēvēi saṁvaraṁ jō pīḍijjai sō na tanhāē ॥
ēvaṁ saṁvēya-parō visaya- virattō vi visaya-mai-juttō ।
nāgō nāṇa-divāgara-guru-pāsē suṇai jiṇa-dhammaṁ ॥
tō kavaḍa-vatta-cittō cāritaṁ gēvhiḍaṁ tavaṁ kāuṁ ।
samaē mariūṇa gaō saggaṁ mōkkhaṁ ca sō lahihī ॥
iti māyāyāṁ nāginī - kathā ||
jō kōha- māṇa- māyā - parihāra- parō vi vajjai na lōhaṁ ।

sasi-kara-dhavalā va guṇā niya-āsaya-vāha - kāraē lōhē |
āvahaṁti jala- kaṇā lōhammi va jalaṇa- saṁsattē ॥
iha lōyammi kilēsē lahium̐ lōbhāu sāgarō garuē ।
para- lōē saṁpattō duggai - dukkhāī tikkhāī ||

muttūṇa ahiṭṭhiyaṁ niya sarīraṁ । bhaṇiyaṁ ca - ahō ! kayagdhattaṇaṁ baḍḍayassa ।
dēvīē vimhiyāi vinnaviō patthivō - kimēyaṁ ? ti ।
rannā niya-vr̥ttaṁtō savvō vi nivēiō tīē ॥
karuṇā- parēṇa rannā mukkō kīrō kayāvarāhō vi ।
jaṁ sappurisā na kuṇaṁti pōrisaṁ dēva nihaēsu ॥

ēyāī kabvāī
pahu ! paḍhaī bālāu huṁta vi,
tattha tumha naranāha ! jai maṇi vahai saṁdēha |
tāu padaṁti ya kōugiṇa tā tumhē nisuṇēhu ॥ 32 ॥
ēkkēṇa dōhiṁ tīhiṁ cauhiṁ paṁcahiṁ chahiṁ ya sattēhiṁ ।
vārēhiṁ dharaṁti kā parapaḍhiyaṁ maṁti-dhūyāō ॥ 33 ॥
javaṇiyaṁtari tāu ṭhaviyāṅa,
tō vararui āgaiu
thui naṁdu taṁ tāu nisuṇahi,
cakkammi tammiya kamiṇa
kavva savva savvāu pabhaṇahiṁ,
tō naranāhiṇa vararuiṇa kuviūṇa vāru nisiḍa ।
vararuh tāva vilakkhamaṇa ulaggai surasiṁdhu ॥ 34 ॥
khivivi saṁjhihiṁ salila diṇāra,
gōsaggi surasari thuṇai
haṇai aṁta-saṁcāru pāiṇa,
ucchalivi tē vi vararuihiṁ
caḍahiṁ hatthi tēṇa ghāiṇa,
lōu papai vararuha gaṁga pasanniya dēi |
muṇivi naṁdu vr̥ttaṁtu ihu sayaḍālassa kahēi ॥ 35 ॥
sō papaī gaṁga jai dēi,
dōṇāra pēcchaṁ yaha
maha imassa tō dēi nicchiu,
saṁjhāi tō sikkhavi
biṁ purisu tattha maṁtiṇa visajjiu,
sō ghacivi pacchatu ṭhiō jā acchai pēcchaṁtu ।

tā vālivi pucchiu samaṇu sauṇa parikkhaṇarēsi ॥ 90 ॥
saccu jaṁpasu abhau tuha samaṇa !,
dōṇārahaṁ lakkhu phuḍu
tujjhu asthi kahi kattha gōviu,
tēṇāvi kaṁbala - rayaṇu
daṁḍa-majjhi saṁṭhiu nivēiu,
tō mukkau gau dittu tiṇa kaṁbalu kōsahi hatthi ।

tēṣu pratyēkamaṣṭāṣṭavāpīḥ śakrō vinirmamē ॥
aṣṭāvaṣṭau sarōjāni vāpīṣu vidadhē hariḥ ।
patrāṇyaṣṭāṣṭapadmānāṁ racayāmāsa vāsavaḥ ॥
patrē patrē sahasrākṣaḥ kr̥talōkakutūhalaiḥ ।
divyairdvātriṁśatā patrairnibaddhaṁ nāṭakaṁ vyadhāt ॥
ēvamairāvaṇārūḍhastisraḥ kr̥tvā pradakṣiṇāḥ ।
bhagavantaṁ mahāvīraṁ namaścakrē purandaraḥ ॥
।
